# Connect your Agoda calendar with other websites

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/115006604248-Connect-your-Agoda-calendar-with-other-websites

Updated: 2025-05-14T07:53:17Z

Connecting your calendars across all the websites where you list your property can easily help you prevent overbookings. In the Agoda extranet, you can fully connect your calendars by exporting your Agoda calendar to other websites and importing their calendar. This way, when your property is booked on one site, the dates will automatically be blocked on the other.

###
**Fully connect the Agoda calendar with other websites** ** **

**Desktop and Agoda app **

- Sign in to your account. If you manage multiple properties, select it from Listings.
- Go to
**Calendar** >> **Calendar connections**.
- Click
**Connect calendars**.
- For the website you want to connect calendars with:
- Copy your Agoda calendar link and paste it into the calendar connection feature of the other website.
- Get the calendar link of the other website and paste it into the
*Other website link* field.
- Name the calendar and click
**Import**.

- Repeat the process for the other websites you want to connect with.

**Managing calendar connections**

You can view and manage your calendar connections at any time in the Agoda extranet by navigating to **Calendar** >> **Calendar connections**.

**Edit or remove a calendar connection** ** **

**Desktop and Agoda app **

- Sign in to your account. If you manage multiple properties, select it from Listings.
- Go to
**Calendar** >> **Calendar connections**.
- For the calendar connection you want to manage:
- Click to edit the connection.
- Click to stop exporting your Agoda calendar. To stop importing the other website’s calendar, visit their website to manage the connection.


**Refreshing calendar connections**

Calendar connections automatically refresh several times a day. You can see when the calendar was last refreshed on the Calendar connections page, and you can refresh all connections at once to ensure availability is up to date.

**Desktop and Agoda app**

- Sign in to your account. If you manage multiple properties, select it from Listings.
- Go to
**Calendar** >> **Calendar connections**.
- Click .


--- FILE: 115006606268-automate-payouts-for-your-bookings.md ---
# Automate payouts for your bookings

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/115006606268-Automate-payouts-for-your-bookings

Updated: 2025-04-21T06:56:55Z

Properties receiving booking payouts through bank transfer or PayPal can enable Auto-pay to automatically initiate payouts, removing the need for you to manually approve bookings.



Auto-pay bookings are processed within 24 hours after the guest checks out and will be paid out based on the conditions you set. Once paid out, earnings will be sent to your account within 3-5 business days.


**Enable and customize Auto-pay**

**Desktop and Agoda app**

- Sign in to your account. If you manage multiple properties, select it from
**Listings**.
- Go to
**Finance **>> **Bookings & earnings**.
- Under
**Earnings**, select **Approve payouts**.
- Click
**Auto-pay settings** and toggle on **Enable Auto-pay**.
- Choose when you want to receive your payouts under
**Payment cycle**.
- Under
**Minimum payout**, enter the minimum total earnings that must be available to make the payout.
- Review your settings, then click
**Save**.


--- FILE: 115006606308-set-up-your-bank-account-to-receive-payouts.md ---
# Set up your bank account to receive payouts

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/115006606308-Set-up-your-bank-account-to-receive-payouts

Updated: 2025-07-22T10:39:21Z

If your current payout method is selected as **Bank transfer**, you will need to set up your bank account after your property is live, and forward the account verification documents** **to us.

We need the following information to set up your bank account:

- Bank location: Country where your bank is located. Only a local bank within the country where the property is located is allowed.
- Account holder or beneficiary name: Either the name that appears on the bank account or the name of your chosen beneficiary.
- Account holder’s or beneficiary’s phone number: Phone number associated with the provided account holder or beneficiary name.
- Bank account name: Exact name that appears on the bank account.
- Bank account number: Series of numbers on your bank book.
- Bank name, branch name, and Swift Code: Bank name, location, and identification code used to identify the exact branch of your bank account.
- Account type: We only accept savings accounts.
- Currency type: Local currency according to your property’s location.
- Bank address: This is the address of the exact branch where you set up of your bank account.

**Special characters such as = ! “ $ % & : * < > ; , # { } [ ] \ _ ^ | ~ @) will not be accepted. If your bank account details contain “&”, please replace it with “and”. **


**Supporting documents**

Once you have filled in your bank details, upload supporting documents to verify your bank account details are valid and ready to receive payouts. When uploading your documents, please ensure that the bank account holder’s name matches the name on the government-issued identification and that all documents are up-to-date and valid. The documents required to add your bank account include:

- Proof of bank account ownership (bank book, online statement, bank statement and canceled check) that clearly shows bank account name and bank account number.
-
**(ONLY for personal accounts)** Government-issued IDs matching the account holder’s name with clearly displayed bank account information.

Examples of accepted supporting documents (*please do not share images of your credit or ATM card*):

**Country** |
**Government-issued ID** |

You can expect to hear back from us – either approving the bank account details or requesting additional documents – within 5 business days.


**Add or update bank accounts**

If your property is using bank transfer, you can add your bank details to receive payouts.

**Add a bank account**

- Sign in to your account. If you manage multiple properties, select one from
**Listings**.
- Go to
**Finance >> Payment accounts**.
- Click
**Add account**.
- Enter the required details into the form in English characters.
- Click
**Choose File** to upload the required documents.
- Review your details and click
**Submit**.

Once you’ve added your bank account, it will be listed under **Bank accounts** as **Pending** while it undergoes verification. We’ll reach out to you via email within 5 business days to inform you if your account is approved or if additional documents are required. If you want to add more accounts, repeat the steps above. If you do not receive any update from us regarding the verification of your bank account within 5 business days, please send a follow-up email to biz@agoda.com.


**Assign a bank account to your property**

The bank account you add will be automatically assigned to your property if there are no other accounts listed. You can check which account is assigned to your property under **Property payout details**. If your property has no account assigned or you want to change the account, you can do so at any time.

- Sign in to your account. If you manage multiple properties, select one from
**Listings**.
- Go to
**Finance >> Payment accounts**.
- Click the three dots next to the property you want to assign a new account to, then select
**Assign new account**.
- Select the account you want to use to receive payouts.
- Click
**Confirm**.


**Assign an approved bank account to other properties**

If you have listed multiple properties on Agoda that receive payouts by bank transfer, you can quickly assign an existing account to all of them at once. This can be done from **Payout accounts**.

The bank account you want to assign must be approved by Agoda before you can take this action. The account will only be assigned to the properties in your Listings that are set to receive payouts by bank transfer.

- Sign in to your account. If you manage multiple properties, select one from
**Listings**.
- Go to
**Finance >> My payment accounts**.
- Click the three dots next to the bank account you want to use, then select
**Assign to all properties**.
- Review your selected account, then click
**Confirm**.


--- FILE: 115006606348-when-will-i-receive-my-payment.md ---
# When will I receive my payment?

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/115006606348-When-will-I-receive-my-payment

Updated: 2024-08-28T14:13:57Z

Depending on the payment method that you choose, please see the details below:

Agoda typically releases your payout automatically about 1-3 days after the guest has checked out. The bank account status must be approved and payment condition must be set to autopay.

If this is your **first reservation**, we may hold your payouts for **30 days after your first guest’s departure**. If you receive another reservation before your first guest payout date, the same 30-day payout condition will be applied. This is to allow time to detect any possible fraudulent activities.

After the 1st guest payout date releases, all future bookings will be paid 24 hours after guest check-out.

You can verify the completed payment transactions (remittance) and details on the Bookings & Earnings section of your listing.

Agoda typically releases your payout to your Paypal account within 24hours after the guest has checkedout. The Paypal account status must be set to active.

If this is your **first reservation**, we may hold your payouts for If you receive another reservation before your first guest departs, the same 30-day payout condition will be applied. This is to allow time to detect any possible fraudulent activities.

After the 30-day payout condition has passed, all future bookings will be paid out 24 hours after the guest check-out.

You will receive the Agoda virtual credit card along with the booking details. This card gives you access to the exact amount, and you can charge the card on the check-out date and up to 3 months after the check-out date (Be sure to check the expiration date on the card).

--- FILE: 17333710858515-clarification-on-reference-sell-rate-loading-and-commission-changes-agoda-homes.md ---
# Clarification on Reference Sell-Rate Loading and Commission Changes: Agoda Homes

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/17333710858515-Clarification-on-Reference-Sell-Rate-Loading-and-Commission-Changes-Agoda-Homes

Updated: 2024-08-28T14:12:15Z

As a valued partner, we believe it's crucial to keep you informed about Agoda’s operational changes on rate loading and commission changes that can directly impact our collaboration and mutual success. Therefore, we would like to provide more information on Reference Sell Rate loading and changes to commission and explain how these changes impact you.

Reference Sell Rate loading means that you load the reference rate that your property will be offered to the bookers. Agoda will collect from bookers, deduct its commission and remit the difference to you.

Note that there is no change in the amount the booker will pay and the amount that Agoda will remit to you, but instead of Agoda calculating the rate on your behalf taking into account Agoda commission, now the rate will be directly provided by you.

This means that you will receive the Reference Sell Rate that you have loaded minus Agoda commission and Tax on it (if applicable). We will remit the difference to you.

In addition, effective September 2023, we will deduct the following commission percentages from the total amount paid by bookers.


After the Reference Sell-rate loading apply, you can see applicable commission in the system by means:

go to Host Manage --> Booking & Earning --> View Commission

**How is the total amount calculated?**

Reference Sell Rate - % Commission - Tax* = Base Rate that you will receive

*If applicable Agoda will apply VAT/GST/sales tax on the commission charged to your property.

Tax = Commission x % Tax on commission


For example:

Below are sample calculations of the Base Rate received by property in Indonesia

Sample A : without promotion and rate channel setup

Sample B : with promotion and rate channel setup

To understand how to calculate your own rates, please access our rate calculation tool attached. This file is a templated spreadsheet allowing you to input relevant data and obtain your calculated rates quickly.

# Introduction to Bank Account Cloning Feature on Host Manage

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/19595980389011-Introduction-to-Bank-Account-Cloning-Feature-on-Host-Manage

Updated: 2023-08-16T06:19:42Z

We are excited to announce the launch of the Bank Account Cloning Feature on Host Manage. If you need to collect revenue from Agoda by Telegraphic Transfer (direct deposit to bank), this feature streamlines your bank account setup process, and saves you valuable time.

Here’s how Bank Account Cloning feature works:

Step 1: Access your Host Manage account and choose the Payment Accounts tab from one of your properties.

Step 2: Locate and click the button “Select Payment Method.”

Step 3: Select which of the approved bank accounts you want to apply to **all** properties, and click “Confirm.”

Step 4: Once the cloning is done, you will see a successful notification on the screen.


Step 1: Access your Host Manage account and choose the Payment Accounts tab from one of your properties.

Step 2: Locate and click the button marked “View Account.”

Step 3: You will be directed to the bank account setup page. Click the “Create” button to proceed.

Step 4: Fill in required information (varies by country) and upload your bank account supporting documentation on the bottom right.

For detailed instructions of bank account setup, please refer to: How do I Set Up my Bank Account? - Agoda Partner Hub

Step 5: Wait for the Agoda Finance team to review your bank accounts.

If the status shows “Pending” for more than 5 business days, please send a follow-up email to biz@agoda.com, mentioning "Follow up" in your email subject line. If the status changes to “Rejected,” the Finance team will reach out to you with the rejection reason by email. Once your bank account status is changed to “Approved” you can move on to the next step.

Step 6: Follow Step. 1~Step.4 in the section “**If you already have some properties with approved bank:”**


Note: Now we can replicate an approved bank account to all your properties! If you want to collect payment by multiple bank accounts, please set up an approved bank account for one of the respective properties and contact Agoda Service Team to support bank account cloning.


--- FILE: 29424036832275-the-sharing-economy-reporting-regime-serr-australia.md ---
# The Sharing Economy Reporting Regime (SERR) Australia

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/29424036832275-The-Sharing-Economy-Reporting-Regime-SERR-Australia

Updated: 2025-01-22T10:21:35Z

As a result of the new Sharing Economy Reporting Regime (SERR), Agoda Company Pte Ltd ("Agoda") has a legal obligation to report information about our partners with properties in Australia to the Australian Taxation Office (ATO). In this article you’ll find everything you need to know about SERR.


SERR is a third-party reporting system that requires operators of electronic distribution platforms (EDP) to collect, verify, and report seller transactions to the ATO.

As Agoda operates in Australia and is considered an EDP, we’re obligated to collect, verify, and report tax information about certain qualifying partners that conduct business through our platform, as well as business transactions made via our platform by those partners. The data collected for SERR will be reported to the Australian Taxation Office bi-annually before 31 January and 31 July every year.


Partners with properties located in Australia or any of its external territories* are within the scope of SERR, irrespective of whether their primary address is within or outside of Australia.

*External territories of Australia:

All partners with properties located in Australia or one of its external territories and listing on our platform will be requested to complete the Tax Compliance Information form to comply with the SERR reporting requirements. Please ensure that the information is always correct and updated.

How to access the Tax Compliance Information Form:


In the Tax Compliance Information Form, you will need to indicate your business type/structure with the following criteria in mind:

You will also provide personal/business details, address, and other individual/business tax details. You will need the following:

The SERR implementation guideline also requires other mandatory information such as the “Financial Account Reference.”

This Financial Account Reference, as defined in the guideline, refers to the account number to which the payment was made, or the most recent bank account used on the seller’s (partner) record. This will be either your bank account number, International Account Identifier, or Online Account Identifier.

When payments are made to more than one account within a reporting period, this reference indicates which bank account was most recently used.

Regardless of the method by which you receive payments from Agoda, you are required to provide the Financial Account Reference mentioned above.

For more information on mandatory information/fields you are required to provide, you may refer to the full text of the SERR Implementation Guide which the ATO regularly updates here: https://softwaredevelopers.ato.gov.au/sharingeconomytaxablepaymentsspecification


We will send regular reminders for partners to complete the form and provide the required details.


Once you’ve submitted your Tax Compliance Information form (the "Form"), we will validate certain data points per the guidance of the Australian Taxation Office (ATO). Please note that the data you provide in this Form will be used only for Australia's Sharing Economy Reporting Regime ("SERR") reporting purposes. Any similar information that you may have or will provide to Agoda through any channels will not be automatically updated by the information collected through this Form. Conversely, the information that you may have or will provide to Agoda through any channels will not be reflected in this Form.


Please note that data about you will be submitted to the ATO and in case the data is not complete or incorrect, this might result in an audit or further requests from the ATO to you.


For more info on how we process your personal data, please read our privacy notices at Agoda NHA Host Privacy Policy


--- FILE: 29818017720339-t-rkiye-touristic-rental-of-residence-permit-certificate.md ---
# Türkiye Touristic Rental of Residence Permit Certificate

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/29818017720339-T%C3%BCrkiye-Touristic-Rental-of-Residence-Permit-Certificate

Updated: 2024-06-04T07:37:43Z

In this article, you will find information on how to update your Touristic Rental of Residence permit number in YCS.

On 1 January 2024, Law no. 7464 on short term rentals took effect in the Republic of Türkiye.

This law requires partners renting entire residential properties for less than 100 nights to obtain a Permit Certificate for Touristic Rental of Residence from the Ministry of Culture and Tourism (“Konutun Turizm Amaçlı Kiralanmasına Ilişkin İzin Belgesi”).

We highly recommend you refer to the full text of Law n. 7464 here: https://www.resmigazete.gov.tr/eskiler/2023/11/20231102-16.htm

To comply with Law no. 7464, you are required to provide Agoda with your permit number or alternatively confirm that you are exempted from obtaining a permit in order to continue using our services.


You may provide this information on Host Manage by following these steps:

**Could you please share more details about this law, and where I can find the official document?**

On 1 January 2024, Law no. 7464 on short term rentals took effect in the Republic of Türkiye.

Partners renting entire residential properties for less than 100 nights must obtain a Permit Certificate for Touristic Rental of Residence from the Ministry of Culture and Tourism (“Konutun Turizm Amaçlı Kiralanmasına Ilişkin İzin Belgesi”).

We encourage you to refer to the full text of Law n. 7464 here: https://www.resmigazete.gov.tr/eskiler/2023/11/20231102-16.htm

If you are unsure whether Law n. 7464 applies to your property, please seek independent legal advice from local counsel.


**What happens if I don’t provide my permit number? **

Listing your property without permit number may lead to fines to you and/or Agoda from the Turkish Ministry of Culture and Tourism. Law no. 7464 requires online travel platforms to display hosts’ permit numbers on their platform after 2 June 2024. If you do not provide your permit number to Agoda or alternatively confirm that you are exempted from obtaining a permit, we will remove your listing from our platform until we receive your permit number or confirmation of exemption.


**What should I do if my property if exempt from Law no. 7464? **

If your property is exempted, please confirm your exemption on Host Manage.

**What happens if I share my information after the deadline? **

After the deadline, your listing will be removed from our platform. We will display your listing again after we receive your permit number or confirmation of exemption.


**How can I enter my registry number? **

Have more questions? Submit a request

--- FILE: 31614803968659-agoda-dac7-faq-page.md ---
# Agoda DAC7 FAQ Page

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/31614803968659-Agoda-DAC7-FAQ-Page

Updated: 2025-01-22T10:25:12Z

DAC7 is an EU law aiming to improve tax cooperation between EU member states – including transparency on revenues earned by sellers through digital platforms. This law will simplify the collection of taxes by local tax authorities. As part of this, Agoda Company Pte Ltd (“Agoda”) has to report information about our partners—both business entities and individuals conducting business through our platform and business transactions executed via our platform—to the Dutch tax authorities (DTA). The DTA will then share this info with the tax authorities from other EU member states.


**Will anything change in how taxes are processed due to DAC7 data reporting obligations?**

DAC7 doesn’t require any changes in the way taxes are processed, neither for the commission charged by Agoda nor for local taxes you charge guests. At the same time, we expect local tax authorities will use data provided by platforms to evaluate the validity and completeness of your taxes. They may also pre-fill parts of your tax return based on the data received from Agoda.


All partners with EU-based property listing on our platform will be requested to complete the Tax Compliance Information form to comply with the DAC7 reporting requirements. Please ensure that the information is always correct and updated.

You may refer to the Glossary of Terms at the end of this page.


**How to access the Tax Compliance Information Form**

**For Hosts (non-Hotel Accommodations):**

**Key Information**

If you identify as being a legal business entity, we request the below information:

If you identify as being an individual conducting business, we request the below information:

Transactional data could include:

**Is this a one-time request or a continual reporting obligation?**

DAC7 is an annual reporting obligation effective for the reporting period 2023 calendar year. The DAC7 collected data will be reported to the Dutch Tax Authorities by January 31 following the reporting year. For example, we’ll report data by 31 January 2024 for the 2023 calendar year, 31 January 2025 for the 2024 reporting year, and so on.


**Where can I find my business registration number, Tax Identification Number (TIN), and Value-Add Tax (VAT) numbers?**

As a party conducting business via Agoda, you must report the following numbers.

**For an entity:**

**For an individual** conducting business through our platform and considered a business by Agoda from a tax perspective:

We recommend contacting your accountant or local tax advisor if you’re unsure where to find these specific numbers.


**As a partner who manages multiple properties, do I need to provide data for every property?**

In general, you have to provide data about the individual or company authorized to bind your property named/specified in Agoda’s extranet/platform in the Tax Compliance Information form.

If you are a host (non-hotel accommodation) with multiple properties listed on Agoda under the same Member ID, then you need to provide the information only once for any one of your properties. Agoda will then use the same information for reporting purposes for all the properties tagged under that Member ID. If you input information for multiple properties under the same member ID, Agoda will only use the latest information which was entered during the reporting period.


**What if I have properties both within and outside the EU?**

If you have any properties within the EU listed on Agoda, you’ll fall into the scope of DAC7, and we’ll notify you to update the Tax Compliance Information form, whether or not your property is open for bookings.

To provide you ample time, you have 90 days from the date of our notification to update the Tax Compliance Information form. After the initial notification, we’ll send you two additional reminders to complete the form.

Please note that we will send the notification for each property, and we ask for your kind cooperation to complete the Tax Compliance Information form for each property.


**I don’t own the property. I only manage it on Agoda. Do I need to provide my data?**

For DAC7 purposes, we collect data about the individual or company with whom we’ve signed contracts with. Thus, if you agreed to our General Terms and Conditions, we still need you to complete the Tax Compliance Information form with the details of the individual or company who signed the contracts for the property listing.


**Will you share my information? And if so, with whom?**

Yes. Agoda has to report information about partners (i.e. business entities and individuals conducting business through our platform, as well as business transactions executed via our platform) to the Dutch Tax Authorities (DTA). The DTA will in turn share this information with the tax authorities from other EU Member States.


**If I remove my property from Agoda, will my information still be shared?**

We must share all data about our partners who make transactions via Agoda with the Dutch Tax Authorities. If you made transactions within a reporting year and decided to close the property for bookings, your data will still be shared with the Dutch Tax Authorities for DAC7 purposes unless you fall under one of the following exemptions:

**What happens if I don’t share my data?**

Under DAC7 enforcement rules for non-compliant partners, where the Seller does not provide the required information after two reminders following the initial notification by the Platform, but no earlier than 60 days from notification date, the Platform is obliged to take certain actions which may include closing the account, preventing re-registration on the platform, or withholding payment until the required information is provided.

Thus, as noted above, we provide you 60 days from notification date to complete the Tax Compliance Information Form, with two additional reminders. If the form is not completed within this timeframe, your EU-based properties may either be temporarily suspended and/or payment to you may be withheld. You’ll still have to honor any existing reservations.

We encourage you to complete the Tax Compliance Information Form for your EU-based property as soon as possible to avoid temporary suspension from the platform and/or the withholding of payments. Please note that in cases where we have withheld payment due to an incomplete EU DAC7 Tax Compliance Information Form, we will resume payment upon completion of this form. Please allow up to 24 hours for the system to be updated.


**How would my data be processed?**

For more info on how we process your personal data, please read our privacy notices:


**Entity:** legal person or legal arrangement, such as a corporation, partnership, trust or foundation. An entity is a related entity of another entity, if either entity controls the other entity, or the two entities are under common control. For this purpose, control includes direct or indirect ownership of more than 50% of the vote and value in an entity. In indirect participation, the fulfilment of the requirement for the holding of more than 50% of the right of ownership in the capital of the other entity shall be determined by multiplying the rates of holding through the successive tiers. A person holding more than 50% of the voting rights shall be deemed to hold 100%.


**Individual:** physical person conducting business through our platform and considered as a business by Agoda from a tax perspective.

--- FILE: 34480620900371-how-do-i-update-my-property-s-tax-driver-settings.md ---
# How do I update my Property’s Tax Driver Settings?

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/34480620900371-How-do-I-update-my-Property-s-Tax-Driver-Settings

Updated: 2024-10-17T06:29:50Z

**Introduction**

The below information will provide you with information and instructions on how you can update your property’s “Tax Driver” settings to ensure that the correct taxes are set up for your property.


Table of Contents

**What are “Tax Drivers”?**

“Tax Drivers” are property attributes that could impact the tax set up that applies to your property. This could include information such as, but not limited to Number of Rooms or Establishment Type. What “Tax Drivers” impact your property may vary depending on the taxes and taxing jurisdictions that your property is subject to.


Tax and Property Impact

It is your responsibility to provide us with accurate tax information, including but not limited to the Tax Drivers, as well as ensuring that such information is accurate and up to date. Failure to provide us with accurate information may result in an incorrect tax rate being set up for your property and therefore incorrect taxes may apply to bookings.


How to update the Tax Driver Settings for your property

Please note that you will need to update this for each property that you manage in their respective YCS extranet pages.



**Tax Driver Question Descriptions**

*Please note that note all questions below will be applicable to your property/properties*

Tax Driver Question |
Description |
| How would you classify this property? | The accommodation type of the property |
| How would you classify this property based on the local property tax assessor? | Tax classification of the property |
| Does your property have a NV Gaming License? | Indicate here whether your property has a NV Gaming License |
| Does your property have a Liquor License? | Indicate here whether your property has a Liquor License |
| Is this property considered to be a "Historical Hotel" based on local definitions? | Definition of a "Historical Hotel" may vary depending on the location of your property |
| Is this the property owner's primary home address? | Indicates lodging is at a private residence and if the owner does or does not occupy the property |
| Is the entire property rented for each booking? | Specifies whether this lodging establishment is rented in whole |
| If this property is considered a private home, is the property owner currently living in this address? | Whether or not the owner of a residence is present during an accommodation stay. |
| Is this property considered to be a "Full Service" lodging facility? | Definition of a "Full Service" may vary depending on the location of your property |
| Does your property have a restaurant? | Indicate here whether there is a restaurant within the lodging facility. |
| Is this property considered to be an "All Inclusive" lodging facility? | Indicate here whether this property is an All Inclusive property |
| What is the Average Daily Rate for this property? (In USD) | The Average Daily Rate is calculated by dividing room revenue of a lodging establishment by the count of rooms sold. This calculation may vary based on the location of your property. |
| What is the Revenue per Available Room for this property? |
The Revenue per Available Room is calculated by dividing the room revenue of a lodging establishment for the prior fiscal year by the room count and by the number of days in the period being measured (1 year). This calculation may vary based on the location of your property. |
| What is the Annual Room Revenue of this property? (In USD) | Annual revenue attributable to room rentals. |
| How many accommodation units are available for rent in this property? | A count of the number of accommodations units available in a lodging establishment. |
| What is the maximum number of occupants that this property is authorized to support? | A count of the maximum number of sleeping people the accommodations unit is authorized to support. |
| How many rooms are intended for sleeping in this property? | A count of the number of rooms intended for sleeping in the accommodation’s unit. |
| How many rooms are in this property? | A count of the number of rooms in the accommodation’s unit. |
| When was this facility constructed? | Facility construction date. |
| Where applicable, would you like to pass on the maximum tax rate to the booker? | The maximum rate may vary depending on the tax and jurisdiction. Please consult your tax advisor if you need additional details. |
| What is the size of this property's available rented event space in square foot? | The size of the rented event space in square foot. Please enter "0" if your property does not have any event space available for rent. |


If you have any further questions or need assistance updating the tax drivers for your property/properties, please email us at support@pricelineagoda.com and we will be happy to support.


--- FILE: 360000118388-why-does-my-bank-account-status-show-as-pending.md ---
# Why does my bank account status show as “Pending”?

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360000118388-Why-does-my-bank-account-status-show-as-Pending

Updated: 2024-08-28T14:12:11Z

If your current payout method is selected as **Direct deposit to bank** and your bank account status is “pending,” it’s because the account has not been reviewed by our finance team yet.

Agoda finance will need to verify your bank account information before sending you a payout. This is to ensure we avoid sending money to the wrong account -- and we only need to verify it once. Once you have filled in your bank details, please provide supporting documents to help our Finance team to review your bank accounts by attaching documents in Host Manage.

**Documents required:**

A. For Personal bank account

B. For Corporate bank account

**Remark:**

If you would like to change bank account, please provide previous bank supporting document or contract/termination letter/ownership transfer between you and the previous owner or a document that shows linkage with the property.

You can expect to hear back from us – either approving the bank account details or requesting additional documents – within 2 business days.

If you have multiple properties, please make sure to set up bank account details for every property. If you do not receive any update from us regarding the verification of your bank account within 2-3 business days, please send a follow-up email to biz@agoda.com mentioning "Follow up - Bank Approval_[your property ID]_[your property name]” in the subject line. Please ensure that the title of your email is correct to avoid any delay.


--- FILE: 360001002608-japan-agoda-homes-license.md ---
# Japan Agoda Homes License

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360001002608-Japan-Agoda-Homes-License

Updated: 2022-12-15T10:20:28Z

The nation of Japan requires a license in order to rent out your home. Below are answers to frequently asked questions, but we also highly recommend that you visit the Japan Tourism Agency’s portal website to apply for your license.

**Q: How do I apply for a license number for my listing? **

**Q: What is the license number? **

The license number is a 10 digit number assigned by local authorities to each individual listing you register.

** **

**Q: What if I refuse to register my listing? **

**Q: If my listing gets unlisted, how do I relist it? **

After getting a license, you will be provided a license number. Please provide that license number and any other required information to Agoda in order to relist your property on the site.


Q: I am hosting under the Hotels License, or Special Economic Zoning Act. In this case, how should I register my property on Agoda?

Or

**Q: Do I need a separate license number for each of my properties? **

Yes, you will need to obtain a license number for each listing. Please apply for your license(s) and add your license number and other necessary information to your Agoda listings.


**Q: What happens if I intentionally enter false information?**

** **

**Q: ****What will happen to my reservations if my listing is unlisted due to being unlicensed?**

Unlicensed properties in Japan may be found in violation of the Hotel Business Act, and Agoda has a policy of unlisting unlicensed properties. While bookings are not automatically canceled for unlisted properties, we reserve the right to cancel reservations for any unlicensed property. This may result in being fined according to the penalty policies outlined in your contract with Agoda. Please apply for the license as soon as possible and add the licensing number and other relevant information to your listings.


**Q: If my listing is unlisted, will Agoda automatically cancel my reservations? Should hosts cancel on their own?**

**Q: Will I still be able to access payment page if my property is unlisted?**

Yes. As long as your account is not deleted, you can still access your payment page and receive any payable funds.


**Q: Would you like to update your rental license? Please click ****HERE****.**

# Why have I not gotten paid for a booking?

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360001263287-Why-have-I-not-gotten-paid-for-a-booking

You will need to complete the bank account setup for each of your properties; if you have multiple properties, you’ll need to fill in the bank settings for each one individually. If your bank account status is pending, you may not have submitted the required documents to biz@agoda.com yet, or our team has not yet reviewed your property listing. If you’ve emailed the documents and still haven’t been paid after 3 to 5 days, please re-send the email with “follow-up” added to the subject line.


Ordinarily, payment is issued 24 hours after guest checkout. However, if this is the first time your property has been booked, there will be a 30-day hold until payment is processed. The 30-day payout window allows us to protect your guests and drive bookings for you. If you receive any further bookings made before the conclusion of the first 30 days payment, the same 30-day payout policy will be applied too.

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360001645708-Adjust-the-nightly-price-for-your-property

Updated: 2025-05-14T08:03:12Z

You can adjust your property’s nightly price anytime after it’s listed, either through the Agoda extranet on your desktop or the Agoda app. You also have the flexibility to set extra guest fees to customize your pricing further.


**Desktop**

**Change the nightly price for all dates**

- Sign in to your account. If you manage multiple properties, select it from
**Listings**.
- Navigate to
**Rates and availability** >> **Pricing**.
- Under
**Nightly price**, enter your new rate.
- Click
**Save**.


**Adjust the nightly price for specific dates**

- Sign in to your account. If you manage multiple properties, select the property from
**Listings**.
- Go to
**Calendar**.
- Use the
**Selected dates** and **Specific days** to set the dates you want to edit.
- Set the
**Availability** to **Available** and enter the minimum price per night.
- Click
**Save**.


**Setting extra guest fees**

- Sign in to your account. If you manage multiple properties, select the property from
**Listings**.
- Click on
**Rates and availability** >> **Pricing**.
- Scroll to the bottom of the page and expand the
**Extra guest** section.
- Enter the rate per night for each extra guest.
- Under
**For each guest after**, enter the number of guests that can stay for the nightly price you set. The extra guest rate will apply to each guest beyond this number, up to the maximum number of people who can sleep in your place.
- Click
**Save**.


**Agoda app**

**Change the nightly price for all dates**

- Open the Agoda app, switch to host mode, and navigate to your listing.
- Tap
**More **>> **Rates and availability** >> **Pricing**.
- Under
**Nightly price**, enter your new rate.
- Tap
**Save**.

**Adjust the nightly price for specific dates**

- Open the Agoda app, switch to host mode, and navigate to your listing.
- Tap on
**Calendar**.
- Tap
**Edit** and use **Selected dates** and **Specific days** to set the dates you want to edit.
- Set the
**Availability** to **Available**.
- Enter the minimum price per night.
- Tap
**Save**.

**Setting extra guest fees**

- Open the Agoda app, switch to host mode, and navigate to your listing.
- Tap
**More **>> **Rates and availability** >> **Pricing**.
- Scroll to the bottom of the page and expand the
**Extra guest** section.
- Enter the rate per night for each extra guest.
- Under
**For each guest after**, enter the number of guests that can stay for the nightly price you set. The extra guest rate will apply to each guest beyond this number, up to the maximum number of people who can sleep in your place.
- Tap
**Save**.

# How to get positive reviews from your guests?

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360001647228-How-to-get-positive-reviews-from-your-guests

Updated: 2024-08-28T13:59:46Z

Good reviews can help you get more bookings. In addition to having a clean, welcoming and comfortable property, make sure you describe your home with detail and accuracy. Of course you’ll want to list all of your home’s good features, but we also recommend being as transparent as possible and not setting up false expectations. For example, you should mention if there are noisy bars or a construction site nearby. Some guests won’t mind, but all guests should get fair warning.

It’s very important to communicate with your guests. Doing so improves their experience and creates a sense of trust. We recommend staying in touch with guests before, during, and after their stay:

Remember, little details matter. You may want to leave a nice note, welcome basket, or a guide to local attractions and conveniences. If your guest is staying long-term, think of various ways to improve their stay.

# What should I do if I see “Rejected” bank account status?

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360002020027-What-should-I-do-if-I-see-Rejected-bank-account-status

Updated: 2024-08-28T13:45:46Z

Once your bank account request has been reviewed, our Finance team will reach out to you to provide more details that are specific to your case. These emails will be sent from Biz@agoda.com. Please check your Inbox and Junk Folder for any communications from Agoda.

Please note that you should not modify your existing bank account submission request. If you cancel the request and create a new submission, this will revert to “new” status and approval may take an additional 5 business days.

**What are some common reasons for rejection?**

Roman/Latin alphabet and numeric characters (0-9) can be accepted, while special characters are not allowed (i.e. = , ! “ $ % & : * < > ; , # { } [ ] \ _ ^ | ~ @). If your bank account details and/or address contain the “&” (ampersand) please replace “&” with “and”.

Note: The only exception is Local Beneficiary Name and Local Bank name for China and Local Beneficiary Name for Japan. Please see the table below for more information.

To activate your bank account on Host Manage you are required to submit supporting documentation in Host Manage main page → Payment accounts → Payout Method →Set up your bank account. Please check if you have attached all required documents for approval.

Bank name, bank account number, or IBAN should be clearly shown in supporting documents and match with Host Manage/YCS.

--- FILE: 360002020867-information-on-our-30-day-payment-window.md ---
# Information on our 30-day payment window

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360002020867-Information-on-our-30-day-payment-window

Updated: 2024-08-28T13:43:41Z

The first payment for your property (based on the first check-out date) is withheld for 30 days after guest departure in order to ensure safety and security for the guest. This 30-day payment window applies to all properties with preferred payout methods of direct deposit to bank and Paypal. This window is also applicable for any bookings and/or check-outs during that 30-day window. Once the 30-day window has passed without any dispute, all payouts will be **PROCESSED within** 24-hours of guest departure if your property is on Auto Pay, or within 1-3 days if you are manually requesting the payments. Payouts will then be sent to the bank within 3-5 business days

If you have listed multiple properties on Agoda, the 30-day payment window will apply to each of your properties. After you receive the first payout for any one property and wish to skip the 30-day payment window condition for other properties under your account, please contact us.

Once your request is approved, any payment for future bookings will be processed within 1-3 days of guest departure.

--- FILE: 360023682874-if-i-have-a-booking-request-does-this-block-my-availability-for-those-dates-unti.md ---
# If I have a booking request, does this block my availability for those dates until I accept or reject?

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360023682874-If-I-have-a-booking-request-does-this-block-my-availability-for-those-dates-until-I-accept-or-reject

Updated: 2022-12-15T10:16:52Z

Yes. You will have 24 hours to choose whether to accept or reject a booking. During that time, the availability of your property during those dates will be blocked. The block will expire after 24 hours, and the dates will become open again.


--- FILE: 360023687274-cancel-a-confirmed-booking-incl-guests-cancelling-bookings.md ---
# Cancel a confirmed booking (incl. guests cancelling bookings)

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360023687274-Cancel-a-confirmed-booking-incl-guests-cancelling-bookings

Updated: 2024-08-28T13:53:51Z

When guests cancel their bookings on Agoda, you will receive a cancellation email notification from us. Guests will be automatically refunded according to the cancellation policy you have set up for your property.

If a confirmed guest contacts you with similar requests, please let him know to reach out to us to facilitate the process. If you need to cancel or modify a confirmed reservation, please note that you can only do so by contacting us on the Agoda Hotline, indicated on the booking confirmation email. Please provide us with your Booking ID so that we can quickly address your concerns.

It is important to note that for each cancellation you initiate, you are required to compensate the amount equivalent to one night’s stay. This may also impact your Top Host status.

May 26, 2020: Cancellation email notification sample


--- FILE: 360023687394-what-do-i-do-if-i-have-two-or-more-guests-show-up-at-the-same-time.md ---
# What do I do if I have two or more guests show up at the same time?

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360023687394-What-do-I-do-if-I-have-two-or-more-guests-show-up-at-the-same-time

Updated: 2022-12-15T10:16:47Z

Please call us as well as the other booking site immediately so that we can find alternate accommodations as quickly and gracefully as possible. The customer service number is provided in the booking confirmation voucher email. Do not attempt to relocate guest(s) on your own. Keep in mind that this is a stressful situation for everyone and it’s crucial to be as kind and understanding as possible with the guests. It’s not the guests’ fault. The important thing is to resolve the situation.

To help prevent double bookings, we recommend logging into your Agoda account and any other booking services you use every day. It’s also a good idea to use our Calendar Sync feature and/or switch from Instant Book to Book on Request. If you use Channel Manager software to manage your bookings across different platforms, please check your settings. Channel Managers may at times incorrectly mark your properties as available after they have already been booked.


--- FILE: 360023687414-avoid-getting-overbooked.md ---
# Avoid getting overbooked

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360023687414-Avoid-getting-overbooked

Updated: 2021-07-06T15:55:09Z

Getting overbooked is always a possibility if you are listing your property across multiple platforms. But when you cancel one booking over another, it will most certainly create an unpleasant experience for your guests. Here are some tips on how to avoid getting overbooked:

Do not panic if your property gets overbooked! Contact the guests to reconfirm their arrival details. Then analyze the bookings to determine who to relocate or cancel. The last received booking is not always the best one to change. Consider the rates, agreements, possible penalties from partners, length of stay, or any other factors associated with each booking and then take the best call.

If you choose to relocate guests who made their booking on Agoda, immediately contact the Agoda Hotline indicated on the booking confirmation email. Please provide us with your Booking ID so that we can assist you promptly.

--- FILE: 360023846093-what-is-a-top-host-and-how-do-i-become-one.md ---
# What is a top host and how do I become one?

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360023846093-What-is-a-top-host-and-how-do-I-become-one

Updated: 2022-12-15T10:18:52Z

Top hosts meet several criteria that establish them as reliable hosts who routinely provide a high quality experience to their guests. To become a top host, you must already be a verified host, have 5 completed and departed bookings, an average review score of 7.5 or above, a response rate over 70%, and no more than two bad cancellations over a six month period. A bad cancellation occurs when a host cancels a guest’s reservation. Top hosts receive more bookings, so it’s worth making the effort to get this status.


--- FILE: 360023858973-what-happens-to-my-top-host-status-if-i-cancel-a-booking.md ---
# What happens to my Top Host status if I cancel a booking?

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360023858973-What-happens-to-my-Top-Host-status-if-I-cancel-a-booking

Updated: 2022-12-15T10:16:40Z

“Bad cancellations” may affect your Top Host status. A “bad cancellation” is any cancellation made without notifying the guest. In order to preserve your Top Host status, you cannot have more than 3 bad cancellations in a 6 month period. This policy is designed to make sure guests have the best experience possible.


If the mistake is on our end, the cancellation will not count against you and will not affect your Top Host status. Contact us if you have any questions about a cancellation and please be as specific as possible about the situation. We will always do our best to make a fair decision.


--- FILE: 360023859113-why-are-phone-numbers-and-email-addresses-blocked.md ---
# Why are phone numbers and email addresses blocked?

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360023859113-Why-are-phone-numbers-and-email-addresses-blocked

Updated: 2022-12-15T10:16:34Z

Agoda is able to protect the safety and security of guests and hosts by facilitating communication through the platform while keeping phone numbers and email addresses private. We cannot provide this security for communications that occur outside of the Agoda platform. With that said, we do plan to alter our policy in the future to allow guests and hosts to exchange email and phone number once bookings are confirmed.

--- FILE: 360023859733-respond-to-guest-reviews.md ---
# Respond to guest reviews

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360023859733-Respond-to-guest-reviews

Updated: 2024-08-28T13:56:38Z

Reviews speak volumes about your property. Our studies have shown that the number of reviews and the review score for each property have an impact on the bookings for the property. Each review is a message from the guest for you, and we encourage you to respond to them graciously. Your response to the guest reviews allows you to thank your guests for their kind words and address any grievances that the guest may have had. All of these communicate to future guests that you care.

Your responses take about 48 hours to get published on our platform.

To respond to a guest review, go to the **Listings** page, **Bookings & Earnings**, **Bookings** tab, and then click **See reviews**. You can respond in 31 different languages.


May 26, 2020: Published guest reviews and your responses will be displayed on the property page

--- FILE: 360024633153-manage-how-guests-book-your-property.md ---
# Manage how guests book your property

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360024633153-Manage-how-guests-book-your-property

Updated: 2025-07-22T10:46:05Z

You can customize how guests book your property under **Rates and availability >>** **Booking settings** in the Agoda extranet to fit your hosting style and ensure a smooth experience for both you and your guests. From this page, you can select your preferred booking process, set your cancellation policy, limit when guests can book, and determine the required lengths of stay. Once you make any changes, be sure to review them and then click **Save**.


Your property will be able to accept bookings from guests instantly once it is live on Agoda. You can change this in **Booking settings** to **Request to book** if you want to review bookings before they are confirmed. Learn more about Request to book here.

** **

The cancellation policy you set will apply to all the bookings you receive. You can change your policy at any time by simply selecting the one you want and then clicking **Save**. Learn more about cancellation policies here.

** **

Set the maximum number of days that guests can make a reservation in advance. This gives you more control over your calendar, helps you stay flexible for personal plans or property maintenance, and lets you adjust pricing or availability as needed.

** **

Set the minimum number of days between when a guest books and their check-in date. This requirement gives you enough time to prepare your property, coordinate cleaning or maintenance, and manage your schedule.


Control how long guests can stay at your property by setting minimum and maximum length of stay requirements. You can apply these rules to all bookings or set stay date conditions for specific dates to optimize your calendar and ensure your property is booked just the way you want.


--- FILE: 360025249513-tips-and-tricks-for-providing-a-great-guest-stay.md ---
# Tips and tricks for providing a great guest stay

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360025249513-Tips-and-tricks-for-providing-a-great-guest-stay

Updated: 2022-12-15T10:18:40Z

Having a clean, welcoming and comfortable home is a must, but you can give guests an extra special experience by going beyond the basics.

**First impressions are important**- think about what you can do to create a “wow” factor when guests first walk in the door. Welcome baskets, cookies, snacks or a bottle of wine can be nice surprises. Guests may have traveled a long way to get to your home, so think about any extra touches that might enhance their comfort.

If you have some information about your guests and their travel plans, you may be able to **customize gifts, treats and other amenities**. A family with children might appreciate a few toys or games, for example. If you know they are vegetarian, you could recommend good vegetarian restaurants in the area, and so on.


--- FILE: 360025249753-what-do-i-do-if-i-have-an-issue-with-a-guest.md ---
# What do I do if I have an issue with a guest?

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360025249753-What-do-I-do-if-I-have-an-issue-with-a-guest

Updated: 2022-12-15T10:18:46Z

Occasionally, problems with guests may arise. We strongly recommend you follow these guidelines to resolve the issue:



**Stay calm!** Listen to the guest carefully and make sure you’ve heard everything. Listen rather than reacting.


**Acknowledge the problem**. Let the guest know you hear what they are saying. You don’t have to agree with the guest, but you need to consider their perspective.


**Offer a solution**. This shows that you are willing to take ownership of the problem. Keep in mind not to make promises you can’t keep.


-
**Contact us**. If you’ve tried all of this but the issue hasn’t been resolved, please contact Agoda customer service team at [biz@agoda.com] with the details of the issue and the support required. We will try to facilitate resolving the issue with guests. If the issue is urgent, please contact Agoda Hotline in your country which you can find the number on your booking confirmation email

# How do I reset my password?

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360025527654-How-do-I-reset-my-password

Updated: 2024-08-28T13:59:48Z

If you forget your password or simply wish to change it, follow these steps:

2. Enter your email address

3. Click on the box provided next to **Verify that you are not a robot**

4. Click **submit **

5. Then you should receive an email from Agoda shortly. In the email, click the **reset password link **

6. Enter your new password and verify by typing it in again in the provided field

7. Click **change password **

8. Click **Back **to get back to the main login page. You can now sign in with your new password.

If you’re still unable to access your account, please go to **contact us **and fill out the request form.

--- FILE: 360026451973-what-legal-support-does-agoda-home-offer-to-the-host.md ---
# What legal support does Agoda Home offer to the host?

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360026451973-What-legal-support-does-Agoda-Home-offer-to-the-host

Updated: 2022-12-15T10:20:28Z

Agoda does not provide any legal advice. Hosts are responsible for learning and complying with short term rental rules in their area, although we recommend reading the following tips:

- Research relevant city laws regarding short term rentals
- Check with your city to see if you need a license to rent your property
- Some cities, counties and states require hosts to pay taxes on rental income, so you should contact your local government.
- If you have a timeshare, lease agreement, or your home is in a condo, contact your landlord to see if renting your home is allowed.


--- FILE: 360047739914-what-commission-would-the-host-pay-to-agoda.md ---
# What commission would the host pay to Agoda?

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360047739914-What-commission-would-the-host-pay-to-Agoda

Updated: 2024-08-28T12:05:30Z

It’s very important to keep your price up to date, where you, as the host, loaded your nightly sell rates into the calendar, and the system automatically deducts the applicable commission from those rates and this is what you get paid, unless subject to additional taxes in certain jurisdictions.

The commission you pay to Agoda is automatically deducted from the rates you input into the system. This means that the rate displayed to guests already includes the commission, ensuring transparency and simplifying the booking process.Commission rates may vary depending on property location, it’s essential to review and understand the specific commission rate applicable to your property.

In some jurisdictions, additional taxes or fees may apply to the commission you pay to Agoda. These taxes can vary significantly based on local regulations and can include value-added tax (VAT), goods and services tax (GST), or other similar levies.

# Update to Agoda Terms & Conditions

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360048688393-Update-to-Agoda-Terms-Conditions

Updated: 2022-12-15T09:59:59Z

Agoda Homes is updating the Terms and Conditions of our agreement with your property and making them easier for you to understand. The updated Terms and Conditions will come into effect on 31 May 2020.

Your continued use of Agoda Homes services after the update comes into effect will be deemed to be acceptance of them.

We encourage you to read the updated Terms and Conditions by logging into your Agoda Homes Host Management account on desktop or app at any time. We have also compiled a list of frequently asked questions for your reference.

If you have any further questions, contact us via the Support button on Host Management

** Improved readability**: These updated terms have been written in plain language to make them easier to understand. We have also reorganized the terms to group related concepts together and reduce duplication. The defined terms have also been grouped together and their definitions have been simplified.

**Added clarity**: We have clarified the terms and obligations relating to extranet account security, charging unique payment cards (UPC), tax and invoicing, and giving notice via the extranet.

**Wider coverage****:** These terms now include updated terms about payment processing, dispute resolution, bookings facilitated by third parties, Agoda Collect & Property Collect obligations and fees for optional programs.

Q: Where can I view, print or download these Terms and Conditions?

A: You can view, print or download the Terms and Conditions from your listings through Host Management ( "Legal" -> "Contract on the left panel" ).

Q: What if I don’t accept the updated Terms and Conditions?

A: If you don’t agree to the updated Terms and Conditions, you can choose to end your relationship with us by terminating your agreement with us via the Support button.

Q: I have a question not covered here, who can I contact?

A: If you have any questions, you can contact us via the Support button.

Q: I manage multiple listings. Do I need to accept this for each listing individually or can I do it once?

A: This contract is per host base, by accepting this update it will automatically applied to all your listed properties.

Q: Is there a deadline by when I have to decide to accept or not?

A: The effective date of the new Terms & Conditions is set as 31 May 2020.

--- FILE: 360050964234-what-are-the-different-types-of-agoda-homes-listings.md ---
# What are the different types of Agoda Homes listings?

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360050964234-What-are-the-different-types-of-Agoda-Homes-listings

Updated: 2020-09-30T04:08:23Z

An Agoda Home is the entire accommodation listed by the property owner or the property manager who has the right to manage the owner’s property. Hosts do not stay on the property with guests.

**Multi-unit** properties: These are properties that have multiple allotments or multiple room choices available for guests to book. A property owner or manager needs to register and manage these properties through our YCS system.

**Single-unit** properties: These are properties with only one allotment. Only one booking may be facilitated in a single-unit property at any given point in time. Hosts need to register and manage these properties through our Host Manage system.


--- FILE: 360050964394-what-are-the-differences-between-agoda-homes-and-hotels.md ---
# What are the differences between Agoda Homes and Hotels?

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360050964394-What-are-the-differences-between-Agoda-Homes-and-Hotels

Updated: 2024-08-28T12:43:43Z

Hotels are established, professionally managed accommodations that allow paid lodging on a short-term basis. Typically, hotels have many rooms with a wide range of pricing to meet various guest requirements. In many aspects, the multi-unit Homes properties (especially the serviced apartments) function similarly to hotels.

Agoda Homes are much more personal and unique in nature. These accommodations are managed by hosts who want their guests to have a quality stay at an affordable price while offering an enjoyable local experience for guests. Agoda Homes are especially great for large groups, allowing guests to maintain their privacy and refrain from sharing common facilities with other guests.

On the Agoda platform, a hotel uses yellow star ratings. An Agoda Homes property will display an **Agoda Homes** badge and uses pink star ratings.


September 1, 2020: Property cards on the web


September 1, 2020: Property cards on the app

Agoda offers a strong brand within Asia and an expanding global footprint through many strategic partnerships around the world. Your property listed on Agoda will reach millions of travelers on our website and mobile app within a short span of time. We also provide our hosts with support all day, every day, and will even assist your guests with our 24/7 customer support offered in multiple languages.

If you are creating a multi-unit property for the first time through your mobile, go to www.ycs.agoda.com and scroll down to **Sign Up for FREE Now**.


September 4, 2020

You need to have the **YCS companion app **installed on your phone in order to manage your multi-unit listings. Download the YCS app from the App Store or Google Play Store.


--- FILE: 360051724334-select-a-name-for-your-property-and-write-a-description.md ---
# Select a name for your property and write a description

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360051724334-Select-a-name-for-your-property-and-write-a-description

Updated: 2024-08-28T14:13:59Z

These details need to be added on the **Description** page.

**Property name: **Your property’s name/title is the most important. It should create the impression of a highly sought-after accommodation that meets the expectations of your potential guests.

Tips: Know your audience. Is your accommodation for business travelers, families, or romantic couples?

Examples: Spacious 4 BR Near Eiffel Tower – 7 min walk, Luxury Beach House Perfect for Romantic Weekend Getaway, Enjoy Sunsets at Fully Equipped 2BR Condo at the Beach, Rustic Private Cottage w/ King Bed + Oceanside View

**Property description: **Your property description is more than just writing about your bedrooms and bathrooms. It is about creating an exciting pitch to travelers to sell a once-in-a-lifetime experience.

Today, most travelers prefer to skim through online descriptions rather than reading a lengthy block of text. To make your description easy for guests to digest, break it up into chunks with clear topic sentences or sub-headers so customers can easily follow. Overall, the description of your home should be at least 120 words.

Here is a guideline for recommended topics:

Tips: Once you have written down the description based on the information of your home, try adding further details and personal touches using these following tips:

Examples: Below is a template to help you generate a simple property description. However, we encourage you to use it as a guide and add your personal twist to make your listing stand out from the crowd.

**Template 1 **Whether you are a tourist or traveling on business, {Home’s Name} is ideal if you are looking for a uniquely stylish yet convenient place to stay in {location}. Only {distance} from the city center and {distance} to the {transportation options}, this (accommodation type) provides guests easy access to all that the lively city has to offer. With its convenient location and simple transport choices, you can easily access the city's must-see destinations such as {things nearby} and see more during your trip.

**Template 2**Uncompromising in its amenities and offerings, this bright, stylish, two-bedroom, city center apartment is the perfect base for anyone who wants to feel like they’re in the heart of {location}. Located near {things nearby}, this contemporary living space is designed and decorated in local flavor, with everything to make you feel at home – high speed WiFi, Netflix, washer and dryer, a queen-sized bed, a fully equipped kitchen, and even handmade tableware, as well as {amenities}.

Guests will enjoy (x) private bedrooms and (x) bathrooms as well as a common living area with a view of {view}. For superior sleep, the home provides Incredibly comfortable beds with high thread-count sheets. Wake up to a view of the {city} skyline that will take your breath away day or night. All bathrooms are stocked with high-end shampoos, thick towels, and all necessary bath products so you don’t have to waste vacation time running to the store.

Enjoy a fresh breakfast each morning on the balcony with its small table and chair or take a neighborhood stroll to the local coffee shops and restaurants. Safely wander around the streets at night where bars are open until midnight or explore {city} by taking the train from {station name} which is only {distance} minutes’ walk from home.

Once you have added your property’s **Location** details, click **Next** and move on to the **Description** page.

January 10, 2023

To update your property description on the website after the property is live, go to the **Listings **page and click **Edit Listing**. Then go to the **Description** page.

If you are creating a new property, move on to the **Description** page once you have finished adding your property’s **Location**.
