--- FILE: 360051724374-how-to-add-property-directions-check-in-info-and-house-rules.md ---
# How to add property directions, check-in info, and house rules

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360051724374-How-to-add-property-directions-check-in-info-and-house-rules

Updated: 2025-04-21T05:55:09Z

Clear and accurate information is key to creating a seamless guest experience. The Arrival guide and house rules allow you to communicate essential details about your property, helping guests plan their stay with confidence. By setting up these sections, you ensure that guests have all the information they need—from how to find your property to understanding your expectations—before and during their stay.

###

### How to add Arrival guide details

**Desktop and Agoda app**

- Sign in to your account. If you manage multiple properties, select it from Listings.
- Go to Property >> Arrival guide.
- For each item (Check-in and check-out times, Check-in instructions, Directions, and Parking):
- Click Edit or Add details next to the item you wish to update.
- Make the necessary changes.
- Once done, review and click Save.

- Repeat the process for any other items you need to add or update.


###

### How to add your house rules

**Desktop and Agoda app**

- Sign in to your account. If you manage multiple properties, select it from Listings.
- Go to Property >> Description.
- Scroll to Additional details and enter the rules guests must follow under House rules.
- Once done, review and click Save.


###

### How Arrival guide and house rules are used

-
**Check-in and check-out times:** Displayed on your Agoda page under Some helpful facts. This helps guests see when they can check in and check out, giving them the clarity they need to finalize their booking decisions.
-
**Check-in instructions:** These details are sent to guests a few days before their check-in date. Providing clear, step-by-step instructions ensures a smooth arrival and reduces guest anxiety about the check-in process.
-
**Directions:** Once a booking is confirmed, your directions are automatically sent to guests. This is key to helping them find your property easily, improving their first impression and ensuring they feel comfortable getting there without any confusion.
-
**Parking:** Parking information is displayed directly on your Agoda page, giving guests confidence that they’ll have a place to park upon arrival, which can be a deciding factor for those with cars.
-
**House rules:** House rules will be displayed on your Agoda page under Policies, helping guests understand your property's expectations and guidelines before booking.

##

### Tips for your Arrival guide and house rules

Setting up your Arrival guide and house rules is essential for ensuring a smooth guest experience and clear communication. Here are some practical tips to help you input these details effectively and understand their impact:

**House rules**

House rules are your opportunity to set expectations for guests during their stay. They should be simple, clear, and easy to follow. Here’s how to create effective house rules:

-
-
**Be concise and straightforward.** Avoid overly complex or specific rules that may confuse guests. Aim for 8-10 items to keep the list manageable and appealing.
-
**Focus on essentials.** Include rules about pets, smoking, quiet hours, and any fees for rule violations.
-
**Inform guests early.** While additional rules can be shared during check-in or through a guest book, it’s best to communicate key rules before booking to avoid surprises.
-
**Recommended length:** Write at least 100 words to show you care about your property and guests.


Examples of common house rules:

*Only registered guests are allowed.*
*Smoking or pets are not allowed.*
*Events or parties are not allowed.*
*Quiet time is after 11:00 PM.*
*Please dispose of all garbage in the trash can.*
*Turn off lights or AC/Heater when not in use.*
*If you break or damage something, please let us know for replacement or repair.*

**Directions to your property**

Clear directions are key to ensuring guests can easily find your property. Include the following:

-
**Transportation options:** Provide details on how guests can reach your property from nearby airports, train stations, or bus terminals. Highlight the easiest and most convenient options.
-
**Step-by-step instructions:** Include journey times, estimated costs, and instructions for entering your property (e.g., main entrance, passcode, key box).
-
**Landmarks:** Mention nearby landmarks or signs to help guests navigate.
-
**Contact information:** Provide primary and secondary contact details for assistance.
-
**Check-in outside normal hours:** Include instructions for late or early check-ins, along with any additional charges.

Example template:

The fastest way to reach our apartment is by taxi, which takes 30 minutes from [Airport Name]. Taxi fare is approximately $70.


Alternatively, you may take Bus 100 from [Airport Name] to [Bus Stop Name], which departs every hour between 8:00 AM and 9:00 PM. Bus fare is $25, and the journey takes about 1 hour. From [Bus Stop Name], you can walk 10 minutes to our apartment, located opposite [Landmark Name].


If you have trouble finding the property, contact us at [Phone Number].

**Check-in instructions**

Providing clear check-in instructions reduces guest uncertainty and enhances their experience. Include:

- Entry details: Explain how guests can access your property (e.g., self-check-in, reception, or meeting staff).
- Key collection: Share door codes, lock-box codes, or contact details for key collection.
- Additional charges: Mention any fees for early or late check-ins to avoid surprises.

###

### Managing details across Arrival guide and Description pages

Details like check-in instructions and directions can be added to either the Arrival guide or the Description page. Changes made in one will automatically sync to the other, ensuring consistency. To streamline your setup, we recommend using the Arrival guide, as it is the most up-to-date tool for managing this information.


--- FILE: 360051729973-what-is-agoda-homes.md ---
# What is Agoda Homes?

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360051729973-What-is-Agoda-Homes

Updated: 2020-09-30T03:52:45Z

Agoda is Asia’s largest online travel agency that caters to more than 2 million travelers who visit our website and app every day. We are committed to providing quality stays in over 5 million properties and accommodation types ranging from hotels and resorts to apartments, homes, and villas.

While we have always had non-hotel accommodation available on our platform, the changing market demands more emphasis and focus on increasing supply and elevating quality. Agoda Homes – a core business line within Agoda – was born from this demand.

An Agoda Homes property is an entire apartment, bungalow, house, or villa listed by you: the property owner or property manager. Unlike other OTA platforms, all Agoda Homes are for the entire accommodation, which means the host does not stay on the property with their guests. The host simply facilitates check-in and check-out, provides local recommendations, and ensures a quality stay for guests.

On Agoda Homes, we support a wide range of accommodation types, including serviced apartments, homes, private villas, farm stays, chalets, boats, and many more.

Click here to list your property with Agoda Homes.


--- FILE: 360051730253-what-commission-would-you-pay.md ---
# What commission would you pay?

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360051730253-What-commission-would-you-pay

Updated: 2024-08-28T14:12:13Z

You set the nightly price on the Host Manage system. This is what you get paid, unless subject to additional taxes in certain jurisdictions.

From the loaded nightly rate, we calculate a **reference sell rate** to the guest – which is the rate on which our commission is based and invoiced. This rate is displayed on the booking voucher issued by Agoda.

The reference sell rate is not necessarily the price the guest will pay. Agoda may choose to apply discounts on the reference sell rate, at our own expense, in order to get you a guest. However, this does not affect the nightly rate you load and what you get paid.


September 1, 2020

To view commission that Agoda charges on your successful bookings based on reference sell rate, go to the **Listings **page, select **Bookings & Earnings**, and then **View Commission**.


September 1, 2020

Note: You may view your contractual commission on Agoda bookings only on the web version. This functionality is not available on the app.


--- FILE: 360052054214-prepare-for-cleaning.md ---
# Prepare for cleaning

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360052054214-Prepare-for-cleaning

Updated: 2020-08-20T04:42:57Z

It is important to ensure you and your cleaning staff are safe and protected by taking all necessary precautions before cleaning. It is also important to know which supplies to stock up on and how to properly use them for your safety and the most effective clean. There are a few simple steps you should take to prepare for your cleaning session.

**Wait before entering your accommodation**: According to WHO, airborne respiratory droplets can last up to three hours. It’s important to note that scientific research is still unclear about how long smaller aerosol particles, such as COVID-19, can last in the air. If possible, it is highly recommended to wait 24 hours before entering your property. If you are unable to wait 24 hours, a minimum waiting time of 3 hours is advised as most airborne droplets would have settled by then.

**Air out the accommodation after entering**: Once you enter the property, open all doors and windows to increase the air circulation of your space.

**Wear personal protective equipment**: Put on proper protective equipment before entering the property and wear it throughout the cleaning session. This can reduce your risk of exposure to germs and chemicals. All cleaning staff should use the following equipment:

**Wash hands regularly**: All cleaners should wash their hands regularly throughout the cleaning process. This includes when they have the gloves on as well as when the gloves are removed. Make sure to wash hands for at least 20 seconds with soap and water. When handwashing is not possible, use hand sanitizer with at least 60% alcohol. ** **

**Avoid touching your face while cleaning**: All cleaners should avoid touching their eyes, nose, and mouth while cleaning.

**Use approved products**: Be sure that only approved sanitizing products are used during your cleaning session. You can refer to relevant agencies for a list of approved cleaners and disinfectants. According to WHO, products with a 70% alcohol solution or products with a sodium hypochlorite concentration of 0.1% are suitable for disinfectant products. Some commonly approved products that you may already have include:

**Read and follow instruction labels on cleaning products: **Always follow the directions on cleaning product and disinfectant labels, including how to use the product, dilution concentration, and contact time. If contact time or concentration is lower than recommended, this will hinder the effectiveness of the cleaning solution or disinfectant. However, if the chemical concentration is higher than recommended, surfaces being cleaned may be damaged.

**Check products and continuously restock:** Keep a checklist of all products needed for cleaning as well as their expiry dates. Use this checklist to determine if any items need to be restocked or replaced. Cleaning products that are past their expiration date may be less effective or ineffective at killing germs.

**Store solutions properly:** Use opaque containers to store your cleaning solutions and keep them in a covered area that is not in direct sunlight. If using chlorine solutions, prepare it daily to ensure the correct concentration is maintained.

**Do not mix cleaning solutions:** Avoid combining different product solutions as this may cause dangerous chemical reactions.


--- FILE: 360052054534-clean-and-sanitize.md ---
# Clean and sanitize

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360052054534-Clean-and-sanitize

Updated: 2020-08-20T04:44:11Z

Cleaning is the removal of dirt, germs, and other impurities from surfaces or objects. Sanitizing is the process of killing germs on surfaces and objects using chemicals or disinfectants. The CDC recommends both cleaning and sanitizing using household cleaners and EPA-registered disinfectants in order to reduce any risk of spreading diseases, including COVID-19.

Here are some general cleaning instructions you should keep in mind for each room of the house.

**Order of cleaning**: Begin cleaning in the cleanest areas and progress to the dirtiest areas. In each room, start from higher to lower levels as debris may fall on the floor.

**Garbage removal:** Before cleaning in any room, remove all garbage or items left behind by the previous guests.

**Wash linens**: To prevent the spread of germs, avoid shaking dirty linens and place them directly in a laundry bag when transferring them to the washing machine. Wash all linens or textiles at the highest heat setting recommended for the fabric.

**Cleaning hard surfaces and floors:** Clean all surfaces, including shelves and hard floors. Start dusting or sweeping higher surfaces and work your way down. After dusting or sweeping, clean the surfaces with multi-surface cleaner and a microfiber cloth. For floors, you may use a mop and floor cleaning solution. Be sure to routinely clean frequently touched surfaces such as tables, doorknobs, light switches, countertops, handles, desks, phones, keyboards, toilets, faucets, and sinks.

**Cleaning soft surfaces**: Vacuum any soft surfaces that cannot be put in the laundry such as carpeting, rugs, or upholstery. Make sure to also vacuum soft furniture such as the sofa. Clean any stains with a brush, soap, and warm water or in accordance with the manufacturer’s instructions.

**Sanitize all surfaces:** Keep germs at bay by wiping all surfaces with disinfectant. To be effective, sanitization usually requires the disinfectant to wet the surface for at least one minute. Be sure to read the label on your products and follow all instructions.

Common areas, such as living and dining rooms, are places where guests and family members spend most of their time with each other. Before you clean, start tidying up by removing any clutter. Follow the steps below when cleaning the common areas:

**Empty all garbage cans:** Remove all items left behind by previous guests. Reline all empty cans with new garbage bags.

**Wash and clean all linens**: Using a high heat setting, wash your linens and other textiles such as throw pillow covers, curtains, and dining room linens. Pillows, duvets, throws, and cushions that cannot be put in the laundry should be sprayed with disinfectant. To minimize the spread of dust and germs through the air, do not shake dirty laundry.

**Collect and clean all objects on surfaces: **Wipe items such as lamps or decor with a microfiber cloth to remove any dirt or dust and use a multi-surface cleaner to remove any residue. Put the items aside while cleaning the rest of the room and replace when finished. For hard to reach places such as ceiling fans or high shelves, use an extendable duster. Start from the highest surfaces and work your way to the bottom.

**Spray or wipe high-touch areas with disinfectant**: Spray all high-touch areas such as doorknobs, blinds, keys or electronic keypads, light switches, remote controls, tabletops, and shelving with disinfectant and wipe with a microfiber cloth or wipe with disinfectant wipes and leave to dry.

**Vacuum soft surfaces**: Vacuum all soft items such as rugs and carpeted areas as well as other furniture with textile surfaces. Spot clean textiles using a water and detergent solution and a bristle brush. To clean furniture made of leather, you can use special cleaning fluid to avoid damaging the texture of the material.

**Clean the floor**: Sweep all non-carpeted areas, then mop the floor using a water and floor cleaning solution. Pay extra attention to corners and sides of the walls. When cleaning the floor using a vacuum or by sweeping, make sure to get areas under the sofa or large furniture. Spot clean any stains with a brush, a detergent solution, and warm water if needed.

**Clean windows and glass**: Working from the highest point to the lowest, clean all windows and glass with a glass cleaner spray and microfiber towel.

Bedrooms are resting areas for guests and one of the most important places to clean. Most items in the bedroom come in close contact with a person’s skin. These items must be in pristine condition – no signs of worn spots, tears, or stains. Follow the steps below when cleaning the bedroom:

**Empty all garbage cans:** Remove all items left behind by previous guests. Reline all empty cans with new garbage bags.

**Wash all linens**: Using a high heat setting, wash your linens and other textiles such as throw pillow covers, curtains, and dining room linens. Pillows, duvets, throws, and cushions that cannot be put in the laundry should be sprayed with disinfectant. To minimize the spread of dust and germs through the air, do not shake dirty laundry.

**Clean the mattress:** Clean your mattress using a disinfectant spray. Spray the solution in a sweeping motion to cover the entire surface, then let it completely dry before using the mattress or putting on the laundered sheets.

**Collect and clean all objects on surfaces: **Wipe items such as lamps or decor with a microfiber cloth to remove any dirt or dust and use a multi-surface cleaner to remove any residue. Put the items aside while cleaning the rest of the room and replace when finished. For hard to reach places such as ceiling fans or high shelves, use an extendable duster. Start from the highest surfaces and work your way to the bottom.

**Wipe high-touch areas with disinfectant**: Wipe all high-touch areas with a microfiber cloth soaked in disinfectant or a disinfectant wipe. High-touch areas include doorknobs, light switches, televisions and remotes, tables, and shelf surfaces.

**Vacuum soft surfaces**: Vacuum all soft items such as rugs and carpeted areas as well as other furniture with textile surfaces such as sofas. Spot clean textiles using a water and detergent solution and a bristle brush.

**Clean the floor**: Sweep all non-carpeted areas, then mop the floor using a water and floor cleaning solution. Pay extra attention to corners or sides of the walls. When cleaning the floor using a vacuum or by sweeping, make sure to get areas under the bed or other large furniture.

**Clean windows and glass**: Working from the highest point to the lowest, clean all windows and glass with a glass cleaner spray and microfiber towel.

A dirty bathroom will turn guests off immediately. Bathrooms are breeding grounds for germs, so ensure to sanitize doorknobs, handles, and other hardware before you begin the cleaning process. Follow the steps below when cleaning the bathroom:

**Wash all linens: **Remove all dirty linens, towels, and shower curtains and put them in a laundry bag to prevent the spread of germs. Wash them on a high heat setting.

**Remove items from the bathroom**: Collect all portable bathroom supplies such as toiletries, soaps, and the hair dryer. Throw away all disposable items offered to guests. For non-disposable items, wipe with a multi-surface cleaner and a microfiber cloth. Put the items aside while cleaning the rest of the room and replace when finished. Finally, empty all garbage cans.

**Clean the toilet: **Spray the surface of the toilet as well as the inside of the bowl with a multi-surface cleaner. Be sure you allow for the solution to set according to the time specified on the product label. Use a toilet brush to clean inside the toilet bowl. Once clean, hold the brush over the toilet bowl and pour bleach over the brush. Let the bleach set for a couple of minutes, then pour water over the brush into the toilet bowl and flush.

**Clean all bathroom surfaces and high-touch areas:** Spray all hard surfaces such as the bathtub, shower, sink, and tiled surfaces with a multi-surface cleaner and wipe with a microfiber cloth. Use a scrub brush if needed for residue that is difficult to get off. Work from top to bottom to avoid falling debris.

**Sanitize all bathroom surfaces and high-touch areas: **After thoroughly cleaning the bathroom surfaces, spray all areas with a multi-surface disinfectant. Wipe all high-touch areas with a microfiber cloth soaked in disinfectant or a disinfectant wipe. Put the cloths used to clean the bathroom in the laundry. Do not use them in other parts of the house.

**Clean the bathroom floors**: Sweep or vacuum the bathroom floors. Once all debris has been removed, mop the floor using a water and floor cleaning solution.

Kitchens tend to get messy after being used. You’ll find some guests will want to cook while staying in your short-term rental and others will only make coffee in the morning. Regardless of how the space is used, it’s important to give your kitchen a deep clean after each guest departs. Follow the steps below on cleaning your kitchen area:

**Empty all garbage cans: **Remove all items, food, and garbage the previous guests left in the kitchen.

**Wash all kitchen utensils:** All dishes, silverware, and glassware should be washed in the dishwasher, including items that appear clean. These items may have been touched or not thoroughly cleaned by previous guests. If you do not have a dishwasher or if there are items that need to be washed by hand, use soap and hot water. Remember to also wash the microwave plate and oven racks or trays.

**Clean kitchen shelves and wall storage**: Clean the shelves you use to hold your dishes with multi-surface cleaner and a microfiber cloth, then spray with a multi-surface disinfectant and allow to air dry. Only return dishes and utensils back to the shelves once it has air dried.

**Clean kitchen equipment**: Spray oven cleaner on kitchen appliances as well as the stovetop, oven interior, and microwave interior. Leave the spray to set following the time indicated on the label, and wipe with a microfiber cloth or rough sponge and water to remove any buildup. Use water to help loosen any tough buildup.

**Clean remaining kitchen surfaces and high-touch areas:** Clean the remaining surfaces of the kitchen with the multi-surface cleaner and microfiber cloth, and spray with multi-surface disinfectant and allow to air dry. This includes counter-tops, drawer handles, the refrigerator exterior and interior, the microwave exterior, and the pantry. Any remaining kitchen appliances such as toasters should be cleaned in the same way. Remember to unplug the kitchen appliances before spaying any cleaning or disinfectant solutions on them.


--- FILE: 360052054554-wrap-up-the-cleaning-session.md ---
# Wrap up the cleaning session

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360052054554-Wrap-up-the-cleaning-session

Updated: 2020-08-20T03:06:30Z

Once your property has been properly cleaned and sanitized, you’ll be ready to throw out and store your cleaning supplies. Follow these instructions to wrap up your cleaning session in a way that avoids cross contamination:

**Wash your hands**: All cleaners should wash their hands for at least 20 seconds with soap and warm water as soon as they remove their gloves. If this is not possible, use a hand sanitizing solution with 60% alcohol content. Remember to do this before going about your normal daily routine.

**Safely dispose of non-reusable cleaning supplies or personal protective equipment: **Throw away disposable products such as disinfectant wipes or sponges.

**Clean and sanitize any reusable cleaning supplies: **Avoid cross-contamination by emptying and sanitizing the vacuum and sanitizing tools such as brooms or mops between each property or cleaning session. Wash any cleaning cloths at the highest heat setting appropriate for the material.

**Clean and sanitize reusable personal protective equipment**: Wash any goggles or face shields with soap and warm water and spray with disinfectant spray. Reusable face masks should be washed at the highest heat setting appropriate for the material.

**Check and restock cleaning supplies as needed**: Check the stock and expiry dates of your cleaning supplies and replace anything as needed. Have a list of all supplies that are used so it is easy for you to keep inventory and refill when needed. This list should also include any supplies you leave for guests during their stay.

# Listing your property: Pick your payout method

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360052490753-Listing-your-property-Pick-your-payout-method

Updated: 2025-05-14T07:52:29Z

When listing your property on Agoda, you’ll select your preferred payout method during the **Pricing **step. The two main options are bank transfer and PayPal. After your property is published, you’ll be asked to provide the necessary details to set up your account.

Payouts via Universal Payment Cards (UPC) are also available for merchant accounts. This method requires a credit card machine and allows you to charge the payout amount up to 150 days after the guest checks out. You can contact us if you’d like to request this option.


**Changing your payout method**

If you wish to change your payout method after your property is listed, you can contact us for assistance. Keep in mind that all payout details will go through fraud checks before they’re approved.


**About your first payout**

The first payout you receive will be available 30 days after your first guest checks out. You can learn more about the 30-day payout window here.


--- FILE: 360052543334-create-your-host-profile.md ---
# Create your host profile

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360052543334-Create-your-host-profile

Updated: 2024-08-28T12:45:06Z

No matter how attractive your property is or how complete the amenities are, it all comes down to the credibility of your home. Giving your listing an identity helps to build trust and credibility, increasing the likelihood of getting bookings.

**Host photo:** Guests looking to stay at a property feel more comfortable communicating with a host they can see. Here are some tips for choosing the ideal host profile photo:

Did you know? A study on host-accommodation platforms found that when a host is perceived to be trustworthy, the better the listing will be and higher the probability of the listing being booked.

**Host name:** Provide your First and Last name, and then the Display name. First and Last name is used for Agoda’s internal purposes only and will not be visible to customers. Display name is visible on the property’s page. You can either put your nickname or your initials here. We recommend you put your first name or nickname and your last name initial as your Display name.

**Preferred language:** Flaunt your language skills to get more bookings. This may be a selling point for overseas guests who are looking for hosts that can speak their native language.

**Host location:** Tell your guests which country, state, and city you live in so that they are aware which time zone you are in. Don’t worry, your exact location will be used internally and will not be publicly displayed on your listing.

**Host description:** Now this is an opportunity to make a good impression with your potential guests by letting them know you more on a personal level. Greet them, tell them who you are, where you are from, or what are your interests. The key is to be relatable. Guests are more likely to book from a host that they can identify or connect with.

Here are some topics you can write about to describe yourself:

Did you know? A study on host-accommodation platforms found that travelers demonstrated higher trust and intention to book listings from hosts whose bio conveys them as being well-traveled.

Note: Host photo, display name, location, and description will be displayed on the property’s page. We currently support only English characters and your property’s local language for free-text fields.

September 4, 2020

# Listing your property: Setting the nightly price

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360052547414-Listing-your-property-Setting-the-nightly-price

Updated: 2025-05-14T07:53:34Z

The price you set is the amount you’ll be paid, except in certain jurisdictions where additional taxes may apply. To determine a competitive price, research similar properties in your area. Consider factors like maximum occupancy, number of rooms, features, and nearby attractions.

Setting a fair and appealing price will help attract guests. When listing your property, consider pricing slightly below the local average to draw more interest. Don’t worry about starting low—you can always adjust your price later.


When listing your property on Agoda, you set the nightly rate on the **Pricing **step. This will be the price for the **Max guests allowed** you set on the **Basics** step. If you want to set rates for extra guests, you can adjust the occupancy and set the extra guest rate once your property is listed.

**Set the price yourself**


**Manage your nightly price with a channel manager**


You can manage your nightly price whenever you need on the Agoda extranet using the Pricing page or Calendar.


--- FILE: 360052808053-provide-safety-for-guests-during-their-stay.md ---
# Provide safety for guests during their stay

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360052808053-Provide-safety-for-guests-during-their-stay

Updated: 2021-03-18T07:41:43Z

Accommodation providers are always having to adapt to changes in the travel industry, and so too are guests. Putting measures in place to enhance your cleaning and ensuring safe interactions with guests will go a long way towards giving them the comfort and peace of mind they need to book a stay at your property. Here are some things you can do to accommodate guests so that they feel safe and secure:

**Contactless check-in and check-out:** Offer contactless check-in and check-out such as a key lockbox or electronic lock to better ensure social distancing. If you have contactless check-in and check-out or plan to offer it at your accommodation, make sure to update your property information and check-in details so guests are informed of the safe environment you are creating.

**Social distancing**: Practice physical distancing if face-to-face interaction with guests is necessary. Instead of a handshake, opt for forms of greetings that do not involve physical contact. Maintain a distance of at least 1 meter when interacting with guests and absolutely avoid any interactions if you are showing any symptoms of sickness.

**Provide cleaning supplies for your guests**: Empower your guests by setting out cleaning supplies they can use. Guests feel more comfortable if they can clean on their own during their stay. Some key items to stock up on are disposable paper towels, multi-surface cleaner, and disinfectant wipes or sprays.

**Provide a reminder about your cleanliness efforts: **Reassure guests by placing a reminder in your welcome booklet or on a desk in the common area informing guests of the following: *This property has been properly cleaned and sanitized for your arrival.*

**Provide protective equipment and supplies for guests**: Providing protective equipment for guests show you care about their personal safety. Small gestures such as leaving antibacterial hand sanitizer, reusable face masks, disposable gloves, and extra hand soap could go a long way.

**Remove shoes when entering the house**: Asks guests to remove their shoes when stepping into indoor areas of the accommodation to avoid dirt and germs from entering the house from outside.

**Educate guests on safe practices**: Inform guests how they can contribute to preventing the spread of germs and what actions they should take if they identify symptoms based on WHO guidelines. Provide a list of local emergency numbers and other important contact information.

--- FILE: 360052808153-cleanliness-guidelines.md ---
# Cleanliness guidelines

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360052808153-Cleanliness-guidelines

Updated: 2020-08-20T04:47:59Z

The spread of COVID-19 has resulted in a rapidly evolving situation. It has become increasingly crucial for property owners to understand proper cleaning procedures as this will reassure guests that they are staying in a safe environment. The overall cleanliness of a property, how cleaning and sanitization is carried out between stays, and how this is explained to guests has become vital to securing bookings. Now is the time to update your existing cleaning protocols to ensure you are minimizing the spread of viruses and other germs. Once done, you’ll want to let potential guests know about the enhanced steps you are taking to ensure the cleanliness of your Homes.

Follow these six key steps to keep your property clean, inform travelers of your cleanliness efforts, and stay up to date with recommended guidelines or policies.

__Disclaimer__

These Agoda cleanliness guidelines (**Reference Guidelines**) are provided to you for your reference only. In developing the Reference Guidelines, Agoda took into consideration elements of certain public health guidelines, including recommendations from the World Health Organization (WHO) and the Centers for Disease Control (CDC). You should treat the Reference Guidelines as a bare minimum standard of care. You are strongly encouraged to adopt a higher standard of care to the maximum reasonable extent, and you acknowledge that additional - or more stringent - measures may very well be necessary to properly clean and disinfect accommodations or protect your guests and staff. The Reference Guidelines are not intended to be a substitute for any guidelines issued by local government authorities in your jurisdiction (**Local Guidelines**). We encourage you to keep up to date with all Local Guidelines and to adjust your practices accordingly to fully comply with all Local Guidelines. You acknowledge and agree that you are solely responsible for keeping your accommodations clean, disinfected, and safe and that Agoda is __not__ directly or indirectly liable to you, or any of your affiliates, for any harm, damages, costs, expenses, penalties, awards, or claims relating to your adherence or non-adherence to the Reference Guidelines. You acknowledge that the Reference Guidelines may be amended by Agoda from time to time.

**Property type:** Choose one of the property types that best describe your accommodation. We support 4 property types: entire apartment, entire bungalow, entire house, villa.

**Property size: **Enter the property size in square meters, rounded to the nearest whole number.

If your property is 24.8 square meters, enter 25 square meters.

Conversion: 1 square foot = 0.093 square meters.

**Maximum occupancy:** Select the maximum number of guests that can sleep comfortably given the total bed space and sofas.

**Number of bathrooms and bedrooms:** Select the number of available bathrooms and bedrooms at your property. This is critical information for our travelers when choosing a property.

**Bedding configuration: **Once you have keyed in the number of bedrooms, you will see options to specify bed configuration in each of the bedrooms (including common space). Enter the count and type of beds for each bedroom (including common space). There are multiple bed types you can select: single, semi-double, double, queen, king, super king, bunk bed, sofa bed, and futon. You may also add multiple bed types for each bedroom by clicking on **Add another bed type**. Click **Next **and move on to the **Location** page.

**Location**: Type in your street address, building, floor and unit number, country, state/province, city, and zip code here. If we are unable to locate your property on the map, help up by dragging and placing the pin on the correct location on our map.

Note: The exact address of your property will not be displayed on our website. Exact location will be provided only after the guest confirms a booking.

--- FILE: 360053434214-set-up-targeted-promotions-for-exclusive-guests.md ---
# Set up Targeted promotions for exclusive guests

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360053434214-Set-up-Targeted-promotions-for-exclusive-guests

Updated: 2025-06-12T08:36:57Z

Pricing is the most important factor for guests when they are looking for accommodation. In addition to setting a competitive nightly price for your property, we encourage you to utilize our wide range of Targeted promotions to make your property more attractive.

Targeted promotions are user-specific discounts that are not publicly available to all travelers, but only to those who meet the promotion criteria. We usually boost rankings of properties offering a Targeted promotion on our search page, making them more discover-able. These properties have also benefited from increased bookings and lower cancellations. Agoda supports a range of Targeted promotions from which you can choose:

-
**Private Sale:** Exclusive discount for travelers logged on to their Agoda accounts while making bookings. The discounts appear as **Insider Deals!** on our search and property pages. Based on historical data, the likelihood of getting bookings increases by 3x if your property is enrolled in this channel.
-
**VIP**** Gold**: Exclusive for Agoda VIP travelers who have chosen Agoda as their preferred accommodation provider. These travelers are also more likely to book properties from us.
-
**Mobile**: Exclusive price for travelers browsing and making bookings via our mobile application.
-
**Domestic **and GoLocal: New channel to tap into domestic demand as markets recover from the Covid-19 pandemic.
-
**China**: Exclusive for Chinese travelers.
-
**Package**: For travelers booking both a flight and hotel together.
-
**Retail: **This is the default channel for properties to be featured on Agoda. There is no discount associated with this channel.

All activated Targeted promotion will stack with any existing promotion. This helps us make sure that our customers are always getting the best deals.

If you would like to enroll your property on any of our channels, please contact us.

September 14, 2020: VIP channel on the web

September 14, 2020: Private sale/Insider deal channel on the web


September 14, 2020: VIP channel (left) and Private Sale channel (right) on the app


**Setting up a Targeted promotion**


**Desktop and mobile**

- Sign in to your account. If you manage multiple properties, select the property from Listings.
- Go to
**Rates and availability >> Promotions**.
- Click
**Choose new promotion**, scroll to the Targeted promotions, and browse the available options.
- Pick the promotion you want to use, review the settings, and fill in the required details.
- Once ready, click
**Activate**.

**Viewing and managing your promotions**

Promotions can be viewed and managed on the main **Promotions** page. Currently running promotions will be listed under the **Active **tab while those that are paused, deactivated, or expired can be found under **Inactive**. Here you can see an overview of your promotion performance and settings as well as take actions like editing or creating a duplicate. Please note these actions may vary depending on the promotion type or settings.

**Desktop**

- Sign in to your account. If you manage multiple properties, select it from Listings.
- Go to
**Rates and availability >> Promotions**.
- Scroll to your list of promotions and click the one you want to view or manage.
- Additional details will be shown as well as actions you can take.
- Select the action you want to take. If editing your promotion or duplicating it to create a new one, be sure to review your settings before saving or activating.

**Mobile**

- Sign in to your account. If you manage multiple properties, select it from Listings.
- Go to
**More >> Rates and availability >> Promotions**.
- Scroll to your list of promotions.

--- FILE: 360053496214-tips-on-tidying-up-and-what-to-avoid-while-photographing-your-property.md ---
# Tips on tidying up and what to avoid while photographing your property

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360053496214-Tips-on-tidying-up-and-what-to-avoid-while-photographing-your-property

Updated: 2024-08-28T13:43:45Z

**Tips on tidying up bedrooms:**

-
Before you start shooting, make sure the clutter from the main bedroom is cleared. Cleaner scenes are less distracting to travelers and will make your space more welcoming.
-
Leave out unsightly objects. Make sure windows, mirrors and floors are spotless.
-
Turn off the television and hide any wires or cables.
-
Leave in the room only what’s available when guests arrive – for example, do not add items like flower arrangements, assortment of magazines, or items that is won’t be offered to guests.
-
Set the ambiance to reflect the energy of your place but don’t overdo it or the space would look unnatural.


**Tips on tidying up bathrooms:**

-
It is important to have clean bathrooms. These details matter and should not be underestimated.
-
Toilet seats must be closed.
-
A full roll of toilet paper makes it seem like it was recently cleaned.
-
Make sure sinks, showers and baths are not wet. Open shower curtains, if it is not glass, so travelers can get the full picture.
-
Towels that are hanging or folded should be of equal lengths.
-
Trash bins must be empty.



**Things to avoid: **

- Road signs or parked cars.
-
Identifying information such as house numbers.
-
People or animals.
-
Any corporate logos, especially hotels.
-
Unsightly objects or views such as construction sites nearby.
-
Poorly lit places.
-
Identical images taken at a different angle.
-
Images of area landmarks or views that you cannot see from the property.

--- FILE: 360053556294-best-practices-on-staying-price-competitive-on-agoda.md ---
# Best practices on staying price competitive on Agoda

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360053556294-Best-practices-on-staying-price-competitive-on-Agoda

Updated: 2024-08-28T13:45:50Z

We encourage that you research the neighborhood where your property is located and get an idea of how similar properties are priced. --- FILE: 360053665154-accept-or-reject-a-booking-request-for-book-on-request-properties.md ---
# Accept or reject a booking request for Book-on-Request properties

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360053665154-Accept-or-reject-a-booking-request-for-Book-on-Request-properties

Updated: 2024-08-28T13:39:53Z

If your property’s reservation type** **is set up as **Require reservation requests**, every booking request will be sent to you via email for you to accept/decline within 24 hours, else the booking will be automatically cancelled. Please note that Book-on-Request reservations create a suboptimal experience for guests as they need to wait for a day to receive a booking confirmation. We encourage you to keep your property reservation type as **Instant book**. If you need to maintain an on-request reservation type, please monitor these reservation request notifications so that you can promptly respond to guests.

Once you accept** **a booking, you will receive an email notification from us stating that the booking is confirmed. If you decline the booking request, the booking will be cancelled. If you have missed the booking request email notification, please go to **Messages** on Host Manage to accept/decline the booking.

All booking statuses are recorded on Host Manage.

September 14, 2020: Booking request email notification sample

To check a reservation request, go to the **Reservations**** **page and click on the **Request **tab where you can either **Decline **or **Accept **a booking request. If you are unable to accept/decline the booking within 24 hours, the booking will be automatically declined.


September 14, 2020


--- FILE: 360053665254-tips-and-tricks-for-welcoming-guests.md ---
# Tips and tricks for welcoming guests

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360053665254-Tips-and-tricks-for-welcoming-guests

Updated: 2022-12-15T10:09:23Z

Guests who choose to stay in Homes properties instead of hotels do so because Homes are cozy, personal, and unique in nature. Treat your guests well. A happy guest will leave you a good review and help you get more bookings in the future. Good reviews are an important decision-making factor for travelers. Here are some tips and tricks that will make your guests’ stay pleasant:

-
Communicate with your guests to inspire trust. We recommend that you reach out to your guests proactively once the booking has been confirmed and continue to stay in touch throughout their stay.
-
Provide clear check-in instructions to your guests. Travelers do not like uncertainty. Leave them detailed instructions on how to get into your property once they arrive.
-
Cleanliness is important. Keep your property sparkling clean. Tidy up the furniture, prepare the bathroom, clean and sanitize the floor and other surfaces. Your guests will appreciate that extra effort you put in to clean your property.
-
Add that personal touch. Some welcome goodies like a welcome basket of snacks could cheer up your guests after a long day on the road. If you are aware of your guests’ plans or itinerary, you may be able to put together some local recommendations for them.

--- FILE: 360055227013-why-and-how-to-use-request-to-book.md ---
# Why and how to use Request to book

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360055227013-Why-and-how-to-use-Request-to-book

Updated: 2025-06-30T05:13:20Z

As a host, you have the flexibility to decide how guests book your property. While allowing guests to book instantly is highly recommended for maximizing bookings, some hosts may prefer additional time to review booking requests before confirming a stay. **Request to book** provides this flexibility, giving you the opportunity to ensure each booking aligns with your preferences and property needs.


**Why choose Request to book?**

**Request to book** allows you to manually review and respond to each booking request within 24 hours. This option can be helpful if:

- You need time to review booking details, such as the length of stay or group size.
- You want to ensure your property is a good fit for the guest’s needs.
- Your property has specific rules or requirements that may need clarification before confirming a booking.

This approach offers more time to manage bookings thoughtfully, but it’s worth noting that it may result in fewer bookings, as some guests prefer the convenience of instant confirmation.


**How to switch to Request to book**

**Desktop**

- Sign in to your account. If you manage multiple properties, select it from
**Listings**.
- Navigate to
**Rates and availability** **>>Booking settings**.
- Change how guests can book your property to
**Request to book**.
- Confirm the change, then click
**Save**.

**Agoda app**

- Open the Agoda app, switch to host mode, and navigate to your listing.
- Tap
**More **>> **Rates and availability** >> **Booking settings**.
- Change how guests can book your property to
**Request to book**.
- Confirm the change and then click
**Save**.


**Things to keep in mind**

-
**Request to book** gives you the time and flexibility to thoughtfully review each booking request. However, it may also reduce your property’s visibility and booking potential, as many guests prefer instant confirmation.
- If you choose
**Request to book**, clearly outline your property’s rules or requirements in your listing’s description to help guests understand what to expect before submitting a request.
- Install the Agoda app and turn on notifications to stay aware of reservation requests. Remember, these requests are automatically declined 24 hours after they are received.
- Always respond to reservation requests promptly. If you can’t accept a request, decline it quickly and consider including a polite message to the guest explaining why. This ensures a smooth experience and keeps the door open for future bookings.


--- FILE: 360055267074-what-is-account-verification.md ---
# What is account verification?

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360055267074-What-is-account-verification

Updated: 2024-08-28T14:01:11Z

All hosts and properties partnering with Agoda are required to complete host details and property ownership information, starting October 01, 2020, regardless of the property’s registration date on Agoda. This is to comply with various legal and regulatory requirements and avoid any service interruptions.

If your property is registered as a single-unit home property, you are required to complete:

**Host details information**: Please identify yourself as hosting properties on your own behalf or managing properties on behalf of property owners.

If you are an existing host on Agoda, you will need to provide the above host details information when adding a new listing to your account or when updating any host profile information as indication here. If you are a new host registering on Agoda for the first time, it is mandatory to provide this information before you add your first listing.

**Property ownership Information**: For any individual who owns 20% or more of the property, please provide details on the ultimate beneficial owners. The details required are first and last names, country of residence, nationality and date of birth. Please provide the property legal name (in case there is no legal name, please provide the property name as registered on Agoda), address and zip code. If any portion of the property is under government ownership or control, please provide the official’s details as well. **This requirement is mandatory for every property that is registered on Agoda.**

Depending on the country your property is in, the property ownership information will need to be completed within 30, 60 or 90 days of the property going live on Agoda.

If your property is registered as a multi-unit property, you are required to complete property ownership information only.

Using secure channels, your information is passed on to a third-party provider who assists in validating the details against various data sources. This interaction between Agoda.com and the third party is fully compliant with our privacy regulations.

If the required information is not provided within the stipulated time, Agoda will temporarily stop listing the account and all properties under the account until the forms are completed. However, if you still choose to not provide the mandatory details, Agoda will terminate the contract due to safety reasons.

When registering a new listing on Agoda, the host details information must be entered on the **Profile** section. Please choose **I host on my behalf** or **I represent a company** and enter all the information as accurately as possible.

September 30, 2020

If you already have an existing account on Agoda Homes, please go to the **Profile** section and choose **I host on my behalf** or **I represent a company** to enter all the information as accurately as possible.September 30, 2020

You may also click on the booster available on the **Overview** section of your account to go to host profile page.

September 30, 2020

To enter the property ownership information, click on the booster available on the **Overview** section of your account. It will redirect you to the account verification form.

October 01, 2020

October 01, 2020

--- FILE: 360055284033-photograph-your-property-pictures-speak-a-thousand-words.md ---
# Photograph your property – pictures speak a thousand words!

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360055284033-Photograph-your-property-pictures-speak-a-thousand-words

Updated: 2024-08-28T11:20:33Z

You will be amazed at how much impact photos have on travelers when it comes to choosing where to stay. The right photos to represent your home can quickly maximize your likelihood of getting bookings. Based on past trends, properties with at least 10 photos can make up to 9x more bookings than properties with fewer photos. We recommend a minimum of 10 photos to give travelers a clear idea of your offerings. These should include:

-
**Common areas:** At least one photo of the exterior, the entrance, and the surrounding environment as well as a photo for each key amenity.


**Rooms**: At least one photo of each bedroom, each bathroom, and each key room amenity.


-
**Main photo: **Pick a main photo that will leave a lasting impression. Remember, this is the big photo that travelers see on the search results page and will invite them directly to your home listing. Selecting the image that best displays your home’s unique selling point will help draw more attention from your potential guests. Here are suggested ideas for picking a main photo based on other successful listings:

-
Exterior shot of the outside of your home.
-
Interior or outdoor shot highlighting an important amenity such as a spacious living room or pool.
- Bedroom with the bed as the main focal point.



Please ensure the following criteria are met for your property photos:

-
Minimum resolution of 800 x 600 pixels (recommend 2048 x 1536 pixels)
- 4:3 aspect ratio.
-
Landscape orientation.
-
JPEG format.


--- FILE: 360055284053-tips-for-shooting-property-images-equipment-and-camera-tricks.md ---
# Tips for shooting property images – equipment and camera tricks

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360055284053-Tips-for-shooting-property-images-equipment-and-camera-tricks

Updated: 2024-08-28T12:05:34Z

You don’t have to spend big to take photos of your property. Using anything from a mobile phone to a professional grade camera, you can capture each room and amenity and appeal to guests. Here are some basics to get you started.


**Photography tricks:**

-
**Rule of thirds**: Turn on your camera’s grid feature or visually divide your image into thirds (imagine a 3x3 square grid over your screen). Use these lines as guides to place your most important objects along the intersections for optimal composition, allowing you to snap a more eye-catching photo.

-
**Leading lines**: Our eyes are naturally drawn to vertical, parallel, diagonal, and even strong horizontal lines. Photos with these kind of lines as the main subject will make viewers feel like they are in the place that is pictured.



-
**Wide shots**: Hold steady and take a wide shot view at eye-level to help travelers visualize the whole space. Make sure that the horizontal and vertical lines in the photos are straight. If you have one available, use a tripod to help you with this.


**Lighting**: Natural light is your best friend. Take photos during the day and open the curtains to let in natural light. Avoid taking photos on a gloomy or cloudy day as the photos will turn out dull. If there isn’t enough natural light in the room, brighten up the space by simply turning on the lights.


-
**No filters or special lenses**: Don’t take black-and-white or fish-eye photos. Show travelers what the room really looks like without distorting the images. This will make the images appear more credible and guests will be more willing to book.


**Mood and tone**: Adjusting the white balance can change the lighting tone of your image. You want to keep the tone clean, bright, and as natural as possible. The best photo temperature is pure white with consistent white balance. This can be adjusted under your camera’s settings.


-
**Editing**: Avoid using HDR, sharpening, shadows, highlights, and clarity filters as much as possible. These will give an inaccurate and unnatural interpretation of the space.


--- FILE: 360055284133-more-tips-on-how-to-best-photograph-your-home-timing-and-areas-to-shoot.md ---
# More tips on how to best photograph your Home – timing and areas to shoot

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360055284133-More-tips-on-how-to-best-photograph-your-Home-timing-and-areas-to-shoot

Updated: 2024-08-28T11:22:19Z

**For common areas**, the “golden hour” is the perfect time to shoot your exterior shots. Take advantage of the time just after sunrise or just before sunset. When the sun is at this low angle and not directly above, photos will have a magical quality of light, with shadows and contrasts that make their centerpiece pop.


The property’s entrance is not to be missed. Travelers need to know exactly what the property looks like when they arrive, so taking shot of the entrance as well as the building’s façade in the context of the street is crucial to a smooth check-in experience.


Capture the surrounding area. If your property has beautiful natural surroundings, show the surroundings in wide property shots so that travelers can sense the specialness of staying there. If you have a city location, choose a property shot angle that includes surrounding architecture or items with cultural interest, such as statues, bridges, old buildings, or markets. Be careful not to capture the house number, road/street signs or parked cars.


Show off your space and community areas. Take photos of each community area from various angles to showcase the entire space. Today’s travelers love to take photos and selfies on vacation, so think like an Instagram influencer. Offer travelers backdrops to their coolest vacation photos, and you will get more bookings.


Highlight all your amenities. Think about what travelers will enjoy when staying at your property. Well-equipped kitchens should be highlighted, including specific equipment, like gourmet coffee machines or a nice cooking range. Also, do not forget to show photos of the balcony, pool, gym, garden, or even the fireplace. Be sure to capture any unique features and amenities that can help a traveler choose your property over a similar one. Sometimes something as simple as an oven, or a rain shower head, can be the deciding factor!


Showcase accessibility features. Guests using wheelchairs, canes, walkers, or other mobility facilities should be able to visualize themselves navigating through the property. Wide walkways, or accessible feature such as a roll in shower should not be overlooked – these can help you appeal to travelers with special needs.

Highlight unique details that can bring your place to life! Whether it is a piece of artwork, a funny paining or a vintage vase from a local market, capture them in your photos to give some personality to your place. These unique visuals will set you apart from other properties. Remember, travelers who rent homes are skipping the hotels for a reason. They seek something special, local, and memorable.


Ambience. Maximize the hominess and warmth as much as possible and place emphasis on the overall ambiance of your space. Show travelers how special your property is by highlighting its unique vibe. For example, if a sense of local culture is reflected in the design of your property or the furniture, show it off in the photos.


**For bedroom shots**, let in as much natural light as possible for indoor shots. Keep blinds and curtains open to show view and enhance the entire space and keep lights on to help further brighten up the room. Capturing a little of the view out the window can help a traveler imagine your place in the context of its surroundings.


Aim at a corner of the room to add a touch of dimensionality to the photo. Shooting directly onto a wall makes a space look smaller than what it is in real life, while shooting into a corner can highlight the broadness and depth of the space.


For smaller spaces, take shots from different angles. You could even take them from outside the bathroom door or inside the shower. Experiment with what works best for your property.


--- FILE: 360055344453-information-on-licenses-for-agoda-homes-properties-in-japan.md ---
# Information on licenses for Agoda Homes properties in Japan

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360055344453-Information-on-licenses-for-Agoda-Homes-properties-in-Japan

Updated: 2024-08-28T14:12:14Z

All hosts in Japan require a license in order to rent out their properties. For properties in Japan to be live on Agoda, we need the property’s license number - a 10-digit number assigned by local authorities to each individual property you wish to rent out. To apply, visit Japan Tourism Agency’s portal website.

Any unlicensed property in Japan has been deactivated since June 15, 2018. A deactivated property does not mean a deleted account. As long as your account is still active on Agoda, you may access your profile to manage your payments and settings.

Any booking for un-licensed properties in Japan with a check-in date on or after June 15, 2018 must be canceled to comply with the country’s regulations. To stay up to date on any rules and regulations, we recommend you visit the Japan Tourism Agency’s website.

If your property has been impacted, you will not be able to receive any bookings. If you wish to reactivate your property, contact us and provide your license number.

Note: Do not intentionally enter false information. Doing so may lead to penalties from national and local regulations. License information provided by you will be displayed on your property page on Agoda and will be subject to inspection by the regulators. Agoda reserves the right to deactivate any property that is found to have missing or false license information.

You may also add the license number yourself on Host Manage. Go to the **Listings **page. Click **Edit listing** and select **Rental License** under **Legal**. Provide your license type, number, full legal name, email address, property address, and room number. Save your changes.


September 14, 2020

Note: You may add rental license information only on Host Manage web. This functionality is not available on the app.


--- FILE: 360055344513-list-of-promotional-discount-templates-supported-by-agoda.md ---
# List of promotional discount templates supported by Agoda

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360055344513-List-of-promotional-discount-templates-supported-by-Agoda

Updated: 2022-12-15T10:07:54Z

Pricing is the most important factor for guests when they are looking for accommodation. In addition to setting a competitive nightly price for your property, we encourage you to utilize our wide range of promotional discounts to make your property more attractive. Unlike channel discounts which are user-specific, promotional discounts are available to all potential guests.

To set up attractive promotions, you may select any of the available templates below or apply a custom promotion.

**Early Bird/Adv****ance**** Purchase**: This helps secure bookings early, typically 30-90 days before guest arrival.

**Last Minute****:** Run some last-minute promotions to appeal to late bookers or to attract a booking when a guest cancels at the last minute. With this promotion, guests get a discount if they book within a few days (typically 7) of arrival.

**72-****H****our**** Promotion**: This limited time offer is best utilized when you want to secure bookings within a short period of time. This promotion creates a sense of urgency for the guest towards a property that may be in high demand.

**Weekend Getaway****:** This promotion allows you to encourage full weekend bookings, perfect for guests looking for weekend getaways.

**First 3 Guests Promotion: **This promotion allows your first three guests to receive a steep 33% discount on your newly registered property. Such a discount increases the possibility of your property getting booked quickly. With the first few bookings, your property will start ranking higher on our search page. Also, a good guest experience during these stays will increase your chances of receiving great reviews, meaning a higher possibility of subsequent bookings.

**Long Stays**: We encourage you to provide steep discounts for long stays as a long booking can often be more lucrative than multiple short bookings.

**After****-****Hours Promotion****:** By default, this promotion may be used between 12:00 AM and 06:00 AM (property’s local time), but it may be adjusted if you require.

**Express Tonight**: This promotion allows for immediate bookings, and you may choose to have the guest stay the same night, next day or day after.

**China Only**: This promotion is available for guests who browse Agoda in Mandarin or search from Greater China origins.

**Free Night**: This is a catchy promotion for guests looking for freebies.

Unable to find something that fits your requirements? Use the **Customized Promotion** template to create your own. This basic template allows you to select range of booking dates, stay dates, and a discount that can be either a percentage, fixed amount, or free nights.


--- FILE: 360055450233-information-on-universal-payment-cards-upc.md ---
# Information on Universal Payment Cards (UPC)

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360055450233-Information-on-Universal-Payment-Cards-UPC

Updated: 2024-08-28T12:43:46Z

The Universal Payment Cards (UPC) payout method is available only for properties with a credit card machine that allows them to charge the virtual credit card number without a physical card. If you wish to set up UPC as your property’s preferred payout method, please contact us.

Note: For security reasons, the UPC number is not visible on the booking voucher. It can only be found on Host Manage. For non-refundable bookings, the charge can be made on the booking date. For all other bookings, the charge can be made only after guest check-out. Do not charge or pre-authorize these cards before the guest check-out as the card will be declined and will become void. Please charge only the amount that is reflected on the booking details; charging any other amount (such as parking fees or other fees) will make the transaction void. UPC payments may be processed up to 150 days after check-out.

You may find UPC details for each booking and process your payouts through the web. Go to the **Listings** page and click **Payment accounts**. Click **GET PAID**.

August 7, 2020

Each booking has its unique UPC details. When you are ready to process your payout, search for the booking by using the **Booking ID** or by providing other key details.

August 7, 2020

Expand the booking information by clicking on the booking and view UPC details. Process the payment using your credit card machine.


August 7, 2020

Note: You may view UPC details only on the web. This functionality is not available on the app.

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360055451053-Handle-no-show-incidents

To report a no-show, please email us at biz@agoda.com or contact us. Provide the Booking ID so that we can take care of your request promptly.

**Creating and using template replies**

You can create template replies to save time and quickly respond to common guest inquiries, such as check-in instructions, property details, or local recommendations.

- Click the
**quick replies** icon and select the message to insert it into the chat.
- Send your message.

**Security and privacy**

Effective communication is key to ensuring a smooth and safe experience for both hosts and guests. To maintain a secure environment, communicate with potential and confirmed guests only through our platform. This helps us protect your information and provide support if needed.

- Links cannot be shared to prevent phishing and malicious websites.
- Messages or attachments will be blocked if the content is identified as a potential risk.
- Never request or conduct payments outside of our platform. This ensures your transactions are secure and protected under our policies.

Remember, always remain vigilant when sending and receiving communications to protect yourself and your guests.


**Tips for communicating with your guests**

- Install the Agoda app and turn on notifications to stay updated on guest messages and requests.
- Send your guest a welcome note to create a positive first impression and set the tone for a great stay.
- Respond to special requests promptly. You can accept, reject, or choose
**Subject to availability** if you’re unable to guarantee the request immediately.
- Send a pre-arrival message 1–3 days before check-in, including tips for reaching your property and checking in while confirming any special requests to ensure a smooth experience for both you and your guest. We will automatically send guests your check-in instructions a few days before check-in.
- Monitor your messages during a guest’s stay to quickly address any questions or issues.
- After a guest checks out, send a message thanking them for staying at your property. Encourage them to leave a review on Agoda to share their experience and help future guests.


--- FILE: 42137366254355-agoda-inbox-attachment-feature-enhance-communication-with-guests.md ---
# Agoda Inbox Attachment Feature: Enhance Communication with Guests

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/42137366254355-Agoda-Inbox-Attachment-Feature-Enhance-Communication-with-Guests

Updated: 2025-06-13T06:48:15Z

**What is the attachment feature?**

*The attachment feature is now available in your Agoda Inbox, enabling you to engage more effectively with guests.*


**In this article:**

- What is the attachment feature?
- What are some example use-cases for the attachment feature?
- Attachment feature details


**What is the attachment feature?**

The attachment feature is now available in your Agoda Inbox, accessible only for confirmed bookings. This enables hosts and partners to share relevant information in image format, up to 10 MB per image. Guests can also share image attachments in the chat. The attachment feature is available on web and mobile app, directly though the Agoda Inbox feature.


**What are some example use-cases for the attachment feature?**

Attachments can be used to send check-in instructions, facilities schedules, directional maps, or other information to guests. In turn, guests can send copies of their passports or other relevant documents ahead of check-in. As a reminder, please do not send any sensitive information via attachments.


**Attachment feature details**

- Attachments can only be sent as an image file (.jpg or .png). If you would like to send another type of file, please convert the file online or take a screenshot.
- Only one image can be sent per message. If you need to send multiple images, please send them one at a time.
- Attachments sent by the host or property remain available in the guest chat for 14 days from the check-out date. After this period, they will be automatically removed and no longer accessible.
- In accordance with our Privacy Policy, image attachments may be reviewed, scanned, and analyzed. Please note, however, that hosts and properties are responsible for ensuring their own compliance with applicable privacy and data protection laws when requesting and processing any attachments from guests sent through this feature.

--- FILE: 4403266014739-thailand-vat.md ---
# Thailand VAT

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/4403266014739-Thailand-VAT

Updated: 2024-08-28T14:14:02Z

In order to comply with the law in a timely manner, we will commence with the process of registering under the VAT Act and apply 7% VAT to Thai consumers (not VAT registered) bookings made on or after 1 September 2021.

We will rely on the VAT information in our system which was provided by you and that such information is complete, accurate, and correct to the best of your knowledge as of the date you provided it.

The Act Amending the Revenue Code No. 53 B.E. 2564 (2021) (“e-Service Tax Law”) regarding value added tax (“VAT”) collection by foreign electronic service providers who provide services to non-VAT registrants in Thailand was published in the Royal Gazette on 10 February 2021, to take effect as of 1 September 2021.

As a company registered in Singapore providing electronic service to Thai consumers, Agoda is required to register under the e-Service Tax Law. Under the Act, Agoda is required to remit 7% VAT on amounts earned from Thai consumers to the Thai Revenue Department.

“Thai consumer” refers to a “service recipient who is non-VAT registered in Thailand”.

Under the VAT Act:

To update your VAT ID on the web after the property is live, go to the **Listings **page and click on **Edit listing****.** Then select **Tax. **Provide the 13-digit VAT ID and click **Save**.


June 11, 2021

Note: The VAT ID can only be updated on the desktop web. This functionality is not available on the app.


--- FILE: 4403408528275-information-on-e-card.md ---
# Information on e-Card

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/4403408528275-Information-on-e-Card

Updated: 2022-12-15T10:10:22Z

The e-Card is a physical credit card that Agoda provides to you for charging all eligible bookings. Like any other credit card, the Agoda e-Card can be swiped at any POS terminal as long as the terminal is under the 7011 merchant category code (MCC for Lodging - Hotels, Motels, Resorts, or Central Reservation Services businesses).

Once you receive your e-Card from us, along with instructions on how to use it, please confirm receipt by **Contacting Us**. The e-Card has no value in it until booking transactions are made. Your e-Card will also have an expiry date, so please make sure to check and only submit payment before its expiry.

Payments will be available to process up to 150 days after check-out. However, we recommend processing payments as soon as possible. Please also ensure that charges are processed in the same currency as the booking in order to avoid undercharging or overcharging.

Please **Contact Us** if you wish to set up the e-Card as your property’s preferred payout method.

--- FILE: 4403600372115-what-should-i-do-if-i-can-t-accommodate-a-guest.md ---
# What should I do if I can’t accommodate a guest?

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/4403600372115-What-should-I-do-if-I-can-t-accommodate-a-guest

Updated: 2024-08-28T13:43:46Z

Agoda is committed to providing the best travel experience to our guest and guarantees that they will be able to stay at the property they booked. Therefore, when you are unable to honor our booking, it not only harms our reputation, but it also creates a bad guest experience.

Under an unusual circumstance where you are unable to honor our booking and accommodate the guest at your property, this is considered booking rejection as stated in Agoda’s Terms and Conditions . You will be responsible to provide and prepay suitable alternate accommodation for our guest, including a private transfer at no extra cost. We recommend contacting your guest in advance to inform them of these arrangements via our Messaging System.

In the event that no alternative is available, you may contact** the Agoda Hotline for assistance **and,** based on ****Agoda’s Terms and Conditions section 14.4**, for each Booking that you fail to honor, you shall compensate Agoda an amount equivalent to one night's average nightly value of the Booking if you accommodate the Guest at your property or two nights' average nightly value if you relocate the Guest. This cost will be charged to your property later, depending on the payment method used by your property. This will normally be reflected as ‘**Adjusted Transaction**’ under your Transaction Page.

You can reach the Agoda Hotline team through the Contact us button and select **Booking related** and **Cannot honor Agoda booking**. If you have urgent booking-related issues, call us at the Agoda Hotel Hotline in your country as soon as possible.


*June 11, 2021*


In order to prevent future booking rejections, we recommend the following approach:

Cause |
Recommendation |
|
This occurs when multiple reservations are made for the same room on the same night |
Set up two-ways Calendar Sync to manage your availability across different platforms |
Incorrect price |
Familiarize yourself with the setup of your Calendar Rates, Promotions, Channel Discounts, and Additional FeesLearn how you can Calculate Your Net Rate with following guideline:(Amount loaded in Calendar) – (Promotion applied during that selling period + Channel discount applied) + (Additional fee if applied)After setting your nightly rate in the calendar, always double check the rates on Agoda.com |
|
|
Bank setup is rejected. Bank setup is pending. The 30-day payout window has not passed yet Autopay hasn’t been activated yet. Manually approve the payout and learn how to set up auto-pay |
|
|
Set up check-in instruction to remind guests to contact you at least 1 day in advance prior to check-in |
|
Property is unavailable |
Please make sure to plan ahead and close your availability according to your renovation timeline, or at least 30 days before deactivation. |
|
|
Close out your calendar allotment and availability to avoid receiving future bookings. Check if you have any upcoming bookings. If yes, please reach out to guests to inform them of the latest regulations and follow the above process. |
