--- FILE: 4409664733587-new-south-wales-nsw-short-term-rental-accommodation-stra-license.md ---
# New South Wales (NSW) Short Term-Rental Accommodation (STRA) License

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/4409664733587-New-South-Wales-NSW-Short-Term-Rental-Accommodation-STRA-License

Updated: 2022-12-15T10:20:28Z

The NSW Government’s * **Code of conduct for the short-term rental accommodation industry* of October 2021 (the “Code”) states the following: * *

*2.2.5 On and from the day that registration on the premises register becomes mandatory under planning laws, a booking platform must ensure that short-term rental accommodation premises are not advertised on the booking platform’s online booking service unless: (a) the premises is registered on the premises register, and (b) the registration number for the premises is displayed alongside the details of the premises on the booking platform’s online booking service*


All STRA premises in NSW require now a license in order to rent out their properties. For properties in NSW to be live on Agoda, we need the property’s license number assigned by local authorities to each individual property you wish to rent out. To apply, visit Short Term Rental Accommodation (STRA) | Planning Portal - Department of Planning and Environment (nsw.gov.au)


Any unlicensed property in NSW will be deactivated from November 1st, 2021. A deactivated property does not mean a deleted account. As long as your account is still active on Agoda, you may access your profile to manage your payments and settings.

Any booking for un-licensed properties in NSW with a check-in date on or after November 1st, 2021 must be canceled to comply with the NSW’s regulations. To stay up to date on any rules and regulations, we recommend you visit the Short-term rental accommodation - (nsw.gov.au).


If your property has been impacted, you will not be able to receive any bookings. If you wish to reactivate your property, Contact Us and provide your license number.

Note: Do not intentionally enter false information. Doing so may lead to penalties from the NSW government. License information provided by you will be displayed on your property page on Agoda and will be subject to inspection by the NSW government. Agoda reserves the right to deactivate any property that is found to have missing or false license information.

You may request re-activation of your property by us at AgodaHomes-Australia@agoda.com.


Update on Web

You may also add the license number yourself on Host Manage. Go to the **Listings **page. Click **Edit listing** and select **Rental License** under **Legal**. Provide your license type, number, full legal name, email address, property address, and room number. Save your changes.




Update on App

Note: You may add rental license information only on Host Manage web. This functionality is not available on the app.



**FAQ**

The NSW Government has implemented a new statewide regulatory framework for Short-Term Rental Accommodations (STRA) to complement the mandatory Code of Conduct. This new STRA regulation requires a license in order to rent out your propriety on Agoda.

Below are answers to frequently asked questions, but we also highly recommend that you visit the Short-term rental accommodation - (nsw.gov.au) website to apply for your license.


**Q: How do I apply for a license number for my listing?**

**Q: What is the license number? **

The license number is a digit number assigned by The department of Planning, Industry and Environment to each individual listing you register.


**Q: What if I refuse to register my listing?**


**Q: If my listing gets unlisted, how do I relist it?**

After getting a license, you will be provided a license number. Please provide that license number and any other required information to Agoda in order to relist your property on the site.


**Q: Do I need a separate license number for each of my properties?**

Yes, you will need to obtain a license number for each listing. Please apply for your license(s) and add your license number and other necessary information to your Agoda listings.


**Q: What happens if I intentionally enter false information?**


**Q: What will happen to my reservations if my listing is unlisted due to being unlicensed? **

Unlicensed STRA properties in NSW may be found in violation of the code of conduct, and Agoda has a policy of unlisting unlicensed properties. While bookings are not automatically canceled for unlisted properties, we reserve the right to cancel reservations for any unlicensed property. This may result in being fined according to the penalty policies outlined in your contract with Agoda. Please apply for the license as soon as possible and add the licensing number and other relevant information to your listings.


**Q: If my listing is unlisted, will Agoda automatically cancel my reservations? Should hosts cancel on their own?**


**Q: Will I still be able to access payment page if my property is unlisted?**

Yes. As long as your account is not deleted, you can still access your payment page and receive any payable funds.


**Q: Would you like to update your rental license? **

Please click HERE.

--- FILE: 5870701117331-french-meuble-de-tourisme-license-regulation.md ---
# French Meuble de Tourisme license regulation

Source: https://agodahomeshelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/5870701117331-French-Meuble-de-Tourisme-license-regulation

Updated: 2022-12-15T10:20:28Z

The French Government implemented a new statewide regulatory framework for furnished tourist accommodations, “Meublés de Tourisme” in France (Code of Conduct). As you may know, this regulation requires Agoda to retain a host name, host address and residence category (Main/Second) for each property listed on our site.

While the “Meublés de Tourisme” planning rules may apply already in your city, you still need to update your license number in Agoda's system in order to keep your property listing active.

Please be sure to update your license number and other required information as soon as possible.

Bookings made for your property without updated license information will be cancelled, and the property will be deactivated on Agoda.

Update on Web

You may also add the license number yourself on Host Manage. Go to the **Listings **page. Click **Edit listing** and select **Rental License** under **Legal**. Provide your license type, number, full legal name, email address, property address, and room number. Save your changes.


If you would like Agoda to enter your license number(s) on your behalf, please contact us here.

For more information about these requirements, please visit our local partner: TOURIZ.FR - FAQ.


Update on App

Note: You may add rental license information only on Host Manage web. This functionality is not available on the app.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

La législation française a mis en place un nouveau cadre réglementaire commune par commune pour les hébergements touristiques meublés dit « Meublés de Tourisme » en France (Loi pour une République numérique et la Loi ELAN). Vous savez peut-être déjà que ce règlement oblige Agoda à qualifier la catégorie de votre résidence (principale ou secondaire) pour chacune de nos annonces sur notre site et à figurer votre numéro d’enregistrement.

Si votre commune a déjà mis en place les règles pour les « Meublés de Tourisme », vous devez mettre à jour votre numéro d’enregistrement dès que possible dans le système d'Agoda afin de maintenir votre annonce sur notre site.

Sans la mise à jour de ces informations, les réservations qui sont confirmées seront annulées et votre logement sera désactivé sur Agoda.


Update on Web

Pour rajouter votre numéro d’enregistrement sur le site d’Agoda Homes, allez sur “Modifier le listing” puis cliquez sur “Licence de location”. Remplissez votre numéro d’enregistrement en dessous de “Numéro de licence”. Ajoutez aussi votre nom complet, votre e-mail, puis sauver en cliquant sur “Enregister”



Cette fonction n’est pas disponible sur l’App

Pour plus d’information, veuillez consulter notre partenaire TOURIZ.FR - FAQ

# How to update my facilities?

Source: https://agodapropertypartnerhelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/115006482827-How-to-update-my-facilities

Updated: 2021-09-20T06:56:06Z

**Overview**
**In this article, you will find information on how to update your property's facilities.**
In response to the COVID-19 outbreak, we have added a number of facilities on YCS which could potentially attract bookings during/post-COVID-19 to your property.
**Content **
This article includes
|


**How to update property amenities in YCS?**

- Login to YCS
- Go to
**Setting >** **Property Settings**
- Depends on the group, select the option on the left side:
-
**Useful Information - **to informed details such as check-in or out time
-
**Facilities section** - for property services, sports-related and more:
- Click ✅ to enable the facility (your property offers this facility)
- Click ❌ to deactivate the facility (your property does not have this facility)


- Click
**Save**
- Click on each tab (facility groups) and mark all the features which are available at your property.

**Facilities Sections**

-
**Property Services:** Facilities and services that are provided by your property.
- Examples of COVID-19 friendly facilities added: doctor/nurse on call, food delivery, first aid kit, sterilizing equipment, free face masks, hygiene certification, contactless check in-out.


-
**Language Spoken:** Languages that are spoken by the staff of your property. This is so customers know the best way to communicate with you during their stay.

-
**Payment information:** The type of payments that are accepted by your property.

-
**Sports and Recreation:** Sports and recreation facilities that are provided by your property.


**Useful Information Section**

Provide the requested information in Useful Information, giving customers a better understanding of your property and its services.


**How to update room amenities in YCS?**

- Login to YCS
- Go to
**Settings**
- Click
**Room Setups**
- Once the page is fully loaded,
**select the room** to expand room setup menu
- Click
**Room Level Amenities **section, the screen will show the active facilities under this room
- Tick the facility you want to add >
**Select **>** Apply**
- Click
**Save**


**Display on the property page**

**Property amenities** under** What they offer**


**Useful Information** under** What they offer**

**Room amenities** under** Room facilities**


__Important information__

- It might take up to 6 hours before reflecting on the website due to the caching issue.
- Your changes will be saved automatically.


**Frequently Asked Questions**

**Can I add operation hours for my facilities such as a gym, swimming pool?**

Yes! You can request via the Accommodation Support Team by clicking the Need Help button in YCS. We will add related information to the property page.


**I have some facilities however its not available in YCS for me to tick.**

--- FILE: 115006667768-how-do-i-change-my-property-description.md ---
# How do I change my property description?

Source: https://agodapropertypartnerhelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/115006667768-How-do-I-change-my-property-description

Updated: 2021-10-01T23:22:00Z

**Overview**
**In this article, you will find information about property descriptions on Agoda.**
**Content **
This article includes
|


**What is ****a p****roperty ****d****escription****?**

A property description covers the main information and selling points of your property. After reading it, a traveler should have a brief understanding of your property, such as the location, room types, facilities, and other features. A complete and well-written description will set your property apart and attract more bookings.




**How do I change my property description?**

Property descriptions on Agoda.com are automatically generated by an algorithm using the data you have provided. There is also an option to add your own description as well, you can send your hotel description in English or in local language(s) to Accommodation Support Team by clicking 'Need Help' button in YCS.

**Property Description Requirements**


There are certain rules we need to follow:

- Word count cannot exceed 160 words.
- The content must be unique, meaning it must not be a duplicate of other websites (copyright)
- Descriptions must be in paragraph format. No other format will be accepted (i.e. bullet point, screenshots, links to websites, etc.)
- The content must be written in the third person perspective (never use “we”, “us”, “I” or “our”)
- Recommended content includes the property’s location, facilities, the hotel’s outstanding features, and other unique selling points.
- Content must not include directions to the property, public notes, policies, or excessive information about facilities, restaurants, special offerings, schedules, etc.
- The content should be clear and easy to understand -- no flowery phrases, redundant information, overuse of adjectives, or excessive listings.
- Do not mention competitors or other hotels.
- The Content Team will try its best to include all information as requested, as long as it is necessary, useful for the guests, and conforms to our guidelines. The descriptions that our team adds is considered final.


**What is the best way to write a property description?**

Each paragraph should include a category summary. Many users only read the first sentence, so it should contain the most important information. The description should end with a context summary that helps a traveler visualize that property as an integral part of the vacation or business travel he or she is booking.


**Category summary**

Most travelers think about their accommodation in broad, standardized categories, and it’s therefore important to immediately inform the user of what kind of category the property fits in.

-
**Traveler purpose: **Transit hotel, business and convention hotel, road motel, beach resort, etc. These categories allow user to immediately identify or un-identify with the property.
-
**Property infrastructure or building type: L**arge resort or small BnB, modern or historic, high-rise or hidden alley, the building itself tells a big part of the story.
-
**Location: **Near the airport, in the gothic quarter, atop a mountain, next to the golf course, these aspects help the user evaluate the property in relation to their anticipated itinerary.

-
**Price: **Supremely indulgent, luxury, mid-price, high-value, budget – sure, the user can see the actual prices on the page, but they also want to compare those prices to their own preconceived notions of what they should be getting for those prices.

A good category summary describes the property’s type, location, and likely usage.

* Examples:*

-
Property: Large business hotel in a high-rise office complex

*The Continent Bangkok is a modern business hotel located in Bangkok’s CBD is closely situated to the capital’s embassies, premium offices, and high-end retail centers, providing a convenient base for efficient access to the city’s business and leisure activities.*


**Context ****summary**

Every property description should end with a strong selling summary that promotes the property as the ideal setting for the kind of traveler to its features, location, and price will attract.

*Examples:*

-
Property: Large business hotel in a high-rise office complex

*For serious business or just a high-class holiday in the center of this vibrant city, the Continent offers the best in five-star amenities and an unparalleled location that will save you time and effort on every day of your stay.*


|
**Please note that every property description will be reviewed by Agoda for compliance, length, and quality. We reserve the right to edit or reject submitted descriptions that do not follow the guidelines.**
|


**Frequently Asked Questions**

**Can I add operation hours for facilities in the property description?**

We have another section called property policies for such information, you can contact Accommodation Support Team by clicking 'Need Help' button in YCS to add information.

####
**What if there is incorrect information in the automatic-generated property ****description?**

Please kindly let us Accommodation Support Team know --we are happy to assist with corrections.


**Learn More**

--- FILE: 115009692387-promotion-types-and-features.md ---
# Promotion Types and Features

Source: https://agodapropertypartnerhelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/115009692387-Promotion-Types-and-Features

Updated: 2021-09-30T05:14:24Z

**Overview**
**In this article, we will outline all information about what kind of Promotion types are available and their features in YCS.**
**Content**
This article include topics of
|

#

**Promotion Types**


**There are different promotion templates that will help you create different sell strategies. Once you click on any type, you will see the short explanation in the box on the right side.**


Each template has different setup fields. Here are the list of templates and their explanation.

**Customized Promotion**- This template will allow you to enter a range of booking dates, stay dates and a discount that can be either a percentage, fixed amount or free night(s)
**Early Bird / Adv. Purchase** - This is the right template if you want to give a discount to customers who booked early by setting **the minimum number of days to book in advance**. For example, if you set 7 Minimum number of days to book in advance, a customer will be able to book rates with this promotion if they search for a stay at least 7 days before their booking date.
**Last Minute**- This promotion will consider **the maximum number of days in advance** and range of stay date. For example, if you set 7 Maximum number of days in advance, only a customer who booked with stay date within 7 days from their booking date will be able to book the rate with this promotion.

**72-hours Promotion** - This template will be giving a limited time sale offer. The promotion can only be booked for the next number of days (default 3 days).

**Weekend Getaway **- This template will support **the specific day of a week on stay date** and offer discounts for customers who booked on weekend. The default days of the week are Friday, Saturday, and Sunday.

**Long Stays** - When you need to offer a special discount for customers who stay longer at your property, you can set **Minimum length of stay** within this template. The default length of stay is 3 days.

**After Hours Promotion** - You will have an ability to limit the specific time a booking can be made. As the default booking time is 00:00 am - 06:00 am, customers who made a booking during these time (property local time) will see the rates with this promotion.

**Express Tonight** - This template allows you to sell your last rooms quickly and easily by entering the final selling rate in the promotion.

**China Only** - Offering a special deal for our **Chinese customers.** This promotion will be available for customers who use Mandarin Chinese or search from Greater China.

**Free Night** - This template will offer **free night(s) benefit** to customers who booked at the selected stay dates.

**Features and Definitions**


There are many options you can select in order to build a promotion. Below is a guide for each feature:

**Promotion name:** Renaming your promotion. This will be displayed in YCS for your reference and searching purpose
**Stackable promotion toggle:** A function to combine benefits from other active promotion when customers search with this promotion
**Sale dates:** Dates that the customers can book this promotion
**Stay dates:** Dates that the customers search for check-in
**Minimum length of stay：** Customer have to book at least this number of stay dates in order to see the promotion
**Maximum length of stay：** Customer have to book with number of stay dates less than this number in order to see the promotion
**Minimum number of days in advance：** This allows you to choose how far in advance a customer must book before check-in date.
**Maximum number of days in advance： **This will limit how far in advance of check-in that customer can book for this promotion
**Customer can book on： **Option to select book date in days of a week
**Customer can check in on： **Option to select check-in date in days of a week
**Booking time from： **Starting of time that you allow promotion to display. This will rely on your property local time.
**Booking time to：**Ending of time that you allow promotion to display. This will rely on your property local time.
**External code： **The code that you can use as a reference with the channel manager
**Discount type： **The discount that you offer to customers which can be in percentage, amount or free night(s)
**Minimum number of rooms： **Required minimum number of room from customers per booking
**Apply discount on： **When you offer free night(s) you can select some specific day that this offer will be applied on.
**How many times does the discount apply： **If you offer free night(s) and have set minimum 2 nights length of stay, once customers book a 4-night length of stay, you want to offer 2 free nights (Multiple times per booking) or 1 night (Once per booking)
**Add restriction： **Restrictions can be set to limit some customers group, rooms or search criteria from this promotion. Available options are Rate Plans, Room types, Customer Segments, Cancellation Policy and Blackout dates.

**Frequent Asked Questions**

**When will the promotion take effective?**


After created, your promotion will instantly display on the website and available to the customers based on the criteria you provided.

**How does the cancellation policy in promotion works?**

Promotion's cancellation policy overwrites all the other cancellation policy.

**Can I add restriction to promotions?**

Blackout days, cancellation policy and other restrictions can be added in **Add a restriction **section

**Learn More**

**Related Articles **

# How do I login using the PIN code?

Source: https://agodapropertypartnerhelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/115009756728-How-do-I-login-using-the-PIN-code

Updated: 2024-08-28T13:38:46Z

**Overview**
**You ****can go**** password-less! Just to sign in once using the YCS app,**** and you’ll stay signed in****. Also, you can use the app**** to sign into YCS via desktop – a more secure and hassle-free way to access your property information.**
**In this article, we will outline ****the ****benefit****s**** of PIN Code, how it**** works****,**** and ****how ****to troubleshoot if you didn’t receive any ****PIN Code ****in your ****e****mail.**
**Content **
This article includes
|


**Why ****r****eplac****e**** ****a ****p****assword with PIN Code****?**

-
**YCS ****d****ata ****p****rotection and ****s****ecurity**

**It is more secure** than using a password, which can be hacked. As YCS contains highly sensitive information, it is essential that this information is kept as secure as possible.
-
**Single ****s****ign-****o****n functionality.**

You only need to **sign**** ****in once to the app**, to stay logged AND use the app to sign in on the desktop – and never enter a password again!


**How ****does the ****PIN Code**** work****?**

-
Log in to YCS with your username (email address):.

-
You can check “remember me” to make sure the system remembers your username.
-
Once you click “next,” an option will appear to let you choose your preferred method of getting the PIN Code.

**Via YCS App **

-
Choose the YCS app option and click “
**Send PIN Code**” button.
-
A pop-up window will appear. If you don’t have the app yet, you can proceed to download by scanning the QR code. If you have installed the YCS app, click on “
**Send PIN to YCS App**”


- A notification from YCS app will appear on your phone


-
Type the
**PIN Code** into the box in the YCS window
-
You can choose to “
**Keep me sign****ed**** in**” so when you open YCS, it will be automatically signed in with your username.
-

--- FILE: 115010406568-how-do-i-change-the-property-name.md ---
# How do I change the property name?

Source: https://agodapropertypartnerhelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/115010406568-How-do-I-change-the-property-name

Updated: 2024-08-28T12:45:02Z

**Overview**
**Your ****property name is**** set up based on the information you provided on the registration form.**** ****There ****may ****be some situation****s**** that**** ****require you to change the property name. In this article, we will outline tips for naming your property and how you can request changes****.**
**Content****s**
This article includes:
|


**Tips on naming your property**

Your property name is important to ensure visibility and clarity to Agoda’s customers when searching and selecting their accommodation.

**Some ****things**** ****to avoid****:**

-
**Usage of Abbreviations **
-
An abbreviation will likely confuse the customer and stop them from booking your property since they are not clear about the meaning behind it.

-
**Usage of emojis, symbols or ALL CAPS **
-
Though it might be cute or eye-catching, to make sure your property looks credible, trustworthy and professional, it’s best to avoid unnecessary additions.

-
**Includ****ing a price or promotion **
-
Price and promotions are subjected to change; keeping it updated will be hard since you would need to update every expiring price or promotion. By updating names too often, you may cause repeat customers to miss your property entirely.

-
**Adding translated name in other languages **
-
Adding translation in the brackets will cause duplication. When customers visit Agoda in that specific language version, they will see duplicate names and it won’t look professional. If you have specific translations you prefer, you can share them with us and we will set it for you to be visible on specific Agoda website and app language versions.



**Tips****:**

-
**Keep it short and unique**
-
Compact names are more memorable and easy to recall by travelers.

-
**Include your accommodation type**** **
-
Your name should tell the guest something specific about your place. Including accommodation type will provide more clarity for customer to avoid any misunderstandings.

-
**Capitalize** **T**he **F**irst **L**etter
-
Standard format in Agoda has the first letter only as capitalized. We recommend you to follow this guideline so it will look consistent and match the website design.



**How ****to update property name****s?**

If you would like to update a property name, simply submit your request to **Agoda accommodation support** via the Support widget in YCS.



**Frequently Asked Questions**

####
**My property ****name is wrong when the view is in ****ano****ther language (not English). How do I change this?**

You may send us the suggested property name in the language you would like to amend. The Agoda Content team will then confirm the updates before the property name is changed from our end.

To send suggestions, please send the request **Agoda accommodation support** via the Support widget in YCS.

####
**There is another property ****with ****a similar name ****to ****mine****. Can you remove the other property from Agoda?**

Property names should be based on the name used during the business license registration process and certificate. These names should not be duplicated on our website or app. Should you come across this issue, please reach out to **Agoda accommodation support** via the Support widget in YCS for our further investigation.


**Learn More**


--- FILE: 115010501008-how-to-best-respond-to-guest-reviews.md ---
# How to best respond to guest reviews?

Source: https://agodapropertypartnerhelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/115010501008-How-to-best-respond-to-guest-reviews

Updated: 2021-08-14T16:40:45Z

#
**Overview**
**In this article, we’ll show you how to handle the reviews you receive from guests, including the best way to reply to a review, both positive and negative, to create optimal resolution and reputation enhancement. **
#
** Contents**
This article includes:
|


**Responding to guests’ reviews**

Getting reviews is just the first step in building your property’s online reputation. How you respond to reviews is just as important, as this process represents your ongoing relationship with your guests. Travelers look carefully at the interaction between property and guests, and use it to create an image of you. Our research shows that 85% of travelers agree that a thoughtful response to a review improves their impression of a hotel. There are very few things you can do that have an 85% benefit rate. Don’t miss this opportunity!

That said, proper review response is not always simple. You have to be thoughtful, responsive, and conciliatory if necessary. We’ve prepared some basic tips to guide you.

How to best respond to positive reviews

-
**Thank the guests.**
- Always thank them for their stay, and express how much you appreciate them taking the time to write a review. This immediately demonstrates politeness, professionalism, and service-mindedness.

-
**Be specific and personal.**
- Craft a personalized message to show that you care about each of your guests. Avoid using a standard template reply for every response. Make references to specific items in the review so that it is clear that you read it all the way through.

-
**Be timely and keep it short.**
- Keep your response short and sweet. Do not over-explain your own position or make excuses, and don’t use the response to promote your property.

-
**Emphasize the positives, within reason.**
- Repeat specific things guests say they enjoyed at your hotel to further highlight your positive reputation for potential guests, but don’t be excessive in self-praise.

-
**Double-check before submitting.**
- Take the time to check grammar and spelling and to make sure your tone and message are clear. Double-check the guest’s first name to make sure you spelled it exactly right.

-
**Encourage a return visit.**
- End your reply by expressing hope to serve the guests again on future travels.



**Example of a good response**

|
Dear Nick,
Thank you for your helpful feedback regarding your stay! We are thrilled to know that you loved the experience. Also, thank you for the kind words about our breakfast and staff service. We put a lot of thought into every dish we serve, and are proud of our excellent staff. Your kind words reaffirm the hard work we put in every day.
Thank you for choosing us and we look forward to welcoming you again soon.
Sincerely,
Jenny Kim, Guest Services Manager
|

###

**Why is this response good?**

- Thanking the guest for taking the time to leave a review.
- Reinforcing the compliments that the guest gave to highlight why your property is a great option for other travelers.
- Ending by thanking the guest again and encouraging a return visit.


**What should not be included in a response?**

- Guest's full name -- just their first name is enough.
- Personal email address and phone number of guest or property.
- Links to other websites.
- Price related references such as room rates.
- Profanity and discriminatory comments.
- OTAs by name

** **

**Responding to negative reviews**

Unfortunately, not all reviews you’ll get will be positive. Even the best properties can’t provide every guest with the perfect stay. At some point, a guest will complain in writing – and it will be posted on your property page.

But there’s no reason to panic – even bad reviews are an opportunity if handled correctly. But you do need to reply quickly and strategically. Never ignore a negative review!

##

**Why respond to negative reviews?**

- Remember -- You're not just replying to just the one guest, but to everyone who reads it, including potential guests.
- Replying shows that you care about feedback and guest satisfaction and have taken steps to ensure this problem won't happen to the next guest.
- Criticism helps you learn what to improve to deliver better guest experiences.

#

#
**How to respond to negative reviews?**

-
**Address the reviewer by name. **
- Your guests want to be heard individually and addressed personally.
- Avoid the generic “Dear guest,” or “Dear customer.”
- Use the first name of the guest only, to respect privacy.

-
**Begin by thanking the reviewer. **
- Express gratitude for taking the time to leave the feedback, even for bad reviews, as it shows the guest and anyone reading that you have a service-minded attitude.
- EXAMPLE:
*“Thank you for your review. I’m sorry to hear you had such a frustrating experience, but we really appreciate you bringing this issue to our attention.”*


-
**Apologize and sympathize.**
- Acknowledge the guest’s bad experience, say sorry, and don’t make excuses for what went wrong.
- Don’t be overly apologetic. Keep your apology sincere and short.
- EXAMPLE:
*“We apologize that our service did not satisfy your expectations.”*
- If possible, make a specific reference to the feelings that the guest expresses. If the guest says the bed was too hard, for example, say
*“We are sorry that the bed was not able to provide optimal sleep.”* This shows that you are listening carefully.


-
**Take responsibility but defend your values.**
- If the negative experience can be attributed to a specific situation, such as a renovation, you can mention it if the situation has been resolved. However, make sure that you still accept responsibility for the experience.
- Insert a little marketing in your response to the bad review -- explain what your customers usually experience and reinforce the company’s standard values.
- EXAMPLE:
*“We’re normally known for our exceptional attention to detail, and we regret that we missed the mark.”*


-
**Make things right and show action**
- If a change or renovation has been made that impacts the situation, be sure to mention it. EXAMPLE:
*“We are sorry that you didn’t find the breakfast adequate. We have since added more food options to the breakfast buffet.” *
- If no change has been made, you can allude to planned changes.
- EXAMPLE:
*“We intend to add more equipment to our fitness center in the near future so that guests will not have to queue for their use.”*
- If the problem has no clear solution, at the very least let them know how you are investigating their complaint to make sure other guests will not have the same experience. EXAMPLE:
*“We can’t fix the past, but you have my personal commitment to improve the way our staff serves every customer. Until then, please accept my sincerest apologies on behalf of everyone on the team.”*


-
**Invite them to come back. **
- After you have addressed the issue and explain your action, ask the guest for another chance so you might offer them a better experience next time. Be welcoming and open, but not specific in the invitation.
- EXAMPLE: We hope you’ll visit us again so that we can show you our improvements based on your valuable feedback.”
-


|
*Please do not include your personal contact information such as phone number and email address in the response.*
|


# Frequently Asked Questions

**Can I edit my response? **

You can easily edit your response through YCS. To edit the response on the YCS mobile application:

- Go to
**More** and select
-
Click
**“Edit this response” **on the response you want to edit.
-
After editing, the response should be displayed under the
**“Response pending approval”**
|
|

You can also edit your response on the YCS website, but only ones that were rejected. To edit rejected responses:

-
Go to
**Manage** and select
-
Select
**Rejected responses**
-
Click
**“View Response** “and edit the response directly on the text box.

**Since Agoda doesn’t allow personal contact information in the response, how can guests further communicate with me?**

Guests can communicate with you through the following channels:

-
**Agoda Customer Messaging System**, which allows guests to send a message to you before or after making a booking. You can check the messages both in YCS or in your registered email.
- Guests can contact you directly via call or email from the contact information of your hotel provided on the
**booking voucher** once they have made a booking.
-
Guests may reach out to
**Agoda’s customer service team **for any inquiries related to bookings or special requests. Agoda’s customer service team may contact you for further follow-up via phone or email.

Learn more about **how can guests communicate with you** HERE.


**Learn more**

# How can I use Advance Guarantee Program (AGP)?

Source: https://agodapropertypartnerhelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/115011637287-How-can-I-use-Advance-Guarantee-Program-AGP

Updated: 2021-09-15T15:40:27Z

|



The AGP program is handled in extranet under the ePass section. Please see the screenshot of the menu section below.



You will need to select the Advance Guarantee contract you want to see transactions details for. If only one contract has been agreed to and is set in the system, it will be selected by default.

The transactions displayed under a given contract are split into two separate tables on the same page:

1. Departed Transactions: these are the reservations benefiting from the Advance Guarantee conditions that have checked out and have been deducted from the Advance Guarantee Amount on check-out day.

2. Transactions Pending Departure: these are the transactions reservations benefiting from the Advance Guarantee conditions that have not reached their check out date. You can filter the transaction to appear in each table by booking dates, check-in dates or check out dates:


In the ePass drop down you will find "Advance Guarantee Transactions". Here you will see all bookings benefiting from the conditions of the Advance Guarantee Program, as well as the remaining balance of your property.



Please kindly your Market Manager for program extension.

# How can I adjust my price?

Source: https://agodapropertypartnerhelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/115011808628-How-can-I-adjust-my-price

Updated: 2021-09-28T07:34:31Z

**Overview**
**In this article, you will find information how to update room rates in YCS.**** **
**Content****s**
This article includes:
|


**How to update your rates?**

It's very important to keep your price up to date. **In case your property is not connected to any channel manager** you can easily manage your rate in Calendar menu.

- Go to
**Rate & Allotment **and select **View**
-
**Select Room Type and Rate Plan **that you want to update
-
**Select the date range** that you would like to adjust
- On the right side,
**fill in your price**
- Click
** **on** Save**




If your price is different for Single, Double and Full Occupancy. You can change this under the calendar page:

-
**Select Room Type and Rate Plan **that you want to update
-
**Select the date range** that you would like to adjust
- On the right side click
**Advanced**
**Fill in the price for Single / Double or Full Occupancy**
- Click
** Save**



**How to set minimum/maximum length of stay?**

-
**Select Room Type and Rate Plan **that you want to update
-
**Select the date range** that you would like to adjust
- On the right side, click
**Advanced**
- Add
** Min and Max stay**
- Click
** Save**




**What is the minimum night for stay-through?**

To help property secure better occupancy during the peak period, we have implemented Minimum Length of Stay Through. This function allows users to set a minimum length of stay by specifying the number of nights that must be booked for stays that include the restriction day (e.g. Monday) in any part of the stay date range.


**What is the difference between Min LOS and Min Night for Stay-Through?**

-
**Min LOS** - applies only on the arrival date
-
**Min Night for Stay-Through** - applies on stay period, meaning any stay date that arrives or touches this min stay through, the booking will be abided by the rules of that night to the entire stay

For example, if the property set a restriction on Friday, Jan 1st.

-
**Min LOS** - applies only on to bookings checking-in/arriving on Fri Jan 1st.
-
**Min Night for Stay-Through** - applies to any booking that includes Fri, Jan 1st (but not bookings checking out on Jan 1st)


**How to set minimum night for stay-through ?**

-
**Select Room Type and Rate Plan **that you want to update
-
**Select the date range** that you would like to adjust
- On the right side, click
**Advanced**
- Add
** # of nights**
- Click
** Save**



- If you work with channel manager, you have to update your rates and allotments in their system. Please contact their support team in case you need any assistance.
- As per our agreement, it is your responsibility to keep our inventory up to date at all times.


**Frequently Asked Questions**

**Can I request Agoda to manage the rate for me?**

As per our agreement, it is your responsibility to keep our inventory up to date at all times. If you need any guidelines or instructions, we are more than happy to help. please kindly reach out Agoda Accommodation Support via the Support Widget in the YCS.

**Can I set up price based on how many people stay in the room?**

Yes! We have this feature available for you. Please refer to this article.


**Learn more**

--- FILE: 115012432788-all-you-need-to-know-about-bookings.md ---
# All you need to know about bookings

Source: https://agodapropertypartnerhelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/115012432788-All-you-need-to-know-about-bookings

Updated: 2021-09-27T06:26:46Z

**In this article, you will find information about our bookings and how they get generated**

Agoda provides instant bookings to the guests, therefore you have to keep the rates and allotment up-to-date all time.

Included topics:


We list your property on our website if all of the below criteria meets:


**How do I get the booking vouchers?**

Once a booking is made on your property, the system will automatically send an email to you with the booking voucher. In case you are working with channel manager, you will receive the booking in your PMS as well.

You can also monitor your bookings in our extranet under **Reports** tab in **Bookings**.

Find more detail here about how to acknowledge the bookings.


__Important information__


**How is the total amount calculated?**

Agoda does not send any invoices. We deduct the commission from the total amount paid by guests.

Reference Sell rate = total amount paid by guest

Net rate = total amount without commission

On the right-hand side of the voucher, you can see if there is any other discount applied (promotion, rate channel)



**How can I reply to a special request?**

In case you receive special requests from a guest, and you would like to contact the guests you need to reply the provided email address under Customer Notes at the bottom of the voucher.


**How do I know if there is a cancellation?**

Once a cancellation has been made by a customer, the system will automatically send an email to notify you, with details of a booking and a request link to acknowledge a cancellation request.

The cancellation fee may be charged based on the cancellation policy that you set up.


__Important information__

External Code ID |
This field is for channel manager purpose. Leave it blank if not in use |
From* |
First eligible date of rate plan |
Until* |
Last eligible date of the rate plan |


Benefit |
The guest benefit of this rate plan. Make sure that the benefits are consistent with the selected Offer Type and the Rate Plan name |

|
Room Type that will be sold on the rate plan |
Cancellation Policy |
Cancellation policy that will be applied to the rate plan |
Sell limit per day |
No of maximum daily allotment that can be sold for this rate plan |
Min LOS |
The minimum number of nights required to book this rate plan. Guest is allowed to book this rates if the number of night is higher than the Min LOS |
Min Days in Advance |
The minimum number of days in advance for the rates. For example, if you set it as 2, guests can purchase this rate only from the day after tomorrow. Leave blank if rate can be booked at anytime |
Max LOS |
The maximum number of nights required to book this rate plan. Guest are not allowed to stay more than max LOS |
Max Days in Advance |
The maximum number of days in advance for the rates. For example, if you set it as 2, guests can purchase this rate for the following check-in dates |



**If you hover your mouse over the text you will see a short explanation (marked with red frame)**


Absolutely, you can set different rate plans to offer different benefits, time periods, room types etc.

If a rate plan is no longer needed, you can deactivate it. Alternatively, if you have planed the active period of the rate plan, you can set up the time period in YCS too. Then the rate plan will be inactive automatically.

# How can I set the price for extra beds?

Source: https://agodapropertypartnerhelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/115012542267-How-can-I-set-the-price-for-extra-beds

Updated: 2021-09-20T06:55:34Z

**Overview **
**In this article, you will find information about how to set up price for extra bed.**
**Contents**
This article includes:
|


**How to set price in YCS?**

There are 3 places to set up extra beds in YCS:


**In the Room Setup**

In the *Occupancy Settings* of *Room Setup *if you add a number to the “extra bed”, this means that that specific room type can accommodate that number of extra beds. Please note: currently, our system is able to manage only 1 extra bed.

- Go to
**Settings**
- Click
** Room Setup**
- Select
**room type **that you want to update
- Select if an
**extra bed** is allowed in the room type (only 1 extra bed type allowed).
- Click
**Save**



**In the Property Settings**

In *Property Settings,* you can input the __standard__ extra bed price that will be pre-populated in the extra bed field of the Calendar page.

- Go to
**Settings**
- Click
**Property Settings**
- Under
** Property Age Policy** Fill in your** Extra Bed Price**
- Click
** Save**


**In the Calendar**

In *Calendar*, for all rooms that have extra beds, there is a field on the *Advanced* tab on the right-hand side, where the extra bed price can be input. If you loaded a rate for the extra bed on Property Settings, this rate will automatically be loaded there. They can be modified at any time.

- Go to
** Manage**
- Click
** Calendar**
- Select
** Room Type **and** Rate Plan **that you want to update
-
**Select the date range** that you would like to adjust
- On the right side, click
**Advanced**
- Update
**Extra Bed** price
- Click
** Save**



- If you update the Extra Bed price in
**Property Settings**, it will update your extra bed's price for all days.
- If you use a channel manager - please inform your channel manager

#

**Frequently Asked Questions**

**Can I set different extra bed price for different room types?**

Yes, you can! Simply update the price in the room setup instead of other ways.


**Can I set an extra bed price for a certain rate plan?**

Absolutely, in the calendar, you can choose the rate plan then update the extra bed price

A list of Channel Managers that are able to connect with Agoda, is attached at the end of this page.

|
|
|
|
Did not pass system validation -- for example if your Single rate is higher than your Double rate, or any rate is lower than the minimum rate set for that room type. |
Depending on the error, generally, you can fix it by either correcting the data as highlighted in the error message, such as updating the relevant settings in the YCS Room Page. |
|
Technical Issue/Connection Error |
This can be caused by several unpredictable factors. We recommend you wait for a few minutes and try to send the update again. |


In general, a booking notification will still be sent via email from Agoda even if you are connecting through a Channel Manager. In some cases, you may receive a booking confirmation from Agoda but not receive that same booking via the Channel Manager system.

|
|
|
|
Channel Manager's Request API does not cover the booking period |
Please contact your Channel Manager for more information. |
|
Connection issue on Channel Manager or on Agoda |
Agoda will try to push the booking message 3 times for Hint partners. If it still fails, we will send the info via email to your Channel Manager. For non-Hint partners, the Channel Manager will have to send a new request to Agoda when the connection is restored. |


|
|
|
|

# How do I manage my rooms?

Source: https://agodapropertypartnerhelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/115015418567-How-do-I-manage-my-rooms

Updated: 2021-09-23T12:44:46Z

**Overview**
**In this article, you will find information about how to set up and manage your rooms in YCS.**
**Content **
This article includes
|

#

**How to add a room?**

Here are the steps how to add new room type. Please provide as many details as possible.

- Log in to YCS
- Go to
**Setting** and select **Room Setup**
- Click
**Add Room Button**
**Fill in details**
- Click
** Save**





**Explanation of each field**

**Basic Info**

-
**Room Name:** Enter the first letter of the room name. You must select from the dropdown list
-
**External Code ID:** Enter the ID provided by your property or channel manager to help you map rooms
-
**No. of Rooms:** No of the rooms for this room type that are available
-
**Minimum Rate:** Enter the lowest possible rate for this room. This is to ensure you do not enter a rate lower than the minimum when uploading the rates.

**Occupancy Settings**

-
**Persons:** Select the number of persons that can stay in the room based on the existing beds.
-
**Extra Beds:** Select the number of extra beds that are allowed in this room. (Maximum one extra bed is supported)
-
**Baby Cots:** Select the number of baby cots/cribs that are allowed in this room.
-
**Allow children in the room type:** Provide information if children can stay in this room type. For child age policy set up click here.

**Content**

-
**Upload photos:** You must upload at least 1 photo for each room with a minimum resolution of 800 x 600 pixels and a maximum file size of 4 MB.
-
**Room Size:** Enter the average size of this room type in sq.m.
-
**View:** Select the view of this room.
-
**Amenities:** Select all amenities that are available in this room.
-
**Bedding:** Select the number and types of beds found in this room.
-
**Bathrooms:** Select the number of bathrooms available in this room


**How to activate/deactivate room?**

- Go to
** Settings** and select **Room Setup**
- Click the
** greyed box** to activate the room/ Click the **green box** for deactivation.
- Click
** OK** and **Save**.


**How to add/update room name?**

If you would like to change the name of existing room, below is the steps;

- Go to
**Settings** and select **Room Setup**
-
**Click on the room** that you would like to amend the name
-
**Under Room Name field** - remove existing room name and start typing (Start from the most important keyword, then add other terms to get the room name you need. Be patient! The list can be quite long)
-
**Select a standard room name **from the drop-down list
- Click
**Save**

Check out more tips to **find a suitable room name** and why we recommend using **standard room names**.


- For existing bookings, updating 'Room name' will not change the actual name in the booking voucher sent to customers
-
Updating the 'Room name'
** **will likely affect upcoming reservations. Remember to check your upcoming bookings first.
- If your property is using a channel manager, please contact your channel manager partner to remove/add the mapping on their side.
|

#

**What if I can't use any of standard room names, can I request to add unique names?**

--- FILE: 1500002419101-proactive-date-amendment-fee-waiver-manual.md ---
# Proactive Date Amendment Fee Waiver Manual

Source: https://agodapropertypartnerhelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/1500002419101-Proactive-Date-Amendment-Fee-Waiver-Manual

Updated: 2021-09-20T06:55:29Z

#
**Overview**
**The Proactive Date Amendment Fee Waiver tool allows you to preselect your property’s policy on allowing date amendment (if any).**
**Content**
This article includes
|


**What is a Proactive Date Amendment Fee Waiver?**

- A simple tool that you can use to preselect your property’s policy on allowing date amendment. You choose the circumstance under which you will allow date amendment (if any).
- Any qualified situation that falls within the circumstance selected under the Proactive Date Amendment Fee Waiver will automatically be allowed through our system.

**Benefits to Property**

- Save time and effort while improving customer satisfaction.
- Substantially decrease the number of calls and emails between properties and guests, making the interaction seamless for you and guests.

**How to Set Up?**

- From the “Settings” screen, click on “Property Settings”

- Select or scroll down to “Optional Settings” until you see “Accept amendment fee waiver requests from our agents”

- If the box is checked for “Accept amendment fee waiver requests from our agents,” you will see a drop-down menu under “Auto date amendment fee waiver setting” where you can preselect your property’s policy on allowing date amendment
- The circumstances you can choose from include:
- Waive fee up to 24 hours before check-in date
- Waive fee up to 48 hours before check-in date
- Waive fee up to 72 hours before check-in date
- Waive fee up to 120 hours before check-in date

- By default, your property will opt into the following option:
- Waive fee up to 48 hours before check-in date

- You can opt-out from the program by unchecking the box for “Accept amendment fee waiver requests from our agents”


**Frequently Asked Questions**

**How do I opt-out, or make changes, to the circumstance that I am opted in to?**

You can opt-out or make any changes directly on YCS by following the instructions on this page.


**Can I quit the program?**

Yes, you can opt-out of the program on YCS by following the instructions on this page.


**Will I receive an additional amount if the new dates are more expensive?**

Yes, you will receive an additional amount equal to the rate difference between the original and new dates.


**How will I know when a booking is amended automatically by this tool?**

You will receive the date amendment details by email each time there is a date amendment fee waiver. The email will resemble a standard booking amendment confirmation email and will include the Booking ID, new check-in and check-out dates, and booking value.

--- FILE: 1500006164381-how-do-i-identify-property-collect-bookings.md ---
# How do I identify Property Collect bookings?

Source: https://agodapropertypartnerhelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/1500006164381-How-do-I-identify-Property-Collect-bookings

Updated: 2021-09-20T06:55:26Z

We are displaying the payment method of your bookings in multiple places.

Booking Voucher

The voucher of a Property Collect booking will always read "TO BE PAID BY GUEST" (1) rather than "PREPAID".

The total booking amount is also the sell inclusive amount to be paid by the guest (3).

The nightly price breakdown will only include the sell inclusive amount that you must collect from the guest. This includes commission too, which will later be offset in ePass. (2)

We display the name of the guest that made the booking to have you know who to collect payment from. (4)

YCS Booking Page

On the Reports > Bookings page of YCS you will be able to filter your bookings by payment model (5,6)

The booking summary will also display the payment model as “Property Collect” (7,8)

YCS ePass Page

You will be able to identify Property Collect bookings in ePass by looking at the “Booking Paid By” field (9)

# How do I verify Property Collect bookings?

Source: https://agodapropertypartnerhelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/1500006168521-How-do-I-verify-Property-Collect-bookings

Updated: 2021-09-20T06:55:25Z

##
|


The first action you will be able to take once a Property Collect booking is confirmed is to verify if the credit card the guest has provided is valid. Clicking ‘Check if guest credit card is valid’ (1) will return an instant result and unlock further actions based on the outcome.

This action is available from the time of the booking until check-in date + 24 hours.


Customers whose credit cards pass this verification are less likely to cancel. If they do cancel and there is a cancellation fee due, charges can usually, but not always, be successfully made to the credit card. This feature is a customer-friendly way of checking if a booking is secure, prior to check-in.

This action is available for Property Collect bookings made with credit card guarantee, from the time of booking until 24 hours after check-in day.

If the first verification fails, you can request a new credit card from the guest or contact them via our messaging service in YCS.

No, if verification fails, you can request a new credit card right away.

This feature can only be used once. If clicked, it will be unavailable for further action. It will also not be available outside the mentioned time window.


--- FILE: 1500006176201-how-do-i-view-the-guest-s-credit-card.md ---
# How do I view the guest’s credit card?

Source: https://agodapropertypartnerhelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/1500006176201-How-do-I-view-the-guest-s-credit-card

Updated: 2021-09-20T06:55:24Z

This action is available from 7 days before check-in.


Payment Card Industry Data Security Standard, or PCI DSS, is a set of requirements put together by major payment networks including Visa and Mastercard. You must declare your compliance with these requirements to view the guest’s payment card details. You can learn more about PCI DSS here.

This action will only be available if the guest's card verification has been completed. The guest's credit card can be viewed a maximum of 3 times.

No, Agoda's systems do not currently support the sharing of the CVV/CVC number of the guest's payment card.

No. Agoda's Property Collect bookings are strictly pay-at-hotel bookings, you should not collect payment from the guest’s credit card prior to arrival. We understand that in some circumstances you may want to temporarily hold an amount to secure a booking in high occupancy periods, however, this is not guest-friendly, and we advise against it.

You need to have a 'YCS SMS' number set up for your account. You can request this from Agoda Accommodation Support via the support widget in YCS.

If you do not accept the initial payment card of the guest, you can request a new one through the YCS extranet. We also recommend you message the guest to let them know which cards you accept.

It is not possible to view the guest’s payment card details more than 3 times as Agoda systems will automatically clear the data afterward.

If you choose to view the guest's credit card, you will become responsible for collecting any cancellation fees should they occur.

By default, Agoda attempts to collect the cancellation fee from the guest's credit card on your behalf. However, if you view the guest's credit card, Agoda will no longer attempt to collect any fees. This logic was introduced to avoid double charging the guest.


--- FILE: 1500006247942-how-do-i-request-a-new-credit-card-from-the-guest.md ---
# How do I request a new credit card from the guest?

Source: https://agodapropertypartnerhelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/1500006247942-How-do-I-request-a-new-credit-card-from-the-guest

Updated: 2021-09-20T06:55:26Z

#
**Overview**
**To help secure payment for your Property Collect with credit card guarantee bookings, we are providing you with a set of features to validate the guest’s payment card. **
**These features are available on the booking summary page in the YCS Extranet (Reports > Bookings). Availability of the actions you can take is based on a specific sequence and the time until check-in. **
**Contents**
This article includes:
|


**How do I request new credit card details from the guest?**

If the guest's credit card verification fails, or you find the card details invalid upon viewing them, you will be able to request a new credit card from the guest.

- Clicking ‘Request new guest credit card’ (1) will trigger an email to the guest with a secure web link to provide a new credit card for payment.
- Once new card information has been entered by the guest, it will be made available in the YCS Extranet, and you will receive an email notification.

This action is available up to check-in date + 24 hours and Guests will be given 48 hours at most to provide new payment details.


**Frequently Asked Questions**

**What should I do if the guest does not provide a new credit card or if the new card is also invalid?**

You may contact the guest through the YCS messaging service. In some circumstances, you can also request to cancel the booking if the guest fails to enter new card details within the allowed time frame (usually 48 hours). Find more details here

**Can I request credit card details from the guest by phone/email?**

No, you should only exchange credit card details through the secure link used by this YCS feature.


**Learn More**

--- FILE: 1500010471361-philippines-quarantine-hotels.md ---
# Philippines - Quarantine Hotels

Source: https://agodapropertypartnerhelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/1500010471361-Philippines-Quarantine-Hotels

Updated: 2021-09-20T06:56:04Z

#
**Overview**
**This article contains important information that applies if your hotel inventory is currently being sold as a Quarantine hotel or ASQ ****accommodation**
#
**Contents**
This article includes
**What is a quarantine hotel?**
**How can customers search for quarantine hotels?**
**What are the current requirements for quarantine bookings?**
**Customer requirements for quarantine bookings**
**Booking flow for quarantine bookings**
**Frequently asked questions**
|



**What is a quarantine hotel?**

Becoming a quarantine hotel means that your property will accept foreign guests and domestic guests who wish to use your hotel to complete the mandatory quarantine requirements as stipulated by the Philippines government.

Please note that Agoda will coordinate with the government of Philippines on specifications and requirements, and information in this article may change or be updated in the future.

Agoda will assist in helping to drive exposure for your hotel to potential quarantine guests.

Quarantine hotels will be displayed via a special link on the Agoda website from May 2021 onwards.


**How can customers search for quarantine hotels?**

Agoda will have a special funnel on our website to display quarantine hotels. This will mean that all hotels currently available as quarantine hotels will be visible to the customer, subject to availability and other Terms & Conditions.

**Please see the link to Philippines Quarantine landing page **here


**What are the current requirements for quarantine bookings?**

Package Details: Customers will be offered a range of packages. The standard requirements are below:

Quarantine packages can be

- 6 nights/7 days stay for inbound travelers coming from abroad
- Shorter duration bookings are possible for customers awaiting results of COVID test before leaving country, and frontline workers who are employed in an area far from their home and stay in quarantine hotels

Only single occupancy is allowed per room, except for the following:

- Families with minor children below 18 years old (if traveling family has two or more adult members, only one adult can stay with the minor)
- Person with Disability (PWD) and his/her companion (only one adult companion is allowed)
- Travelers with medical emergencies (only one adult companion is allowed)

There will be no minimum length of stay setting applied to the BLT page

It may be possible to include additional benefits in your package, such as complimentary welcome minibar (with no alcohol), yoga mats or gym materials, extra meals (e.g. afternoon tea), free consultation with doctors, and other items that will make the quarantine stay more comfortable for your guest.

**Customer requirements for quarantine bookings**

**For Overseas Filipino Workers (“OFWs”):**

- OFWs need to fill out the Electronic Case Information Form (“e-CIF”) at least 3 days prior to arrival in the Philippines.

-
**For land-based OFWs:**Red Cross e-CIF https://c19.redcross.org.ph/arriving-passengers
-
**For sea-based OFWs:**First Aide https://ecif.firstaide.ph/#/
- The e-CIF should be filled out prior to immigration and can be completed 3 days prior to arrival in the Philippines. It is best to complete your e-CIF before arrival.
- To successfully complete the e-CIF, travelers must provide basic personal data, contact details, and travel information
- Travelers are also asked to declare whether they are currently experiencing any COVID-19 symptoms. All the information provided must be accurate and truthful.
- A photograph of the identification document that will be used to travel to the Philippines should be uploaded before submitting the form for review.

- A confirmation email and QR code will be sent to customer email after the 2-step registration process.
- Download the TRAZE app and sign up for an account. This will be used for contact tracing.
- Download, print, and completely fill out the Affidavit of Undertaking.
- Prepare proof of your pre-booked accommodation for at least 6 nights in an accredited quarantine hotel.


**For Non-OFWs and Foreign Nationals:**

- Non-OFWs should fill out an e-CIF at least 3 days prior to arrival in the Philippines.
-
**For Cebu Pacific and other Terminal 3 and Terminal 1 passengers: **ly/ECIFall
-
**For Philippine Airlines Passengers (Terminal 2 passengers): **ly/MNLPALeCIF
- The e-CIF must be filled out prior to immigration and can be completed 3 days prior to arrival in the Philippines. It is best to complete your e-CIF before arrival.
- To successfully complete the e-CIF, travelers must provide basic personal data, contact details, and travel information
- Travelers are also asked to declare whether they are currently experiencing any COVID-19 symptoms. All the information provided must be accurate and truthful.
- A photograph of the identification document that will be used to travel to the Philippines should be uploaded before submitting the form for review.



- A confirmation email and QR code will be sent to customer email after the 2-step registration process.
- Download the TRAZE app and sign up for an account. This will be used for contact tracing.
- Download, print, and completely fill out the Affidavit of Undertaking.
- Prepare proof of your pre-booked accommodation for at least 6 nights in an accredited quarantine hotel.

** **

**For travellers bound to Cebu**, additional registration is required through the online MCIA Passenger Arrival Registration Form. All arriving international flight passengers are REQUIRED to register no earlier than 5 days prior to departure. A Travel Registration Number (TRN) will be generated once registration is complete.

** **

**Booking flow for quarantine bookings**

It is important to note that confirming quarantine bookings requires additional steps. You should have already been briefed on the requirements by the government of Philippines.

Once a booking is received, Agoda requires you to:

- Check all booking details and confirm that you are able to accommodate the guest. Once confirmed, please click the green "Acknowledge this booking" button on the voucher.

Please communicate to customer in advance on any restrictions, such as not being allowed to go to common areas, receiving food deliveries, or visitors, or leaving their rooms.


**Frequently asked questions**

- What happens if a quarantine hotel cannot honour a booking?

Please note that standard A.R penalties will apply regarding bookings that cannot accommodate the customer

The selected responsibilities determine the initial selection of subscription in Subscriptions tab. **Please note that the function to send notifications as per the subscription is still under development. **

# YCS Companion App -- Manage rate and allotment

Source: https://agodapropertypartnerhelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360000345067-YCS-Companion-App-Manage-rate-and-allotment

Updated: 2021-08-27T03:17:29Z

Allotment feature shows allotment status and availability for the property in each day. You can select the date to view allotment, close and open allotment, or adjust the number of allotment, or view and update rate plan from this screen.

Allotment screen shows the list of the property's rooms and its availability. You can tap on the room name to see the room details, change the date, or drill-down the calendar to select the date in the future.

You can manage your allotment by increasing and decreasing the number of the room, or scroll down to the end of the room list to close out all rooms and tap SAVE to save the change. If you want to discard the change you have made, tap Reset. You can also update allotment, close out each room, or update the rate in the room details screen as well.

# How do I view booking transactions?

Source: https://agodapropertypartnerhelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360001072407-How-do-I-view-booking-transactions

Updated: 2021-08-09T12:10:04Z

#
**Overview**

**In this article, we will introduce how to check and view booking transactions in ePass. You may find the tutorial video attached for further reference below.**

**Contents**

This article includes:


**How to search for previous transactions**

**Search on 'All Transactions' page with various criteria**

- Login into
** YCS**
- Go to
** ePass tab**
- Click
**All Transactions**



The All Transactions screen allows you to query your transactions on a number of criteria:

- By booking date
- Check-in date
- Check-out date
- You can also use the checkbox option to include or exclude manual adjustments that have been made

The search can return information from the beginning until present. The default display period is 6 months.




**Filter transaction by payment status**

You can also filter by transaction status:

- Pending departure
- Departed
- Approved
- Disputed
- Paid

**How to view transaction details**

You can click on a transaction in order to see the transaction details at the bottom of the page.

You could see details:

- Guest Name
- Number of Rooms for this booking
- Number of Nights for this booking
- Payment Status
- Payment Reference Number


- Bookings which are visible on All Transactions page will also become visible in 'Current Transactions' page when they become eligible for payment.
- Non-refundable bookings are eligible for payment on the booking date, flexible cancellation bookings will be eligible for payment upon guest departure


**Frequently Asked Questions**


**Why one of booking shows unpaid in All Transaction but I can't find in Current Transaction?**

If you are on UPC on ePass, its likely that you have submitted this transaction but haven't charge the card we provided. You can go to "Remittance" and obtain UPC card to charge. Otherwise you can reach out Agoda Accommodation Support via the Support Widget in the YCS.


**Learn More**

--- FILE: 360001082068-how-do-i-get-paid-via-upc-on-epass.md ---
# How do I get paid via UPC on ePass?

Source: https://agodapropertypartnerhelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360001082068-How-do-I-get-paid-via-UPC-on-ePass

Updated: 2024-08-28T13:38:47Z

##
|


This is a payment method that generates a single-use virtual credit card (UPC) for you to charge for each payment batch consisting of multiple bookings.

Please note that Agoda UPC cards are restricted to be charged via POS terminals under 7011 merchant category code (MCC) only, Lodging - Hotels, Motels, Resorts, Central Reservation Services businesses.

It allows you to create one payment batch for multiple reservations and charge the whole amount from one virtual credit card. Since the card is single-use, the full amount must be charged at once.

If you are on UPC on ePass payment method, you will be able to see the “ePass” menu on YCS. You may visit **How do I log in and begin with ePass?** for details on how you can access the ePass menu.


First time using ePass? Unfamiliar with how it works? Check our interactive tutorial here to familiarize yourself with the tool in a test environment.


**1. **Select **Current Transactions** under the ePass menu.

2. Check the **Booking Transactions** section.

3. Scroll down on the same page to check the **Adjustment Transactions** section.


4. Click **Next** to view a summary of your payment amount.




5. Click **Submit** to be directed to a summary page with your credit card details to be charged.


6. Depending on your role, you will be able to see either masked card details or full card details. Tick the box to acknowledge that you understand the card can be swiped only once and should be fully charged. **Press OK** to complete the payment process.

To improve the security of your operation, the virtual card is only valid for 24 hours. If you do not charge the card within 24 hours, it will become invalid. We suggest you charge the card immediately for the full amount as stated on the summary page. |

7. All payments that have been approved will be removed from the current transactions page. These transactions can be viewed on the **All transactions** page for your future reference.

8. If you forget to record the card details or you would like to review the card and transaction details, you can view it in the Remittances page. Visit **How do I Review Past Payments? **for more information on how to access the remittance page.



We have included a video link below to help you better understand how to charge UPC on ePass |


If your booking has been amended or canceled, Agoda will send you an amendment email (with “AMENDED” appearing in the subject line) with an amended hotel voucher or cancellation email notification including information of the eligible cancellation fee.

This updated amount will be reflected immediately for the relevant booking displayed on the current transactions page.


You may dispute each incorrect transaction on the *YCS > **ePass** > Current Transactions > Booking Transactions*** .** Visit

You will still be eligible to receive the payment for the booking. Just follow the steps in **How do I Reissue UPC in ePass? **to self-issue a replacement card.

There is no limit; however, please make sure you do not exceed your daily credit limit on charged transactions with your acquirer since the card will only be valid for 24 hours once issued.

This error message means that your POS terminal is not under the 7011 merchant category code (MCC). We recommend that you always use a POS terminal with 7011 MCC; you may contact your POS terminal provider for further information on MCC code set-up. If you have difficulty changing your MCC code, please contact Agoda accommodation services via the Need Help button in YCS to report your issue.

Do not worry! There are some conditions that you will need to finalize before contacting Agoda. Please visit **How do I handle partial charge in ePass?** to find out more.

After you finalized the actions needed, you can report this issue to Agoda accommodation support via the Need Help button in YCS. They will be able to help you top up the remaining amount back to *ePass*** > Current Transactions > Adjustment Transactions**.

Please note that due to the complexity of this operation, it might take at least up to 5-7 business days to top up your remaining balance.

It is important to understand that you are required to collect payment within the 150-day deadline. You can contact Agoda accommodation support via the Need Help button in YCS for assistances.


--- FILE: 360001101528-what-can-i-do-if-the-guest-did-not-show-up-no-show.md ---
# What can I do if the guest did not show up (No-Show)?

Source: https://agodapropertypartnerhelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360001101528-What-can-I-do-if-the-guest-did-not-show-up-No-Show

Updated: 2024-08-28T14:01:08Z

##
|


There are several ways to report a No-Show for bookings, depending on the booking payment method. Agoda offers guests 2 payment options: AGODA COLLECT and PROPERTY COLLECT. Guests may select their preferred payment method during the pre-booking process.


An Agoda Collect booking means that Agoda is responsible for collecting the payment from the guest; in another words, it’s prepaid. We will then pay the property using the payment methods implemented for each property.

Upon booking creation, Agoda will send you a confirmation voucher. An Agoda Collect booking voucher will have a **PREPAID** remarks on it, as below:


You may also refer on** YCS Reports > Bookings** and search for the booking ID/list for the payment model as well.

You have 2 ways to notify us of Agoda Collect No-Show bookings: via call or email. Be sure to include the booking ID when sending the request.

A Property Collect booking means that the property should be collecting payment from the guest upon arrival. Agoda will then deduct the booking commission on ePass from the property.

On the booking confirmation voucher, you will see **TO BE PAID BY GUEST** remarks as below:


As with Agoda Collect bookings, you can also refer to ** YCS Reports > Bookings** and search for the booking ID/list for the payment model.


For Property Collect Bookings, you have the option to mark No-Show without contact to Agoda. See the steps below:


The system will automatically compute the No-Show charge for you.

|
|


No-Shows fees will be collected based on the cancellation policy attached to the booking being reported. On every cancellation policy, a no-show policy will also be included. The fees will then be transferred based on your property’s payment method.

Again, you may view the cancellation policy on the **hotel voucher** or ** YCS > Reports > Bookings**.

**On Hotel Voucher:**


**On YCS Reports > Bookings:**


To change your cancellation policy, you can find more details in this article.


Agoda will attempt to charge the guest’s card stored in our system once a No-Show is reported, given that the property has **NOT** viewed the guest’s credit card details.

Agoda will let you know if the charge was or was not made in the cancellation email. You may visit this article for more detailed information.
