--- FILE: 360001113708-introduction-to-property-collect.md ---
# Introduction to Property Collect

Source: https://agodapropertypartnerhelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360001113708-Introduction-to-Property-Collect

Updated: 2024-08-28T13:45:46Z

#
**Overview**
**In this article, we will introduce a new payment model called Property Collect, and outline its benefits to you. **
**Contents**
This article includes:
|


Please also find attached the **“Property Collect -- Accommodation Partner Manual”** that will give you further explanation of our new payment program. |


**What is Property Collect**

Property Collect is Agoda’s pay-at-hotel solution. It allows guests to book Agoda’s inventory with payment due directly to you. Complementing Agoda’s prepaid model, it supplies the high demand of customers looking to pay directly upon check-in.


**Why Property Collect?**

-
**Customers love** the flexibility of paying at the hotel
-
**The pay-at-hotel filter** is Agoda’s most frequently used filter for search results
-
**Many customers only book** if they can have payment flexibility
-
**Get more visibility** in search results and through our affiliates and additional marketing
-
**Get more traction** with long lead time customers
- Properties activating Property Collect get on average,
**5% More Bookings**
-
**Option to drive even more bookings** by offering your pay-at-hotel rates without a credit card required (e.g. for low season)
-
**Easily pay** your commission through Agoda’s self-service payment platform, ePass


**Types of Property Collect**

|
**Types **
|
**Features**
|
|
Property Collect - Credit Card Guarantee
|
Guests will provide credit card detail to secure the booking.
|
|
Property Collect without Credit Card
|
Guest can make a reservation without providing credit card details; visit __here__ for more details
|

** **

**How does it work?**

The booking and payment flow of Property Collect are based on Agoda’s prepaid model with a few exceptions:

- Guests will pay the full booking amount directly to you upon check-in.
- You will be able to collect the full selling amount from the guest booking Property Collect.
- Agoda will deduct the commission from your other prepaid bookings to avoid manual invoicing.


**What are the benefits?**

**Simple to Manage**

- Payment for both Prepaid and Property Collect' reservations can be managed from one platform in ePass. Learn more here.
- We understand it's important to you to be able to track your offset commission amounts. You can print out a booking statement for all payments that include Property Collect commissions.

##
**Easy to Get Paid**


- We don't need you to transfer money to us at the end of every month for Property Collect booking commissions. We will take care of that on our end by offsetting the amount you owe us against what we owe you for prepaid reservations. This way it's always you that gets paid.

**More Customers**

- More variety means more solutions. All guests that are looking to pay at check-in can now find this option, which can increase your booking numbers. Attract a wider customer audience, get bookings with longer lead-times, and possibly improve conversion.


**YCS Features**

In YCS, there are four features which you can use to manage Property Collect bookings specifically (only available for Property Collect with credit card)

|
**Features**
|
**Functions**
|
**When to use**
|
|
**Check if guest credit card is valid**
|
A 0-authorization to check that guest card is valid without blocking money, returns an instant response.
|
As soon as the booking is made, until day of check-in.
|
|
**View guest credit card details**
|
Allows you to view guest credit card details after going through a 2-factor authentication security process.
|
From seven days before check-in day, up to three times.
|
|
**Request new guest credit card**
|
Sends an email and an SMS message to the guest asking them to update their credit card details using a secure portal.
|
From booking day until check-in day.
|
|
**Request to cancel booking**
|
Cancels the booking, waives commission for the booking, and releases the inventory.
|
After you request a new credit card from the guest and guest fails to provide a credit card number.
|


**Frequently Asked Questions**

**How do I distinguish Property Collect bookings and Agoda Collect bookings?**

Booking vouchers that Agoda sends to your property will have information related to any payment needed to be collected directly from the guests. Please visit article **here** for further details on how the Property Collect voucher looks.

**Will I still receive pre-paid bookings after turning on Property Collect?**

Yes, if you turn on Property Collect, you will receive bookings under both Agoda Collect and Property Collect, --which means more guests, and more bookings.

**Will I be sent commission invoices for Property Collect bookings? **

No, our internal offsetting system will automatically deduct commission for Property Collect from your other prepaid bookings. This process replaces manual invoicing for you, however, you will be able to collect a commission statement from ePass on your completed payments.

**How do I turn on/off and change options for Property Collect?**

You may adjust the settings by contacting Agoda Accommodation Support via the Need Help button in the YCS.


**Learn More**


--- FILE: 360001445708-how-do-i-manage-additional-fees.md ---
# How do I manage additional fees?

Source: https://agodapropertypartnerhelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360001445708-How-do-I-manage-additional-fees

Updated: 2021-09-20T06:55:31Z

**Overview **
**In this article, we will outline how to manage surcharges（additional fees).**
**Contents**
This article includes:
|

#

**What are surcharges?**

Surcharges are additional charges to the room rate, therefore should not be taxes.

**Type of surcharge**

YCS supports mandatory (M / Agoda Collect) and excluded (E / Property Collect) surcharge types, the list is predefined and must be selected from the drop-down. It is up to the property owner which one you choose.

-
**Mandatory (Agoda Collect**): Compulsory to booking, must pay addition to the room rate. This type will be included in the final price upon making the booking.
-
**Excluded (Property Collect):** Excluded from the room rate. Customer will get a note on the booking form that the additional fee needs to be paid to the hotel upon check-in.


**Add & Delete surcharges (YCS-Manage-Surcharge)**

- Log into YCS
- Click Manage - Surcharges


- Select the dates
- Select applicable days
- Surcharge drop-down list
- Make your selection
- The selection autofill charge type (Per Guest Per Night/ Per Booking/ Per Adult Per Booking etc.)
- Surcharge type (who is responsible for collecting the fee Agoda or Property)

- Select individual room(s) or All room types
- Select value (Remember it could be either an amount or a percentage %)


- Unwanted surcharges may be deleted by clicking on the bin icon.

__Important information__

- Excluded surcharge (property collect) must be collected by the property.
**Agoda will not take any responsibility in case of missed collection.**
- The surcharge is always based on the same currency as your property setting
- Always check if your surcharge is an amount value or %


**Learn more**

**Overview**
**Your username and password will be automatically created ****when you ****have a property registered with Agoda****.**** ****However, you may want to change your username or password—so i****n this article, we will outline**** how to create ****a ****new username and link ****it ****to your current****ly**** registered property.**

**How to create a new username? **

-
Go to
**Agoda.com** and click on “**Create account**”


-
A pop-up window will appear. Please choose “
**Sign Up via Email**”
-
Make sure you create a new password that’s minimum 8 characters long. We highly recommend using a combination of letters, numbers, symbols, capital letters, and lower-case letters for increased security.



**How can I link ****my ****new username to my current property****?**

Unfortunately, it’s not possible for you to link your new username to your current property in YCS by yourself. However, the **Agoda Accommodation Support** team can help you with this. Simply send your request by clicking the “**Need Help**” button on the bottom-right side of **YCS**.

New username email address
-
Details if any subscription is needed for notification from Agoda

**How to reset password****?**

Agoda has no longer requiring any password to log in to the YCS extranet, you might refer to "How do I login using a PIN Code?" for further steps on login in using the PIN code.

However, when the password is needed from channel manager connection or other setup requirements and if you forget the password, please follow the steps below:


- Find and click on "Forgot Password?"


- Insert the email address and tick on the box "
**I'm not a robot**"
- Click "
**Reset Password**" and you will be informed that a link to reset the password has been sent to your email.



- When you receive the email from Agoda and click on the "
**Reset my password**" button
- Then a pop-up window will appear that will allow you to submit a new password.
- Fill in all the necessary information and click "
**Change Password**"
- Now you should be able to log in with the new password.

--- FILE: 360001709828-what-should-i-do-if-i-can-t-accommodate-a-property-collect-booking.md ---
# What should I do if I can't accommodate a Property Collect booking?

Source: https://agodapropertypartnerhelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360001709828-What-should-I-do-if-I-can-t-accommodate-a-Property-Collect-booking

Updated: 2024-08-28T13:59:47Z

##
|


All Property Collect bookings are confirmed by default. There are, however, scenarios where cancellation is made possible to you based on the guest’s credit card verification status

In case the guest fails to provide a new credit card within 48 hours of the request, or the new credit card provided is also invalid, the action to cancel the booking will be made available. Clicking ‘Request to cancel booking’ (1) will trigger a cancellation email to both you and the guest.

This action is available up to 24 hours before check-in.


The system is going to generate an automatic notification email to the customer when a booking has been canceled.


In case the guest does not show up at your hotels to check in, the action to mark the booking as a no-show will be made available. Clicking ‘Mark booking as no-show’ (2) will cancel the booking and trigger a cancellation email to both you and the guest.

This action will be available from midnight on the check-in day up to 72 hours.

If you failed to report a No-show within 72 hours, the function will be grayed out and you must contact Agoda's Customer Service to report the no-show via **biz@agoda.com****.**


You or Agoda will be responsible for collecting the cancellation fee depending on the actions you have taken on the guest’s credit card verification.

In case you have not used the action to view the guest’s credit card, Agoda will attempt to collect the cancellation fee on your behalf. Canceling the booking or marking it as a no-show will automatically trigger a charge attempt on the credit card, and an email to you with the outcome. If the charge is successful, the amount will be added to ePass.

In case you have used the action to view the guest’s credit card, you will be responsible for collecting any fees upon canceling the booking or marking it as a no-show. You will be able to get in touch with the guest via phone (3) or email (4) through the YCS bookings page



You can cancel a booking if the guest credit card is invalid or if the guest did not provide an alternative payment card. This action is available up to 24 hours before check-in.

No, you cannot reinstate the booking after cancellation.

If you have not viewed the guest’s credit card before canceling, Agoda will attempt to collect any fees on the booking. In case you have used the action to view the card details, you will be responsible for collecting any fees.

No, once a Property Collect booking is canceled, the commission will be removed from ePass.

# MaxAllowedFreeChildren (YCS Setting)

Source: https://agodapropertypartnerhelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360022732854-MaxAllowedFreeChildren-YCS-Setting

Updated: 2020-12-23T07:59:14Z

|


This new setting has been created to address your concerns regarding the limited flexibility of Agoda’s child policy support. This setting allows you to set “free child” limits at the room level.

This new setting ** replaces** the “Free Child Logic” field and both the “Default free children logic” AND “Respect the number of max allowed guests” settings (shown below). This field will be removed from the Property Settings section in favor of the MaxAllowedFreeChildren in an effort to provide greater flexibility to child for your property.

This setting is located in the Room Setup view within the Settings tab.

If you have enabled “Children stay free on existing bedding”, it will have certain YCS settings updated in order to fully enable effective child policies.

**Properties with “Children stay free on existing bedding” enabled and “Respect the number of max allowed guests including free children” selected**:

Updates include:

**Properties with “Children stay free on existing bedding” enabled and “Default free children logic” selected:**

Updates include:

|
|
|
|
1 |
1 |
|
2 |
2 |
|
3 |
2 |
|
4 |
2 |
|
5 |
2 |
|
6+ |
3 |


**Properties with “Children stay free on existing bedding” NOT enabled will now see the new field available with a default setting of Max Allowed Free Children = 0.**


Partners can now update this field within YCS by opening the Room Setup option in the Settings tab. This setting can now be updated for each room.


**1.) Access the Room Setup settings as shown below:**


**2.) Once in Room Setup, update the “Children allowed for free” field to the desired value for each room:**



This new setting is available to all properties, however only properties which currently have “children stay free on existing bedding” enabled will see any noticeable differences as part of the update.

Properties will now be able to indicate exactly how many children can stay for free at the room level. To do this, update the Children allowed for free to the desired value. Note, child guests in excess of this value will be treated as adult guests and subject to standard room occupancy constraints.

This setting will allow properties to customize the maximum number of “free” children per each room – and avoid situations where a guest arrives with too many children.

The following settings will be updated only if you currently have enabled “children stay free on existing bedding”:

Other minor visual / aesthetic changes will be made

**If you do not wish to allow children to stay for free at your property**, please disable the “children stay free on existing bedding” setting.

**If you wish to allow children to stay for free at your property, but want to exclude this benefit from certain rooms**, set the Children allowed for free to “0” for the specified room.

**If you do not wish to allow ANY children to stay at your property**, please update the “Minimum Guest Age” setting to the desired age.

**If you do not wish to allow children to stay in certain rooms**, please update the “Allow children in this room type” setting to “NO”

Please submit your question / concern via the support widget.


--- FILE: 360035872893-proactive-cancellation-fee-waiver-manual.md ---
# Proactive Cancellation Fee Waiver Manual

Source: https://agodapropertypartnerhelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360035872893-Proactive-Cancellation-Fee-Waiver-Manual

Updated: 2021-04-26T04:55:17Z

#
**Overview**
**The Proactive Cancellation Fee Waiver will allow you to pre-select the policies under which your property will waive the cancellation fee (if applicable).**
**Content**
This article includes
|


|
**Not all properties have this access and can only be set by properties in pilot market**
|


**What is the Proactive Cancellation Fee Waiver**

- A simple setting in YCS that properties can use to pre-select the policies and guest circumstances for waiving the cancellation fee (if any).
- Any qualified guest situation that falls within the circumstances selected by the property under the Proactive Cancellation Fee Waiver (PCFW) will automatically be waived through our system.


**Benefits to Property**

- Save time and effort while improving customer satisfaction.
- Substantially decrease the number of calls and emails between properties and guests, making the interaction seamless for you and guests.
- Add flexibility to existing cancellation policies within a limited set of guest circumstances.


**How to Set Up?**

1. From the Settings screen, you can set up your cancellation policy by clicking on “Cancellation Policy Setup”


2. On the Cancellation Fee Waiver Settings, click on “Change Settings”

3. Once you click Change Settings, a pop-up will appear and you will be able to choose your cancellation fee waiver settings. You will be able to select the circumstances under which you will waive the cancellation fee (if any).

4. Toggle **ON **to select the circumstances in which you will waive the fee, and then select the appropriate setting that applies to each circumstance.

5. Toggle **OFF **for the circumstances in which you will not waive the fee

6. The circumstances listed in the tool include:

- Grace period (not applicable for bookings within 48 hours of check-in)
- Medical issue
- Death within family
- Flight canceled
- Flight delayed




**Frequently Asked Questions**

**How do I participate in this program?**

Unfortunately, this function is currently only available in certain markets. Stay tuned for future announcements regarding when it will be released in your market.

**Can I quit the program?**

Yes, you can update this in your YCS settings.

**How will I know when a booking is automatically waived by this tool?**

You will receive the cancellation waiver details, including the Booking ID and waiver reason, by email each time there is a cancellation fee waiver.

**Can I adjust my settings so that last-minute bookings will not be automatically waived?**

Any booking made less than 48 hours before check-in will not be subject to the Proactive Cancellation Fee Waiver Policy’s grace period.


#
**Learn More**


--- FILE: 360037826634-how-do-i-handle-partial-charge-in-epass.md ---
# How do I handle partial charge in ePass?

Source: https://agodapropertypartnerhelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360037826634-How-do-I-handle-partial-charge-in-ePass

Updated: 2024-08-28T13:43:42Z

**In this article, we will outline what to do in the case you make a partial charge. **

This article includes:


The card that has been generated from ePass can be charged ONE TIME only, therefore if you didn't charge the full amount of the balance, a partial charge occurs, you will not be able to charge the card again.


If you encounter the below scenarios, means you partially charged the card.

Submitted transaction as bulk but did not charge or authorize the card with full amount

Submitted transaction as bulk but cannot charge full amount due to POS/EDC machine limitation

The payment batch was not charged the full amount and the amount was returned to the Agoda card (Reverse Authorization)

An error occurred on the POS/EDC machine when charged, causing payment to be stuck; bank returned amount back to Agoda card (Reverse Authorization)

Contact your bank for details of the transaction status to find out if it was successfully processed to be returned or reversed

Status reverse authorization might take **up to 14 days** for the amount to be returned to the card

**After 14 days**, contact our support team via the "Help" button in the extranet to request to top up the total remaining balance to ePass




In cases when a payment batch has been created and the card has been authorized, even if the status has not settled yet, the system automatically considers the booking(s)** paid**. Reverse authorization also will not change the **paid** status

Sorry, the payment batch that has been submitted and created cannot be reverted back or canceled.

Cards that have been generated from ePass can be charged **ONE TIME** only**. **Please always charge** FULL AMOUNT **as stated on the payment batch.

The safeguarding of customers and partners is of paramount importance to Agoda. We have been closely monitoring the Coronavirus updates and latest official travel advice to assess the impact on our customers and partners. At present, travels from, to and within affected regions has been severely impacted and prohibited in certain regions.

Following the latest official travel advice about the Coronavirus, it is unlikely that customers can travel to, from and stay at their accommodations in areas affected around the world. Aside from areas affected by the outbreak, travel bans announced by the government of specific countries or areas are also impacting guests traveling from all around the world.

The purpose of this article is to confirm which areas and period are within Agoda cancellation waivers amid COVID-19. This information is based on locally-sourced intelligence. For official travel guide, we recommend that you consult official government websites

Customers impacted by the travel ban announced by the government (eg: bans on entry, mandatory quarantine on arrival, mandatory quarantine upon return home, or the suspension of on-arrival visas) or any other individual cases where customers are not able to travel (eg: due to quarantine notice/ area hotel shut down due to infection) are also entitled for the cancellation fee waiver.

|
*
Cancellation requests can only be initiated by the customer. In the event of fee waiver, Agoda will fully refund the guest and no payment shall be made to the property. All commission and charges are to be waived. Affected countries/ regions as specified in the above section will be considered as " Travel bans announced by the government on specific areas will also be considered as " If a customer contacts your property directly requesting to cancel, please advise them to initiate the request by going to My Bookings on the Agoda website or contact Agoda’s Customer Experience agents via the contact details on their booking voucher. |

# Long Stay Feature & Promotion

Source: https://agodapropertypartnerhelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360043257454-Long-Stay-Feature-Promotion

Updated: 2021-09-20T06:55:32Z

|


Previously, Agoda only allows customers to book up to 30 days. After conducting some studies, we found that a longer period of stays could create more bookings for properties!

We have added this feature on Agoda to allow our partner's businesses to expand with us. This feature will allow customers to book for up to 90 nights on Agoda for your property.


You will be able to manage the maximum number of nights available for bookings on YCS.


If you have received our email notification on the Long Term Rental promotion, you may click on the **"Create Long Stay Promotion"** and the promotion will be activated for 30% discount for bookings more than 28 days.



If you want to get the maximum advantage over your competition, we recommend setting your **discount at 30% for a minimum stay of 28 nights. **


Absolutely! You can deactivate the promotion anytime you like, simply go to Manage - Promotions.


Setting up the discount rate is totally up to you! We recommend 30% to maximum advantage however you can adjust it anytime.

--- FILE: 360044087734-how-to-issue-tax-invoice.md ---
# How to Issue Tax Invoice?

Source: https://agodapropertypartnerhelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360044087734-How-to-Issue-Tax-Invoice

Updated: 2021-09-20T06:55:29Z

**Overview**
**In this article, you will find out factors about tax invoice, when and how you will issue tax invoice to our mutual guests.**
**Content****s**
This article includes:
|


**Do I need to issue a Tax Invoice to the Guest? **

Properties located in all countries** ****except **the US, Mainland China, and Taiwan are liable to issue a tax invoice to guests. A tax invoice can be issued either on paper or email (or both).


**What information is required when issuing a Tax Invoice to Guests?**

1. Hotel name

2. Guest full name

3. Amount exclusive of GST/VAT

4. GST/ VAT

5. Total Amount: Reference Sell Rate (All-inclusive amount incl. tax & fees)*


** Please refer to the Agoda property voucher for the Reference Sell Rate*



**Sample of a Tax Invoice**

The below sample is for illustrations purpose only, please do not use this template. The exact Tax Invoice template will depend on the VAT/GST laws of the country where your property is located.


#
**Frequently Asked Questions**

**What if my property is tax exempted by the government?**


The law and regulations in different countries and areas may vary. If your property has a special status, kindly reach out to Agoda Accommodation Support via the Support widget in YCS.

**Why Agoda is not issuing the tax invoice?**

__A) Law__

Please note under local law, the property is required to issue local VAT invoices to guests specifying the room rate (Reference Sell Rate)

__B) Legal contract signed by Property and Agoda__

Under our agreement with your hotel, you shall issue a tax invoice to the guest (when they request) specifying the reference sell rate.

__C) Transaction model__

Please note that Agoda collects the money on behalf of you and makes the payment after deducting our commission. This is no different if the guest pays the room rate to you directly and you send the commission amount to Agoda.

__D) Role of Agoda__

Agoda is a “booking facilitation service/ middleman/agent” – legally we do not provide hotel rooms, thus we earn only the commission for our service. Under local law, the provider of accommodation service (hotel rooms) needs to issue a tax invoice to the guest.


**Learn more**


--- FILE: 360044732914-article.md ---
# فيروس كورونا: نهج أجودا المُتبع

Source: https://agodapropertypartnerhelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360044732914

Updated: 2021-02-10T13:49:15Z

*يرجى مراجعة هذه الصفحة بانتظام للحصول على أي تحديثات حول الوضع الراهن *

*هذه المقالة متاحة باللغات التالية:** التايلاندية، الماندرين، اليابانية، الكورية، الإسبانية، الملايو، البهاسا، الإيطالية، الإسبانية، الفرنسية، الألمانية، العربية.*


**نهج أجودا **

تعد حماية عملائنا وشركائنا أولويتنا الأولى في أجودا راقبنا عن كثب تحديثات فيروس كورونا وأحدث نصائح السفر الرسمية لتقييم الآثار المترتبة على عملائنا وشركائنا. في الوقت الحاضر، تأثر السفر من المناطق المتأثرة وإليها وداخلها بشدة، وتم حظر السفر في بعض المناطق.

تباعًا لأحدث نصائح السفر الرسمية حول فيروس كورونا، من غير المحتمل أن يتمكن العملاء من السفر والإقامة في أماكن إقامتهم بالمناطق المتضررة حول العالم. بصرف النظر عن المناطق المتضررة من تفشي الفيروس، فإن حظر السفر الذي أعلنته حكومة دول أو مناطق معينة يؤثر أيضًا على النزلاء القادمين من جميع أنحاء العالم.

يهدف هذا المقال توضيح المناطق والفترات التي تقع في نطاق إعفاءات أجودا من رسوم الإلغاء الجزائية خلال وضع فيروس COVID-19 الحالي. تستند هذه المعلومات إلى مصادر استخبارية محلية. للحصول على دليل السفر الرسمي، نوصيك بمراجعة مواقع الويب الحكومية الرسمية.

|
|



**التأثير العالمي**

**ساموا الأمريكية**

جميع الحجوزات الواردة للعقارات في **ساموا الأمريكية** (باستثناء الرحلات الداخلية والخارجية **)،** بتاريخ تسجيل وصول بين **24 مارس 2020 و30 يونيو 2020 (شامل هذا اليوم)**.

**أنتيغوا وبربودا**

جميع الحجوزات الواردة التي قام بها مسافرون أجانب إلى عقارات في أنتيغوا وبربودا الذين سافروا إلى **الصين وإيطاليا وإيران واليابان وكوريا الجنوبية وسنغافورة** في الأيام الـ 28 السابقة، مع تسجيل الوصول من **12 مارس 2020 حتى 30 أبريل 2020.**

**الأرجنتين - حظر السفر**

جميع الحجوزات الداخلية والخارجية التي تشمل **الأرجنتين**، مع تاريخ تسجيل الوصول بين **1 أبريل 2020 و14 أكتوبر 2020 (شامل هذا اليوم)** .

جميع الحجوزات المحلية التي تتم داخل كرواتيا بتاريخ تسجيل وصول بين **23 مارس 2020 و20 مايو 2020 (شامل هذا اليوم).**

**كوراساو**

جميع الحجوزات الداخلية والخارجية التي تشمل **كوراكاو** (باستثناء الرحلات الداخلية)، مع تاريخ تسجيل الوصول بين **16 مارس 2020 و1 أغسطس 2020 (شامل هذا اليوم).**

**Cuba**

جميع الحجوزات الواردة والصادرة التي تشمل **كوبا** (سواء كانت مكان إقامة العقار أو النزيل) باستثناء الرحلات المحلية، بتاريخ تسجيل وصول بين **23 مارس 2020 و1 يونيو 2020 (شامل هذا اليوم).**

**Cyprus**

جميع الحجوزات الواردة من المسافرين (باستثناء أستراليا، بلجيكا، كندا، الصين، الدنمارك، إستونيا، فنلندا، جورجيا، ألمانيا، اليونان، هونغ كونغ، أيسلندا، أيرلندا، إيطاليا، اليابان، لاتفيا، ليختنشتاين، ليتوانيا، نيوزيلندا، النرويج، بولندا، رواندا، سان مارينو، صربيا، سلوفاكيا، كوريا الجنوبية، السويد، تايلاند، المملكة المتحدة، أوروغواي، جنسيات مدينة الفاتيكان) للعقارات في **قبرص **بتاريخ تسجيل الوصول بين **24 سبتمبر 2020 و19 أكتوبر 2020 (شامل هذا اليوم)**.

** **

**جمهورية التشيك**

جميع الحجوزات الواردة للعقارات في **جمهورية التشيك** (باستثناء أندورا، أستراليا، اليابان، كندا، كوريا الجنوبية، موناكو، نيوزيلندا، سان مارينو، تايلاند، المملكة المتحدة، تونس، الفاتيكان، الرابطة الأوروبية للتجارة الحرة ****، الاتحاد الأوروبي ** * الجنسيات)، بتاريخ تسجيل الوصول بين **16 أكتوبر 2020 و5 نوفمبر 2020 (شامل هذا اليوم)**.

** **

**الدنمارك **

جميع الحجوزات الواردة للعقارات في **الدنمارك** (باستثناء بلغاريا وقبرص وإستونيا وفنلندا وألمانيا واليونان وإيطاليا ولاتفيا وليتوانيا وبولندا والسويد وليختنشتاين والنرويج والفاتيكان وأستراليا وكندا وجورجيا واليابان ونيوزيلندا ، جنسيات كوريا الجنوبية وتايلاند وتونس وأوروغواي**)** مع تاريخ تسجيل الوصول بين **3** أكتوبر **2020 و19 أكتوبر 2020 (شامل هذا اليوم)**.

**Egypt**

جميع الحجوزات الواردة والصادرة التي تشمل **مصر** (باستثناء الرحلات الداخلية) بتاريخ تسجيل وصول بين **17 مارس 2020 و30 يونيو 2020 (شامل هذا اليوم)**.

**El Salvador**

**Estonia**

**الاتحاد الأوروبي - إغلاق الحدود**

جميع الحجوزات الواردة من المسافرين الأجانب إلى العقارات في **الاتحاد الأوروبي*** (باستثناء الرحلات الداخلية والخارجية) بتاريخ تسجيل وصول بين 17 **مارس 2020 و16 إبريل 2020 (شامل هذا اليوم).**

**Finland**

جميع الحجوزات الواردة للعقارات في **فنلندا** (باستثناء النزلاء من إستونيا، ولاتفيا، وليتوانيا، وإيطاليا، وسلوفاكيا، والمجر، وليختنشتاين، والفاتيكان، وجورجيا، ونيوزيلندا، ورواندا، وكوريا الجنوبية، وتايلاند، وتونس، وأوروغواي، والصين**)** بتاريخ تسجيل الوصول بين **16 مارس 2020 و8 سبتمبر 2020 (شامل هذا اليوم)**.

**فرنسا**

**جورجيا**

جميع الرحلات الداخلية داخل **جورجيا** بتاريخ تسجيل وصول بين **21 مارس 2020 و15 يونيو (شامل هذا اليوم)**.

**ألمانيا - الإغلاق التام**

**Iceland**

**Lithuania**

**لوكسمبورج**

**ماكاو - تقييد السفر**

**مالطا**

جميع الحجوزات الواردة والصادرة التي تمت بخصوص موريشيوس (باستثناء الرحلات الداخلية) مع تاريخ تسجيل الوصول بين **20 مارس 2020 و3 ديسمبر 2020 (شامل هذا اليوم هذا اليوم).**

جميع الرحلات الداخلية داخل موريشيوس بتاريخ تسجيل وصول بدءًا من **20 مارس 2020 و14 أكتوبر 2020 (شامل هذا اليوم)**.

**فيتنام - تقييد السفر**

جميع الحجوزات الواردة التي أجراها المسافرون من جنسيات أخرى إلى العقارات في **فيتنام** (باستثناء الرحلات الداخلية والخارجية)، بتاريخ تسجيل وصول بين **3 أبريل 2020 و20 **أكتوبر** 2020 (شامل هذا اليوم).**

جميع الحجوزات المحلية الشاملة للعقارات في **دا نانغ، فيتنام** بتاريخ تسجيل وصول بين **26 يوليو 2020 و8 أغسطس 2020 (شامل هذا اليوم).**

جميع الحجوزات المحلية التي تشمل العقارات في **هوي آن، فيتنام** بتاريخ تسجيل وصول بين **28 يوليو 2020 و11 أغسطس 2020 (شامل هذا اليوم).**


**مناطق أخرى متأثرة بفيروس كورونا**

العملاء المتأثرون بحظر السفر الذي أعلنته الحكومة (على سبيل المثال: الحظر على الدخول، والحجر الإلزامي عند الوصول، والحجر الإلزامي عند العودة إلى الوطن، أو تعليق التأشيرات عند الوصول) أو أي حالات فردية أخرى حيث لا يتمكن العملاء من السفر ( على سبيل المثال: بسبب إشعار الحجر الصحي/إغلاق فندق المنطقة بسبب الإصابة) يحق لهم أيضًا الإلغاء المجاني.


|
*
يجب أن يكون العميل هو من يطلب الإلغاء. في حالة الإعفاء من الرسوم، ستقوم أجودا برد المبلغ بالكامل إلى النزيل، ولن يتم دفع أي مبلغ إلى مكان الإقامة. سيتم إعفاء جميع العمولات والرسوم. البلدان/المناطق المتضررة كما هو محدد في القسم التالي سيتم اعتبارها مناطق تتعرض لـ" سيتم اعتبار حظر السفر الذي أعلنته الحكومة في مناطق معينة بمثابة " إذا اتصل أحد العملاء بعقاراتك طالبًا الإلغاء مباشرة، يرجى توجيهه الخدمة الذاتية عبر الانتقال إلى |

# Coronavirus : l'approche d'Agoda

Source: https://agodapropertypartnerhelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360045244933-Coronavirus-l-approche-d-Agoda

Updated: 2021-09-14T13:10:26Z

*Veuillez consulter régulièrement cette page pour obtenir les dernières mises à jour sur la situation. *

*Veuillez noter que cet article est également disponible dans les langues suivantes : *thaïlandais, mandarin, japonais, coréen, malais, indonésien, italien, espagnol, français, allemand, arabe.


**L'approche d'Agoda **

La protection de nos clients et de nos partenaires est primordiale pour Agoda. Nous avons suivi de près les dernières informations disponibles sur le coronavirus et les conseils officiels destinés aux voyageurs afin d'évaluer les répercutions de la situation sur nos clients et partenaires. Actuellement, les voyages en provenance, à destination et à l'intérieur des régions touchées ont été sévèrement affectés et même interdits dans certaines régions.

Selon les derniers conseils officiels adressés aux voyageurs concernant le coronavirus, il est peu probable que les clients puissent séjourner, se rendre ou revenir de leur lieu d'hébergement dans les régions du monde qui sont touchées. Outre les zones touchées par l'épidémie, les interdictions de voyager annoncées par les gouvernements de certains pays ou de certaines régions ont également des répercussions sur les voyageurs en provenance du monde entier.

Cet article à pour but de confirmer quelles zones et quelles périodes sont concernées par les exemptions d'annulation d'Agoda dans le cadre de la pandémie de la COVID-19. Cette information est basée sur des renseignements obtenus localement. Pour pouvoir accéder à un guide de voyage officiel, nous vous recommandons de consulter les sites web mis en place par les gouvernements.


|
**MISE À JOUR IMPORTANTE :** Un certain temps s'étant écoulé depuis l'apparition de la pandémie, nous présumons que clients et hôtels partenaires sont maintenant parfaitement conscients des risques liés aux voyages. Ainsi, les réservations effectuées à partir du **10 avril 2020** ne donneront droit à aucune exonération de frais. Toute demande d'annulation ou de modification se fera conformément aux conditions de réservation normales.
|


**Impact Global **

**Samoa américaines**

- Toutes les réservations à destination d'établissements situés aux
**Samoa américaines** (à l'exception des déplacements intérieurs et des voyages vers l'étranger) et dont la date d'enregistrement est comprise entre le **24 mars et le 30 juin 2020 (inclus).**

**Antigua-et-Barbuda**

- Toutes les réservations effectuées par des voyageurs ne bénéficiant pas de la citoyenneté d
**'**Antigua-et-Barbuda dans des établissements situés à Antigua-et-Barbuda qui se sont rendus en Chine, en Italie, en Iran, au Japon, en Corée du Sud et à Singapour au cours des 28 derniers jours et une date d'enregistrement comprise entre le **12 mars et le 30 avril 2020**.

**Argentine - Interdiction de voyager**

- Toutes les réservations intérieures et à destination de l'
**Argentine**, dont la date d'enregistrement est comprise entre le **1er avril et le 14 octobre 2020 (inclus).**
- Toutes les réservations intérieures en
**Argentine**, dont la date d'enregistrement est comprise entre le **1er avril et le 20 juin 2020 (inclus).**

**Arménie**

- Toutes les réservations à destination d'établissements situés au
**Arménie **(à exception des voyages intérieurs et à destination de l'étranger), ayant une date d'enregistrement comprise entre **le 3 avril et le 13 juillet 2020 (inclus).**

**Aruba**

- Toutes les réservations à destination d'établissements situés à
**Aruba** (à l'exception des ressortissants du Canada, des États-Unis, des pays de l'UE*, des pays de l'espace Schengen*, des pays des Caraïbes, des déplacements intérieurs et des voyages vers l'étranger) et dont la date d'enregistrement est comprise entre le **16** **mars et le 1er août 2020 (inclus).**
- Pays des Caraïbes* (27 pays) : Anguilla, Antigua-et-Barbuda, Aruba, les Bahamas, la Barbade, Bonaire, Saba et Saint-Eustache, les îles Vierges britanniques, les îles Caïmans, Cuba, Curaçao, la Dominique, la Grenade, la Guadeloupe, la Jamaïque, la Martinique, Montserrat, Porto Rico, Saint-Barthélemy, Saint-Christophe-et-Nevis, Sainte-Lucie, Saint-Martin, Saint-Vincent-et-les-Grenadines, Saint-Martin, Trinidad-et-Tobago, îles Turks et Caicos, îles Vierges américaines

- Toutes les réservations effectuées par des voyageurs en provenance d'un autre pays à destination d'établissements situés en
**Australie** (à l'exception de la Nouvelle-Zélande) et dont la date d'enregistrement est comprise entre le **16 octobre et le 3 décembre 2020 (inclus)**.

**Australie** (à l'exception des déplacements intérieurs) et dont la date d'enregistrement est comprise entre le **25 mars et le 3 décembre 2020 (inclus)**.

- Les réservations à destination d'établissements situés en Tasmanie et dont la date d'enregistrement est comprise entre le
**26 octobre et le 19 novembre 2020 (inclus).**

**8 juillet et le 19 novembre 2020 (inclus).**

**Hongrie** effectuées par des voyageurs en provenance d'Albanie, Belarus, Bosnie-Herzégovine, Kosovo, Moldavie, Monténégro, Macédoine du Nord, Ukraine, tout pays d'Afrique, tout pays d'Amérique du Sud ou tout pays d'Asie (sauf le Japon et la Chine) et dont la date d'enregistrement est comprise entre le **1er septembre et le 3 novembre 2020 (inclus)**.

**Islande**

- Toutes les réservations effectuées par des étrangers (à l'exception des ressortissants d'Algérie, Andorre, Australie, Canada, Géorgie, Japon, Monténégro, Monaco, Maroc, Nouvelle-Zélande, Rwanda, Serbie, Corée du Sud, Thaïlande, Tunisie, Saint-Marin, Royaume-Uni, Uruguay, Vatican, ni ceux des pays de l'UE* ou de l'AELE*), avec une date d'enregistrement comprise entre le
**15 juillet 2020 et le 14 octobre 2020 (inclus)**.

**Inde**

- Toutes les réservations à destination d'établissements situés en Inde avec enregistrement entre le
**13 mars et le 14 septembre 2020 (inclus)**.

- Tous les voyages intérieurs en Inde avec une date d'enregistrement comprise entre le
** 25 mars et le 15 juin 2020 (inclus).**

**Indonésie **

- Toutes les réservations à destination d'établissements situés en
**Indonésie** et dont la date d'enregistrement est comprise entre le **2** **avril et le 31 octobre 2020 (inclus).**

**Ireland** et dont la date d'enregistrement est comprise entre le** 24 mars et le 29 juin 2020 (inclus)**.

**Île de Man** (à l'exception des voyages sortants) avec une date d'enregistrement entre le **26 mars 2020 et le 31 juillet 2020 (inclus)**.

**Italie **seront soumises à la décision de l'établissement.

**Jamaïque** (qu'il s'agisse de l'établissement ou du lieu de résidence des hôtes, à l'exception des déplacements intérieurs) et dont la date d'enregistrement est comprise entre le **31 mars et le 15 juin 2020 (inclus)**.

**Taïwan - Restriction de voyage**

- Toutes les réservations à destination d'établissements situés à
**Taïwan** (à l'exception des déplacements intérieurs et des voyages vers l'étranger) et dont la date d'enregistrement est comprise entre le **19** **mars et le 30 juin 2020 (inclus).**

**Thaïlande - Fermeture des frontières**

- Toutes les réservations à destination d'établissements situés à
**Thaïlande** et dont la date d'enregistrement est comprise entre le **14** **mars et le 30 juin 2020 (inclus).**


**Tunisie**

- Tous les voyages à l'arrivée ou au départ concernant la Tunisie (qu'il s'agisse d'un établissement ou d'une localité d'accueil à l'exception des déplacements intérieurs), avec une date d'enregistrement comprise entre le
**24 mars et le 26 juin 2020 (inclus)**.
- Tous les déplacements intérieurs à destination d'établissements situés en
**Tunisie** et dont la date d'enregistrement est comprise entre le **24** **mars et le 4 juin 2020 (inclus).**

**Turquie - Interdiction de voyager**

- Tous les voyages à l'arrivée concernant la
**Turquie** (à l'exception des voyages intérieurs et vers l'étranger), avec une date d'enregistrement comprise entre le **14 mars et le 26 mai 2020 (inclus)**.
- Toutes les réservations nationales dans des établissements situés en
**Turquie** et dont la date d'enregistrement est comprise entre le **4 avril et le 26 mai 2020 (inclus).**

**Îles Turques-et-Caïques**

- Toutes les réservations à destination d'établissements situés dans les
**Îles Turques-et-Caïques** (à l'exception des voyages domestiques), dont la date d'enregistrement est comprise entre le **24 mars et le 30 juin 2020 (inclus).**

**Émirats Arabes Unis (UAE) - Suspension des visas**

- Tous les voyages à destination et au départ pour des établissements situés aux
**Émirats arabes unis** (qu'il s'agisse de l'établissement ou du lieu de résidence des hôtes) et dont la date d'enregistrement est comprise entre le **17 mars et le 7 juillet 2020 (inclus)**.

**Ukraine - Fermeture des frontières**

- Toutes les réservations effectuées par des voyageurs n'ayant pas la nationalité ukrainienne dans des établissements situés en
**Ukraine **(à l'exception des voyages intérieurs) et dont la date d'enregistrement est comprise entre le** 16 mars et le 22 juin 2020 (inclus)**.

- Toutes les réservations nationales à destination d'établissements situés à
**Hoi An **au** Vietnam** et dont la date d'enregistrement est comprise entre le **28 juillet et le 11 août 2020 (inclus).**

**Autres régions affectées par le coronavirus**

- Les clients touchés par l'interdiction de voyager annoncée par le gouvernement (par exemple : interdiction d'entrée, quarantaine obligatoire à l'arrivée, quarantaine obligatoire au retour, ou suspension des visas à l'arrivée) ou tout autre cas individuel dans lesquels les clients ne peuvent pas voyager (par exemple : en raison d'un avis de quarantaine / fermeture d'un hôtel de la région en raison d'une infection) ont également droit à l'exonération des frais d'annulation.


-
***Pays de l'espace Schengen** : Allemagne, Autriche, Belgique, Danemark, Espagne, Estonie, Finlande, France, Grèce, Hongrie, Islande, Italie, Lettonie, Liechtenstein, Lituanie, Luxembourg, Malte, Norvège, Pays-Bas, Pologne, Portugal, République tchèque, Slovaquie, Slovénie, Suède, Suisse.
-
**Pays de l'Espace économique européen (EEE)** : **Allemagne, Autriche, Belgique, Bulgarie, Croatie, République de Chypre, Danemark, Espagne, Estonie, Finlande, France, Grèce, Hongrie, Irlande, Islande, Italie, Lettonie, Liechtenstein, Lituanie, Luxembourg, Malte, Norvège, Pays-Bas, Pologne, Portugal, République tchèque, Roumanie, Slovaquie, Slovénie, Suède.
-
**Union européenne (UE)** :** Autriche, Belgique, Bulgarie, Croatie, République de Chypre, République tchèque, Danemark, Estonie, Finlande, France, Allemagne, Grèce, Hongrie, Irlande, Italie, Lettonie, Lituanie, Luxembourg, Malte, Pays-Bas, Pologne, Portugal, Roumanie, Slovaquie, Slovénie, Espagne, Suède
-
**Association européenne de libre-échange (AELE)** :** Islande, Liechtenstein, Norvège, Suisse
- Les demandes d'annulation ne peuvent être initiées que par le client.
- En cas d'exonération des frais, Agoda remboursera intégralement l'invité et aucun paiement ne sera effectué à l'établissement. Toutes les commissions et frais doivent être supprimés.
- Les pays/régions touchés, tels que spécifiés dans la section ci-dessus, seront considérés comme entrant dans la catégorie des cas de
**force majeure** et les frais d'annulation seront supprimés.
- Les interdictions de voyager annoncées par le gouvernement dans certaines régions seront considérées comme des cas de
**force majeure** et les frais de réservation seront supprimés.
- Si un client venait à contacter directement votre établissement pour demander une annulation, veuillez lui conseiller d'initier une demande en allant sur Mes réservations sur le site web d'Agoda ou de contacter les agents de l'équipe de Satisfaction Clientèle d'Agoda via les coordonnées figurant sur leur bon de réservation.

# Coronavirus: Die Vorgehensweise von Agoda

Source: https://agodapropertypartnerhelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360045245173-Coronavirus-Die-Vorgehensweise-von-Agoda

Updated: 2021-08-19T08:28:02Z

*Bitte prüfen Sie diese Seite regelmäßig auf Aktualisierungen zum Thema. *

Dieser Artikel ist auch in den folgenden Sprachen verfügbar:Thai, Mandarin, JPN, KR, Malaiisch, Bahasa, Italienisch, Spanisch, Französisch, Englisch, Arabisch.


**Vorgehensweise von Agoda **

Der Schutz von Kunden und Partnern ist für Agoda von höchster Wichtigkeit. Wir beobachten die Coronavirus-Updates und die neuesten offiziellen Reisehinweise genau, um die Auswirkungen auf unsere Kunden und Partner zu bewerten. Gegenwärtig sind Reisen aus und zu betroffenen Regionen sowie innerhalb betroffener Regionen stark beeinträchtigt und in bestimmten Regionen ganz verboten.

Laut den neuesten offiziellen Reisehinweisen zum Coronavirus ist es weltweit unwahrscheinlich, dass Kunden zu Unterkünften in den betroffenen Gebieten reisen bzw. von dort ausreisen können. Abgesehen von den vom Ausbruch direkt betroffenen Gebieten wirken sich die von der Regierung bestimmter Länder oder Regionen angekündigten Reiseverbote auch auf Gäste aus der ganzen Welt aus.

Der Zweck dieses Artikels besteht darin, Sie darüber zu informieren, für welchen Zeitraum und für welche Gebiete Agoda aufgrund von COVID-19 auf die Stornierungsgebühr verzichtet. Die hier zusammengestellten Daten stammen aus lokalen Quellen. Für offizielle Reisehinweise empfehlen wir Ihnen, die offiziellen Webseiten der jeweiligen Regierung aufzusuchen.

|
|

# Pendekatan Agoda Terkait Wabah Virus Corona (COVID-19)

Source: https://agodapropertypartnerhelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360045245293-Pendekatan-Agoda-Terkait-Wabah-Virus-Corona-COVID-19

Updated: 2021-02-16T05:59:24Z

*Silakan periksa halaman ini secara berkala untuk informasi terbaru terkait isu ini. *

*Perlu diketahui bahwa artikel ini juga tersedia dalam bahasa-bahasa berikut; *Bahasa Thailand, Bahasa Mandarin, Bahasa Jepang, Bahasa Korea, Bahasa Melayu, Bahasa Inggris, Bahasa Italia, Bahasa Spanyol, Bahasa Perancis, Bahasa Jerman, Bahasa Arab.


**Pendekatan Agoda **

Menjaga keselamatan pelanggan dan partner merupakan hal yang sangat penting bagi Agoda. Kami memantau dengan saksama kabar terbaru mengenai Virus Corona dan saran perjalanan resmi terbaru untuk menilai dampak pada pelanggan dan partner kami. Saat ini, perjalanan dari, ke, dan dalam wilayah terdampak sudah sangat terpengaruh dan bahkan dilarang di beberapa wilayah tertentu.

Mengikuti saran perjalanan resmi terbaru terkait Virus Corona, pelanggan tidak dimungkinkan untuk melakukan perjalanan ke, dari dan menginap di akomodasi yang berada di wilayah terdampak di seluruh dunia. Selain wilayah yang terkena dampak wabah, larangan perjalanan yang diumumkan oleh pemerintah negara atau wilayah tertentu juga berdampak pada tamu yang melakukan perjalanan dari seluruh dunia.

Tujuan artikel ini adalah untuk mengonfirmasi area dan periode yang termasuk dalam pembebasan biaya pembatalan Agoda di tengah COVID-19. Informasi berikut berdasarkan intelijen yang mengandalkan sumber lokal. Untuk panduan perjalanan resmi, kami menyarankan agar Anda memeriksa situs resmi pemerintah.

**INFORMASI PENTING TERBARU:** Karena sudah cukup lama sejak wabah pandemi, kami harap pelanggan dan partner hotel mengetahui dengan baik risiko perjalanan saat ini. Dengan demikian, pesanan yang dibuat mulai** 10 April 2020** dan seterusnya tidak akan mendapatkan pembebasan biaya. Semua pembatalan atau permintaan perubahan akan mengikuti kebijakan pemesanan standar. |


**Dampak Global**

**Samoa Amerika**

- Semua reservasi masuk yang dibuat untuk properti di
**Samoa Amerika** (kecuali perjalanan domestik dan keluar negeri), dengan tanggal check-in mulai **24 Maret 2020 hingga 30 Juni 2020.**

**Antigua dan Barbuda**

- Semua reservasi masuk yang dibuat oleh wisatawan berkewarganegaraan asing (orang asing) untuk properti di Antigua dan Barbuda yang pernah melakukan perjalanan ke
**Cina, Italia, Iran, Jepang, Korea Selatan dan Singapura** dalam waktu 28 hari terakhir, dengan tanggal check-in mulai **12 Maret 2020 hingga 30 April 2020.**

**Argentina - Larangan Perjalanan**

- Semua reservasi masuk dan keluar negeri yang melibatkan
**Argentina**, dengan tanggal check-in mulai **1 April 2020 hingga 14 Oktober 2020.**
- Semua reservasi domestik yang melibatkan
**Argentina**, dengan tanggal check-in mulai **1 April 2020 hingga 20 Juni 2020.**

**Armenia**

- Semua reservasi masuk yang dibuat untuk properti di
**Armenia** (kecuali perjalanan domestik), dengan tanggal check-in mulai **3 April 2020 hingga 13 Juli 2020.**

**Aruba**

- Semua reservasi masuk yang dibuat untuk properti di
**Aruba** (kecuali warga negara Kanada, Amerika Serikat, negara-negara UE*, negara-negara Schengen*, negara-negara Karibia, dan perjalanan domestik), dengan tanggal check-in mulai **16 Maret 2020 hingga 1 Agustus 2020.**
- Negara-negara Karibia* (27): Anguilla, Antigua dan Barbuda, Aruba, Bahama, Barbados, Bonaire, Saba dan Sint Eustatius, Kepulauan Virgin Britania Raya, Kepulauan Cayman, Kuba, Curacao, Dominika, Grenada, Guadeloupe, Jamaika, Martinique, Monserrat, Puerto Riko, Saint Barthelemy, Saint Kitts dan Nevis, Saint Lucia, Saint Martin, Saint Vincent dan Grenadines, Sint Maarten, Trinidad dan Tobago, Kepulauan Turks dan Caicos, Kepulauan Virgin

**Australia - Pembatasan Perjalanan**

- Semua reservasi masuk yang dibuat oleh tamu dari Selandia Baru untuk properti di Australia (kecuali perjalanan domestik), dengan tanggal check-in mulai
**25 Maret 2020 hingga 29 Oktober 2020.**
- Semua reservasi masuk yang dibuat oleh tamu dari negara lain untuk properti di Australia (kecuali Selandia Baru), dengan tanggal check-in mulai
**16 Oktober 2020 hingga 3 Desember 2020.**
- Semua reservasi keluar negeri yang dibuat oleh tamu dari Australia (kecuali perjalanan domestik), dengan tanggal check-in mulai
**25 Maret 2020 hingga 3 Desember 2020.**
- Reservasi domestik yang dibuat untuk properti di wilayah yang disebutkan di bawah:
- Perjalanan masuk ke Tasmania dengan tanggal check-in mulai
**26 Oktober 2020 hingga 19 November 2020.**
- Perjalanan masuk dan keluar yang melibatkan Victoria dengan kode pos yang disebutkan berikut: 3012, 3021, 3032, 3036, 3038, 3042, 3046, 3047, 3055, 3060, 3063, 3064, 3031, 3051
- Perjalanan masuk dan keluar yang melibatkan Kota Melbourne dengan tanggal check-in mulai
**19 Agustus 2020 hingga 26 Oktober 2020.**
- Perjalanan masuk ke New South Wales untuk tamu dari Victoria dengan tanggal check-in mulai
**8 Juli 2020 hingga 19 November 2020.**
- Perjalanan masuk ke Wilayah Ibukota Australia untuk tamu dari Victoria dengan tanggal check-in mulai
**8 Juli 2020 hingga 19 November 2020.**
- Perjalanan masuk ke Australia Selatan untuk tamu dari Victoria dengan tanggal check-in mulai
**8 Juli 2020 hingga 19 November 2020.**
- Semua perjalanan masuk ke Wilayah Utara untuk tamu dengan tanggal check-in mulai
**8 Juli 2020 hingga 19 November 2020.**
- Semua perjalanan masuk ke Australia Barat untuk tamu dengan tanggal check-in mulai
**8 Juli 2020 hingga 14 November 2020.**
**Semu perjalanan masuk ke Queensland untuk tamu yang pernah berkunjung ke wilayah yang termasuk dalam daftar Wilayah dengan Risiko Tinggi Queensland dengan tanggal check-in mulai 8 Juli 2020 hingga 19 November 2020. **


**Austria - Lockdown**

- Semua reservasi masuk yang dibuat untuk properti di
**Austria** (kecuali wisatawan dari negara-negara berikut: Andorra, Kepulauan Faroe, Monako, San Marino, Britania Raya, Vatikan, negara-negara UE* atau negara-negara Schengen*), dengan tanggal check-in mulai **14 Juli 2020 hingga 5 November 2020.**

**Azerbaijan**

**Bahama - Pembatasan Perjalanan**

**Wilayah Lain yang Terdampak COVID-19**

- Pelanggan yang terdampak oleh larangan perjalanan yang diumumkan oleh pemerintah (contoh: larangan masuk, karantina wajib saat kedatangan, karantina wajib saat kembali ke rumah, atau penangguhan Visa on Arrival) atau kasus lain di mana pelanggan tidak dapat melakukan perjalanan (contoh: karena pemberitahuan karantina/penutupan area hotel karena infeksi) juga termasuk dalam pengabaian biaya pembatalan.

-
***Negara-negara wilayah Schengen**: Austria, Belgia, Republik Ceko, Denmark, Estonia, Finlandia, Perancis, Jerman, Yunani, Hongaria, Islandia, Italia, Latvia, Liechtenstein, Lithuania, Luksemburg, Malta, Belanda, Norwegia, Polandia, Portugal, Slowakia, Slovenia, Spanyol, Swedia, Swiss.
-
**Negara-Negara Wilayah Ekonomi Eropa (EEA)*:** Austria, Belgia, Bulgaria, Kroasia, Republik Siprus, Republik Ceko, Denmark, Estonia, Finlandia, Prancis, Jerman, Yunani, Hongaria, Islandia, Irlandia, Italia, Latvia, Liechtenstein, Lithuania, Luksemburg, Malta, Belanda, Norwegia, Polandia, Portugal, Rumania, Slowakia, Slovenia, Spanyol, Swedia.
-
**Uni Eropa (UE)**:** Austria, Belgia, Bulgaria, Kroasia, Republik Siprus, Republik Ceko, Denmark, Estonia, Finlandia, Prancis, Jerman, Yunani, Hongaria, Irlandia, Italia, Latvia, Lithuania, Luksemburg, Malta, Belanda, Polandia, Portugal, Rumania, Slowakia, Slovenia, Spanyol, Swedia
-
**Asosiasi Perdagangan Bebas Eropa (European Free Trade Association/EFTA)**:** Islandia, Liechtenstein, Norwegia, Swiss
- Permintaan pembatalan hanya dapat dilakukan oleh pelanggan.
- Dalam hal pengabaian biaya, Agoda akan memberikan refund penuh kepada tamu dan tidak ada biaya yang perlu dibayarkan kepada properti. Semua komisi dan biaya harus dibebaskan.
- Negara/wilayah terdampak sesuai yang disebutkan di atas dianggap sebagai peristiwa "
**force majeure**" dan akan dibebaskan biaya pembatalan.
- Larangan perjalanan yang diumumkan oleh pemerintah pada wilayah tertentu akan dianggap sebagai peristiwa
**"force majeure" **dan biaya pemesanan akan dibebaskan.
- Jika pelanggan menghubungi properti Anda secara langsung untuk pembatalan, mohon beri tahukan kepada mereka untuk mengajukan permintaan melalui Pesanan Saya di situs web Agoda atau dengan menghubungi agen Layanan Pelanggan Agoda melalui informasi kontak pada bukti pemesanan mereka.
|

**Anda punya pertanyaan? Hubungi kami melalui langkah-langkah ****di sini****.**

# Coronavirus: el enfoque de Agoda

Source: https://agodapropertypartnerhelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360045245793-Coronavirus-el-enfoque-de-Agoda

Updated: 2020-11-16T07:02:39Z

*Por favor, consulte esta página con regularidad para leer actualizaciones sobre este tema. *

*Tenga en cuenta que este artículo también está disponible en los siguientes idiomas:* tailandés, mandarín, japonés, coreano, malayo, indonesio, inglés, francés, alemán y árabe.


**Enfoque de Agoda **

La protección de los clientes y socios es de suma importancia para Agoda. Hemos estado monitorizando de cerca las actualizaciones de coronavirus y los últimos consejos oficiales de viaje para evaluar el impacto en nuestros clientes y socios. En la actualidad, los viajes desde, hacia y dentro de las regiones afectadas se han visto gravemente afectados y prohibidos en ciertas regiones.

Siguiendo los últimos consejos oficiales de viaje sobre el coronavirus, es poco probable que los clientes puedan viajar a, desde y permanecer en sus alojamientos en áreas afectadas en todo el mundo. Aparte de las zonas afectadas por el brote, las prohibiciones de viaje anunciadas por el gobierno de determinados países o áreas también están afectando a los huéspedes que viajan desde todo el mundo.

El propósito de este artículo es confirmar qué áreas y períodos están dentro de las exenciones de cancelación de Agoda a causa del COVID-19. Esta información se basa en la inteligencia de origen local. Para la guía de viaje oficial, le recomendamos que consulte los sitios web oficiales del gobierno.

|
**ACTUALIZACIÓN IMPORTANTE:** Dado que ha transcurrido algún tiempo desde el brote de la pandemia, esperamos que los clientes y socios hoteleros sean conscientes del riesgo de viajar ahora. Por lo tanto, las reservas realizadas a partir del **10 de abril de 2020** en adelante no tendrán derecho a exención de pago. Toda solicitud de cancelación o modificación seguirá la política de reserva estándar.
|


**Impacto global**

**Samoa Americana**

- Todas las reservas de entrada realizadas para alojamientos en
**Samoa Americana** (excepto viajes nacionales y de salida), con fecha de check-in entre el **24 de marzo de 2020 y el 30 de junio de 2020** **(incluidas)**.

**Antigua y Barbuda**

- Todas las reservas entrantes realizadas por viajeros de otras nacionalidades (extranjeros) a alojamientos en Antigua y Barbuda que hayan viajado a China, Italia, Irán, Japón, Corea del Sur y Singapur en los 28 días anteriores, con fecha de check-in del
**12 de marzo de 2020 al 30 de abril de 2020**.

**Argentina - Prohibición de viajes**

- Todas las reservas de entrada realizadas para alojamientos en
**Argentina**, con fecha de check-in entre el **1 de abril de 2020 y el 31 de agosto de 2020** **(incluidas)**.
- Todas las reservas nacionales realizadas en
**Argentina,** con fecha de check-in entre el **1 de agosto de 2020** y **el 20 de junio de 2020** **(incluidas)**.
- Todas las reservas salientes desde
**Argentina**, con fecha de check-in entre el **1 de abril de 2020** y **el 1 de septiembre de 2020** **(incluidas)**.

**Armenia**

- Todas las reservas entrantes realizadas por viajeros de otras nacionalidades (extranjeros) a alojamientos en
**Armenia**(excepto viajes nacionales y salientes) con una fecha de check-in entre el **3 de abril de 2020 y el 13 de junio de 2020** **(incluidas).**

**Aruba**

- Todas las reservas de entrada realizadas para alojamientos en
**Aruba** (excepto viajes nacionales y viajeros de Canadá Estados Unidos, UE, Países del área de Schengen, Países del Caribe), con fecha de check-in entre el** 16 de marzo de 2020 y el 1 de agosto de 2020** **(incluidas).**

**Australia - Restricción de viajes**

- Todas las reservas entrantes y salientes realizadas a propiedades en Australia (excepción de viajes nacionales), con una fecha de llegada entre el 16 de marzo de 2020 y el 4 de septiembre de 2020 (incluidas).

**16 de marzo de 2020 y el 30 de september de 2020** **(incluidas)**.

- Países Schengen *: Austria, Bélgica, República Checa, Dinamarca, Estonia, Finlandia, Francia, Alemania, Grecia, Hungría, Islandia, Italia, Letonia, Liechtenstein, Lituania, Luxemburgo, Malta, Países Bajos, Noruega, Polonia, Portugal, Eslovaquia, Eslovenia, España, Suecia, Suiza.
- Espacio Económico Europeo (EEE) ** Países: Austria, Bélgica, Bulgaria, Croacia, República de Chipre, República Checa, Dinamarca, Estonia, Finlandia, Francia, Alemania, Grecia, Hungría, Islandia, Irlanda, Italia, Letonia, Liechtenstein, Lituania, Luxemburgo, Malta, Países Bajos, Noruega, Polonia, Portugal, Rumania, Eslovaquia, Eslovenia, España, Suecia.

- Las solicitudes de cancelación solo pueden ser iniciadas por el cliente.
- En caso de exención de tarifas, Agoda reembolsará por completo al huésped y no se realizará ningún pago a la propiedad. No se aplicarán todas las comisiones y cargos.
- Los países / regiones afectados como se especifica en la sección anterior se considerarán como "fuerza mayor" y no se aplicarán las tarifas de cancelación.
- Las prohibiciones de viaje anunciadas por el gobierno en áreas específicas también se considerarán como "fuerza mayor" y no se aplicarán las tarifas de cancelación.
- Si un cliente se comunica directamente con su establecimiento para solicitar la cancelación, avísele que inicie la solicitud en Mis reservas en el sitio web de Agoda o comuníquese con los agentes de experiencia del cliente de Agoda a través de los datos de contacto que figuran en su vale de reserva.

**Otras áreas afectadas por coronavirus**

- Los clientes afectados por la prohibición de viaje anunciada por el gobierno (por ejemplo: prohibiciones de entrada, cuarentena obligatoria a la llegada, cuarentena obligatoria a su regreso a casa, o la suspensión de visados a la llegada) o cualquier otro caso individual en el que los clientes no puedan viajar (por ejemplo: debido a aviso de cuarentena / hotel de la zona cerrada debido a la infección) también tienen derecho a la exención de la tasa de cancelación.

-
*Países del área Schengen: Austria, Bélgica, Chequia, Dinamarca, Estonia, Finlandia, Francia, Alemania, Grecia, Hungría, Islandia, Italia, Letonia, Liechtenstein, Lituania, Luxemburgo, Malta, Países Bajos, Noruega, Polonia, Portugal, Eslovaquia, Eslovenia, España, Suecia, Suiza.
-
**Países del Espacio Económico Europeo (EEE)****: Austria, Bélgica, Chequia, Dinamarca, Estonia, Finlandia, Francia, Alemania, Grecia, Hungría, Islandia, Irlanda, Italia, Letonia, Liechtenstein, Lituania, Luxemburgo, Malta, Países Bajos, Noruega, Polonia, Portugal, Rumanía, Eslovaquia, Eslovenia, España y Suecia.
- Las solicitudes de cancelación solo pueden ser iniciadas por el cliente.
- En caso de exención de cargos, Agoda reembolsará totalmente al huésped y no se realizará ningún pago al alojamiento. Todos los cargos y comisiones se reembolsarán.
- Los países/regiones afectados, tal como se especifica en la sección anterior, se considerarán de "fuerza mayor" y se eximirán las tasas de cancelación.
- Las prohibiciones de viaje anunciadas por el gobierno en áreas específicas se considerarán como "
**fuerza mayor**" y se eximirán las tarifas de las reservas.
- Si un cliente se pone en contacto directamente con su alojamiento solicitando la cancelación, aconséjele iniciar la solicitud accediendo a Mis Reservas en la página web de Agoda o contactar con el Equipo de Atención al Cliente a través de la información de contacto que aparece en la confirmación de reserva.

# Pendekatan Agoda Tentang Wabak Coronavirus (COVID-19)

Source: https://agodapropertypartnerhelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360045246033-Pendekatan-Agoda-Tentang-Wabak-Coronavirus-COVID-19

Updated: 2021-01-17T07:02:33Z

*Sila semak halaman ini secara kerap untuk sebarang perkembangan terkini. *

**Harap maklum artikel ini juga tersedia dalam bahasa berikut**; Thai, Mandarin, JPN, KR, Bahasa Melayu, Bahasa Indonesia, Itali, Sepanyol, Perancis, Jerman, Arab.


**Pendekatan Agoda **

Menjaga keselamatan pelanggan dan rakan kerjasama kami adalah keutamaan Agoda. Kami telah mengawasi dengan teliti perkembangan Coronavirus dan nasihat perjalanan rasmi terkini untuk menilai kesan terhadap pelanggan dan rakan kerjasama kami. Pada masa ini, perjalanan dari, ke dan dalam kawasan yang terkesan telah terjejas teruk dan dilarang di wilayah tertentu.

Berikutan nasihat perjalanan rasmi terbaru tentang Coronavirus, adalah mustahil pelanggan dapat melakukan perjalanan ke, dari dan menginap di tempat penginapan mereka di kawasan yang terjejas di seluruh dunia. Selain daripada kawasan yang terjejas oleh wabak ini, larangan perjalanan yang diumumkan oleh kerajaan negara atau wilayah tertentu juga memberi kesan kepada pelanggan yang melakukan perjalanan dari seluruh dunia.

Tujuan artikel ini adalah untuk mengesahkan kawasan mana dan tempoh yang berada dalam pengecualian pembatalan Agoda semasa wabak COVID-19. Maklumat ini berdasarkan maklumat sumber tempatan. Untuk panduan perjalanan rasmi, kami mengesyorkan agar anda melihat laman sesawang rasmi kerajaan.

|
**PENGUMUMAN PENTING:** Oleh kerana sudah beberapa minggu sejak wabak covid-19 meletus, kami menjangkakan pelanggan dan rakan kerjasama hotel menyedari risiko untuk membuat perjalanan pada masa sekarang. Oleh itu, tempahan yang dibuat dari **10 April 2020** dan seterusnya tidak akan dikecualikan caj. Semua permintaan pembatalan atau pindaan akan mengikut polisi tempahan standard.
|

**Kawasan Lain yang Terjejas akibat Coronavirus**

- Pelanggan yang terjejas akibat larangan perjalanan yang diumumkan oleh kerajaan (misalnya: larangan masuk, kuarantin mandatori semasa ketibaan, kuarantin mandatori semasa pulang ke rumah, atau penggantungan visa ketibaan) atau mana-mana kes individu lain iaitu pelanggan tidak dapat melakukan perjalanan (contohnya: disebabkan oleh notis kuarantin/ kawasan hotel yang ditutup kerana jangkitan) juga berhak untuk pengecualian caj pembatalan.


- *
**Negara **Schengen: Austria, Belgium, Republik Czech, Denmark, Estonia, Finland, Perancis, Jerman, Greece, Hungary, Iceland, Itali, Latvia, Liechtenstein, Lithuania, Luxembourg, Malta, Belanda, Norway, Poland, Portugal, Slovakia, Slovenia, Sepanyol, Sweden, Switzerland.
- **
**Negara Kawasan Ekonomi Eropah (EEA)**: Austria, Belgium, Bulgaria, Croatia, Republik Cyprus, Republic Czech, Denmark, Estonia, Finland, Perancis, Jerman, Greece, Hungary, Iceland, Ireland, Itali, Latvia, Liechtenstein, Lithuania, Luxembourg, Malta, Belanda, Norway, Poland, Portugal, Romania, Slovakia, Slovenia, Sepanyol, Sweden.
-
**Kesatuan Eropah (EU)**:** Austria, Belgium, Bulgaria, Croatia, Republik Cyprus, Republik Czech, Denmark, Estonia, Finland, Perancis, Jerman, Greece, Hungary, Ireland, Itali, Latvia, Lithuania, Luxembourg, Malta, Belanda, Poland, Portugal, Romania, Slovakia, Slovenia, Spain, Sweden
-
**Persatuan Perdagangan Bebas Eropah (EFTA)**:** Iceland, Liechtenstein, Norway, Switzerland
- Permintaan pembatalan hanya boleh dimulakan oleh pelanggan.
- Sekiranya terdapat pengecualian bayaran, Agoda akan membayar balik sepenuhnya dan tiada bayaran akan dibuat kepada pihak penginapan. Segala komisen dan caj yang akan dikecualikan.
- Negara/wilayah terjejas seperti yang dinyatakan dalam bahagian seterusnya akan dianggap sebagai "
**force majeure**" dan bayaran pembatalan akan dikecualikan.
- Larangan perjalanan yang diumumkan oleh kerajaan di kawasan tertentu akan dianggap sebagai "
**force majeure**" dan bayaran tempahan akan dikecualikan.
- Jika pelanggan menghubungi penginapan anda untuk membuat pembatalan, sila nasihatkan mereka untuk memulakan permintaan pembatalan dengan pergi keTempahan Saya pada laman sesawang Agoda atau menghubungi ejen Khidmat Pelanggan Agoda menerusi nombor telefon yang dinyatakan dalam baucar tempahan.

--- FILE: 360045316413-what-is-occupancy-model-display-setting.md ---
# What is Occupancy Model Display Setting?

Source: https://agodapropertypartnerhelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360045316413-What-is-Occupancy-Model-Display-Setting

Updated: 2021-09-26T08:40:34Z

|


Please note that you have to be logged into YCS to make these changes, you can find how to do this here.

This article is available in; Thai, Japanese, Korean, Vietnamese, Mandarin, Cantonese & Simplified Mandarin

This is a new functionality that allows rates to be added based on the actual occupancy of the room, and will mean that existing rates will be adapted to a per person occupancy format in the new YCS calendar. This will be available for YCS desktop only for the time being.

You may be part of the test roll-out on April 6th If not, you will see this change when rolled out globally mid-April.


**Example**

**If you have a room with a maximum occupancy of 5 and rates are loaded as single = 1200 / double = 1300 / full = 1400, the new YCS calendar will display rates as follows:**

**1 person = 1200 / 2 people = 1300 / 3 people = 1400 / 4 people = 1400 / 5 people = 1400**


All rates, allotments and restrictions that were previously loaded into the calendar will not be wiped, and will remain in place.

If your Channel Manager doesn't support occupancy based pricing, rates can be sent from Channel Managers using existing Full Occupancy Models. The new YCS calendar will display the updates from Channel Managers per occupant.

Rates will be sold as they were updated in the calendar, even if your Channel Manager doesn’t support Occupancy Based Pricing. If the Channel Manager attempts to get the most updated rates and allotment from Agoda, they will be able to receive single / double / full rates. Full will be equal to the rate for maximum occupancy.


To access the new features of the YCS calendar

a) Login to YCS as normal

b) Navigate to the calendar page by selecting "View" from the Rate & Allotment menu.

c) Select a single date or range of dates and click on the advanced tab on the right hand side of the screen.

d) Within the advanced tab, scroll down to a rate plan and then select "Edit Price Based on Occupancy"

e) You have now accessed the new features of the new version of the YCS calendar. Continue with one of the sections below to update rates.


**Note about discount per occupancy**: "Discounting" for the new calendar works by using the full occupancy rate as the base price. The discount % from the maximum occupancy is increased by the base discount % for each descending occupancy.

**Example**

**If a room has a maximum occupancy of 3 and the full occupancy rate is 100 USD and the discount is 10% then the per occupancy rate would be as follows.**

**3 People: 100 USD**

**2 People: 100 - 10 = 90**

**1 Person: 100 - (10 x 2 ) = 80**


a) Set a rate for the full occupancy of the room

b) Set the discount per unit of unused occupancy

c) The rate per occupant will automatically be filled in.

d) click save rates

**Note about discount per occupancy**: "Discounting" for the new calendar works by using the full occupancy rate as the base price. The discount amount from the maximum occupancy is increased by the base discount amount for each descending occupancy.


**Example**

**If a room has a maximum occupancy of 3 and the full occupancy rate is 100 USD and the discount amount is 10 USD then the per occupancy rate would be as follows.**

**3 People: 100 USD**

**2 People: 100 - (100 -10) = 90**

**1 Person: 100 - ((100 - (10 x 2 )) = 80**


a) Set the rate for full occupancy of the room

b) set the discount per unit of unused occupancy

c) The rate per occupant will be automatically filled in

d) click save rates

**Note about setting a specific discount per person**: A discount for an occupancy level can't be left blank, and can't be negative. It is however possible to set a specific occupancy level at a discount percentage / amount higher or lower than the preceding or following occupancy level.

**Example 1: **

Base Price: 10,000

|
Occupancy
|
Discount %
|
Rate
|
|---|---|---|
| 4 | 10 | 9,000 |
| 3 | 15 | 8,500 |
| 2 | 20 | 8,000 |
| 1 | 25 | 7,500 |

**Example 2: **

Base Price: 10,000

|
Occupancy
|
Discount %
|
Rate
|
|---|---|---|
| 4 | 10 | 9,000 |
| 3 | 5 | 9,500 |
| 2 | 15 | 8,500 |
| 1 | 20 | 8,000 |

**Example 3: **

Base Price: 10,000

|
Occupancy
|
Discount Amount
|
Rate
|
|---|---|---|
| 4 | 1,000 | 9,000 |
| 3 | 2,000 | 8,000 |
| 2 | 3,000 | 7,000 |
| 1 | 4,000 | 6,000 |

**Example 4:**

Base Price: 10,000

|
Occupancy
|
Discount Amount
|
Rate
|
|---|---|---|
| 4 | 1,000 | 9,000 |
| 3 | 5,000 | 5,000 |
| 2 | 3,000 | 7,000 |
| 1 | 1,000 | 9,000 |



a) Set a rate for full occupancy of the room

b) fill in the rate per occupant.

c) click save rates.


It is possible to load rates for partial occupancy. The calendar will display rate data for the occupancy level it has received.


We are working on moving more features including this one to our YCS App, please stay tuned!


--- FILE: 360045352314-what-is-the-account-verification-form.md ---
# What is the Account Verification Form?

Source: https://agodapropertypartnerhelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360045352314-What-is-the-Account-Verification-Form

Updated: 2021-09-26T12:28:01Z

|
**Terms**
|
**Explanation**
|
|
Individual
|
- A ‘natural person’ (in legal meaning, i.e. one who has their own legal personality) who is an individual human being and is not formed and administered as per corporate law.
|
|
Property legal name
|
- The official name of the property as used on official registration documents
|
|
Ultimate Beneficial Owner
|
-
The ultimate beneficial owner is the individual who ultimately owns the property. If an individual person owns the property legally, then they are the ultimate beneficial owner. If a company owns the property, the person who owns
*this company* is the *ultimate* beneficial owner. The ultimate beneficial owner is the person who is *ultimately* at the top of the ownership structure.
|
|
Alternate Name
|
- Some companies operate under a name that differs from the registered, legal name of the business. This could be a trade name, trading name or business name.
|
|
Property Management Company
|
- A management company manages the daily operations of a hotel, either for an incentive fee, a base fee or a cut of the gross revenue. They typically function as third-party operators, providing day-to-day management services as well as support in accounting, sales and marketing, food and beverage, human resources, auditing, revenue management, etc.
|
|
Ultimate Beneficial Owner Name
|
-
The ultimate beneficial owner. If a company owns the property/management company, we need the full legal name of the company.
-
If the property/management company is owned by an individual, then we will need the full legal name of that individual.
|
|
Government control
|
- Where an entity is wholly owned or controlled (i.e. through more than 50% ownership) by a government body or government official.
|
